  const SCHEDULER_BUCKETS = [
    { id: "ready-now", title: "Ready Now", copy: "Clears the schedule and makes the issue due immediately." },
    { id: "tomorrow", title: "Tomorrow", copy: "Schedules the issue for tomorrow at 09:00 local time." },
    { id: "next-week", title: "Next Week", copy: "Schedules the issue for next Monday at 09:00 local time." },
    { id: "later", title: "Later", copy: "Schedules the issue two weeks out at 09:00 local time." },
  ];

  const TASK_STATUS_GROUPS = [
    { id: "failed", title: "Failed", copy: "Runs and tasks that need intervention or a rerun." },
    { id: "blocked", title: "Blocked", copy: "Work waiting on approvals, review, or external state." },
    { id: "active", title: "Active", copy: "Currently running or actively being processed." },
    { id: "queued", title: "Queued", copy: "Ready to run once capacity is available." },
    { id: "completed", title: "Completed", copy: "Finished, dismissed, or otherwise out of the active lane." },
  ];

  function defaultTaskComposerState() {
    return {
      repoSlug: "",
      kind: "investigation",
      title: "",
      description: "",
      scheduleAt: "",
      runMode: "now",
      templateID: "template:custom",
      idempotencyKey: nextTaskComposerIdempotencyKey(),
      creating: false,
      savingTemplate: false,
      investigationQuery: "",
      codingWorkType: "feature",
      codingPriority: "3",
      scoutRole: "improvement-scout",
      scoutDestination: "review",
      scoutSessionLimit: "4",
      scoutFocus: "",
    };
  }

  function nextTaskComposerIdempotencyKey() {
    const secureUUID = window.crypto && typeof window.crypto.randomUUID === "function"
      ? window.crypto.randomUUID()
      : "";
    if (secureUUID) return `task-${secureUUID}`;
    return `task-${Date.now().toString(36)}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10)}`;
  }

  function resetTaskComposerIdempotencyKey() {
    state.taskComposer.idempotencyKey = nextTaskComposerIdempotencyKey();
  }

  function ensurePlannedFormIdempotencyKey(repoSlug) {
    const normalizedRepo = defaultString(repoSlug, "");
    if (state.plannedFormRepoSlug !== normalizedRepo || !String(state.plannedFormIdempotencyKey || "").trim()) {
      state.plannedFormRepoSlug = normalizedRepo;
      state.plannedFormIdempotencyKey = nextTaskComposerIdempotencyKey();
    }
    return state.plannedFormIdempotencyKey;
  }

  function resetPlannedFormIdempotencyKey(repoSlug) {
    state.plannedFormRepoSlug = defaultString(repoSlug, "");
    state.plannedFormIdempotencyKey = nextTaskComposerIdempotencyKey();
  }

  function defaultFeedbackState() {
    return {

  }

  function defaultApprovalsState() {

      selectedID: "",

      error: "",
    };
  }

  function defaultUsageState() {
    return {
      report: null,
      loading: false,
      loaded: false,
      error: "",
      lastLoadedAt: 0,
      filters: {
        since: "30d",
        root: "all",
        activity: "",
        phase: "",
        model: "",
      },
    };
  }

  function defaultViewFilter() {
    return {
      query: "",
      repo: "",
      attention: "all",
      status: "all",
      kind: "all",
    };
  }

  function defaultScopedViewFilter(repoSlug) {
    return {
      ...defaultViewFilter(),
      repo: defaultString(repoSlug, ""),
    };
  }

  function defaultWorkspaceFilters() {
    return {
      issues: defaultViewFilter(),
      investigations: defaultViewFilter(),
      work: defaultViewFilter(),
      feedback: defaultViewFilter(),
      approvals: defaultViewFilter(),
    };
  }

  function defaultLiveVersions() {
    return {
      generatedAt: "",
      overview: "",
      usage: "",
    };
  }

  function clearUsageRefreshTimer() {
    if (!usageRefreshTimer) return;
    window.clearInterval(usageRefreshTimer);
    usageRefreshTimer = 0;
  }

  function shouldAutoRefreshUsage() {
    return state.currentView === "usage" && document.visibilityState === "visible";
  }

  function usageRefreshAgeMs() {
    return state.usage.lastLoadedAt ? (Date.now() - state.usage.lastLoadedAt) : Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY;
  }

  function syncUsageAutoRefresh() {
    if (!shouldAutoRefreshUsage()) {
      clearUsageRefreshTimer();
      return;
    }
    if (usageRefreshTimer) return;
    usageRefreshTimer = window.setInterval(() => {
      if (!shouldAutoRefreshUsage()) {
        clearUsageRefreshTimer();
        return;
      }
      if (state.usage.loading) return;
      if (!state.usage.loaded || usageRefreshAgeMs() >= USAGE_AUTO_REFRESH_INTERVAL_MS) {
        loadUsage({ silent: true });
      }
    }, USAGE_AUTO_REFRESH_INTERVAL_MS);
  }

  function refreshUsageIfStale() {
    if (!shouldAutoRefreshUsage() || state.usage.loading) {
      syncUsageAutoRefresh();
      return;
    }
    if (!state.usage.loaded || usageRefreshAgeMs() >= USAGE_AUTO_REFRESH_INTERVAL_MS) {
      loadUsage({ silent: true });
      return;
    }
    syncUsageAutoRefresh();
  }

  function api(path, options = {}) {
    const headers = {
      ...(options.body ? { "Content-Type": "application/json" } : {}),
      ...(options.headers || {}),
    };
    return fetch(apiBase + path, {
      ...options,
      headers,
    }).then(async (response) => {
      const contentType = response.headers.get("Content-Type") || "";
      const isJSON = contentType.includes("application/json");
      const payload = isJSON ? await response.json().catch(() => null) : null;
      const text = payload === null ? await response.text() : "";
      if (!response.ok) {
        const error = new Error((payload && payload.message) || text || response.statusText);
        if (payload && payload.code) error.code = payload.code;
        if (payload && payload.repair_command) error.repairCommand = payload.repair_command;
        throw error;
      }
      if (payload !== null) return payload;
      return response.json();
    });
  }

  function toast(type, title, message) {
    Teryx.toast({ type, title, message, duration: 3500 });
    announce(`${title}. ${message}`);
  }

  function announce(message) {
    const text = String(message || "").trim();
    if (!text) return;
    const region = document.getElementById("app-live-region");
    state.liveRegionMessage = text;
    if (!region) return;
    region.textContent = "";
    window.setTimeout(() => {
      region.textContent = text;
    }, 10);
  }

  function escapeHTML(value) {
    return String(value ?? "")
      .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
      .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
      .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
      .replace(/"/g, "&quot;")
      .replace(/'/g, "&#39;");
  }

  function defaultString(value, fallback) {
    const trimmed = String(value ?? "").trim();
    return trimmed || fallback;
  }

  function timestamp(value) {
    const parsed = Date.parse(value || "");
    return Number.isNaN(parsed) ? 0 : parsed;
  }

  function formatDateTime(value) {
    if (!value) return "No update yet";
    const date = new Date(value);
    if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) return value;
    return date.toLocaleString();
  }

  function formatTokenCompact(value) {
    const numeric = Number(value || 0);
    if (!Number.isFinite(numeric)) return "0";
    if (numeric >= 1000000) return `${(numeric / 1000000).toFixed(1)}M`;
    if (numeric >= 1000) return `${(numeric / 1000).toFixed(1)}k`;
    return String(Math.round(numeric));
  }

  function formatPercent(value) {
    const numeric = Number(value || 0);
    if (!Number.isFinite(numeric)) return "0%";
    return `${numeric.toFixed(1)}%`;
  }

  function readDraftFieldValue(field) {
    if (!field || field.type === "file") return null;
    if (field instanceof HTMLSelectElement && field.multiple) {
      return {
        kind: "select-multiple",
        values: Array.from(field.selectedOptions || []).map((option) => option.value),
      };
    }
    if (field.type === "checkbox" || field.type === "radio") {
      return {
        kind: field.type,
        checked: Boolean(field.checked),
      };
    }
    return {
      kind: "value",
      value: String(field.value ?? ""),
    };
  }

  function writeDraftFieldValue(field, draft) {
    if (!field || !draft || field.type === "file") return;
    if (draft.kind === "select-multiple" && field instanceof HTMLSelectElement && field.multiple) {
      const selected = new Set(draft.values || []);
      Array.from(field.options || []).forEach((option) => {
        option.selected = selected.has(option.value);
      });
      return;
    }
    if (draft.kind === "checkbox" || draft.kind === "radio") {
      field.checked = Boolean(draft.checked);
      return;
    }
    field.value = String(draft.value ?? "");
  }

  function draftScopeForField(field) {
    const scopeHost = field && typeof field.closest === "function"
      ? field.closest("[data-draft-scope]")
      : null;
    return scopeHost ? defaultString(scopeHost.getAttribute("data-draft-scope"), "") : "";
  }

  function focusScopeForField(field) {
    const scopeHost = field && typeof field.closest === "function"
      ? field.closest("[data-draft-scope], [data-focus-scope]")
      : null;
    if (!scopeHost) return "";
    return defaultString(
      scopeHost.getAttribute("data-draft-scope"),
      defaultString(scopeHost.getAttribute("data-focus-scope"), ""),
    );
  }

  function draftFieldKey(field) {
    if (!field) return "";
    if (field.name) return `name:${field.name}`;
    if (field.id) return `id:${field.id}`;
    return "";
  }

  function captureDraftField(field) {
    const scope = draftScopeForField(field);
    const key = draftFieldKey(field);
    if (!scope || !key) return;
    const draft = readDraftFieldValue(field);
    if (!draft) return;
    state.formDrafts[scope] = {
      ...(state.formDrafts[scope] || {}),
      [key]: draft,
    };
  }

  function restoreDraftScope(scope, root = document) {
    const draftFields = scope ? state.formDrafts[scope] : null;
    if (!draftFields || !root) return;
    root.querySelectorAll("input, textarea, select").forEach((field) => {
      if (draftScopeForField(field) !== scope) return;
      const draft = draftFields[draftFieldKey(field)];
      if (!draft) return;
      writeDraftFieldValue(field, draft);
    });
  }

  function clearDraftScope(scope) {
    if (!scope) return;
    delete state.formDrafts[scope];
  }

  function clearDraftField(field) {
    const scope = draftScopeForField(field);
    const key = draftFieldKey(field);
    if (!scope || !key || !state.formDrafts[scope]) return;
    delete state.formDrafts[scope][key];
    if (Object.keys(state.formDrafts[scope]).length === 0) {
      delete state.formDrafts[scope];
    }
  }

  function clearDraftScopesByPrefix(prefix) {
    if (!prefix) return;
    Object.keys(state.formDrafts || {}).forEach((scope) => {
      if (scope.startsWith(prefix)) {
        delete state.formDrafts[scope];
      }
    });
  }

  function usageFiltersDraftScope() {
    return "usage:filters";
  }

  function issuesDetailDraftScope(issue) {
    return issue ? `issues:detail:${issue.id}` : "";
  }

  function repoControlsIssueDraftScope() {
    return state.selectedRepo && state.selectedIssue
      ? `repo:${state.selectedRepo}:tracked-issue:${state.selectedIssue}`
      : "";
  }

  function repoControlsPlannedDraftScope() {
    return state.selectedRepo ? `repo:${state.selectedRepo}:planned-create` : "";
  }

  function repoSchedulerSearchDraftScope(repo) {
    return repo ? `repo:${repo.repo_slug}:scheduler-search` : "";
  }

  function repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(repo, item) {
    return repo && item ? `repo:${repo.repo_slug}:planned-detail:${item.id}` : "";
  }

  function taskFindingDraftScope(repo, finding) {
    return repo && finding ? `investigations:finding:${repo.repo_slug}:${finding.id}` : "";
  }

  function findingImportCandidateDraftScope(repo, session, candidate) {
    return repo && session && candidate
      ? `investigations:import:${repo.repo_slug}:${session.id}:${candidate.candidate_id}`
      : "";
  }

  function repoConfigFocusScope(repo) {
    return repo ? `repo:${repo.repo_slug}:config` : "";
  }

  function repoOnboardingFocusScope() {
    return "workspace:repo-onboarding";
  }

  function workItemFixInstructionFocusScope(item) {
    return item ? `work-item:${item.id}:fix-instruction` : "";
  }

  function clearIssuesDetailDrafts() {
    clearDraftScopesByPrefix("issues:detail:");
  }

  function clearRepoControlsDrafts(repoSlug = state.selectedRepo) {
    const repo = String(repoSlug || "").trim();
    if (!repo) return;
    clearDraftScope(`repo:${repo}:planned-create`);
    clearDraftScope(`repo:${repo}:scheduler-search`);
    clearDraftScopesByPrefix(`repo:${repo}:tracked-issue:`);
    clearDraftScopesByPrefix(`repo:${repo}:planned-detail:`);
  }

  function clearInvestigationsDrafts(repoSlug = "") {
    const repo = String(repoSlug || "").trim();
    if (!repo) {
      clearDraftScopesByPrefix("investigations:finding:");
      clearDraftScopesByPrefix("investigations:import:");
      return;
    }
    clearDraftScopesByPrefix(`investigations:finding:${repo}:`);
    clearDraftScopesByPrefix(`investigations:import:${repo}:`);
  }

  function currentRouteDraftContext() {
    return {
      view: defaultString(state.currentView, "home"),
      repoSlug: defaultString(state.selectedRepo, ""),
      repoTab: defaultString(state.repoTab, "overview"),
    };
  }

  function clearDraftsForRouteContext(context) {
    if (!context) return;
    switch (defaultString(context.view, "home")) {
      case "usage":
        clearDraftScope(usageFiltersDraftScope());
        break;
      case "issues":
        clearIssuesDetailDrafts();
        break;
      case "investigations":
        clearInvestigationsDrafts(context.repoSlug);
        break;
      case "repo":
        if (defaultString(context.repoTab, "overview") === "controls") {
          clearRepoControlsDrafts(context.repoSlug);
        }
        break;
      default:
        break;
    }
  }

  function clearDraftsForRouteTransition(nextContext = {}) {
    const current = currentRouteDraftContext();
    const next = {
      view: defaultString(nextContext.view, current.view),
      repoSlug: defaultString(nextContext.repoSlug, current.repoSlug),
      repoTab: defaultString(nextContext.repoTab, current.repoTab),
    };
    if (current.view !== next.view || current.repoSlug !== next.repoSlug || (current.view === "repo" && current.repoTab !== next.repoTab)) {
      clearDraftsForRouteContext(current);
    }
  }

  function isDraftFocusableField(field) {
    return field instanceof HTMLInputElement
      || field instanceof HTMLTextAreaElement
      || field instanceof HTMLSelectElement;
  }

  function draftFieldSupportsSelection(field) {
    if (field instanceof HTMLTextAreaElement) return true;
    if (!(field instanceof HTMLInputElement)) return false;
    return ["text", "search", "url", "tel", "password"].includes(String(field.type || "").toLowerCase());
  }

  function focusSnapshotRootContains(root, field) {
    if (!field) return false;
    if (!root || root === document) return true;
    return typeof root.contains === "function" ? root.contains(field) : true;
  }

  function readDraftFieldSelection(field) {
    if (!draftFieldSupportsSelection(field)) return null;
    try {
      if (typeof field.selectionStart !== "number" || typeof field.selectionEnd !== "number") {
        return null;
      }
      return {
        start: field.selectionStart,
        end: field.selectionEnd,
        direction: typeof field.selectionDirection === "string" ? field.selectionDirection : "none",
      };
    } catch (_error) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  function captureDraftFocusSnapshot(root = document) {
    if (!root) return null;
    const field = document.activeElement;
    if (!isDraftFocusableField(field)) return null;
    if (!focusSnapshotRootContains(root, field)) return null;
    const scope = focusScopeForField(field);
    const key = draftFieldKey(field);
    if (!scope || !key) return null;
    return {
      scope,
      key,
      selection: readDraftFieldSelection(field),
    };
  }

  function findDraftField(scope, key, root = document) {
    if (!scope || !key || !root) return null;
    const fields = root.querySelectorAll("input, textarea, select");
    for (const field of fields) {
      if (!isDraftFocusableField(field)) continue;
      if (focusScopeForField(field) !== scope) continue;
      if (draftFieldKey(field) !== key) continue;
      return field;
    }
    return null;
  }

  function focusDraftField(field) {
    if (!field || typeof field.focus !== "function") return;
    try {
      field.focus({ preventScroll: true });
    } catch (_error) {
      field.focus();
    }
  }

  function restoreDraftFocusSnapshot(snapshot, root = document) {
    if (!snapshot || !root) return false;
    const field = findDraftField(snapshot.scope, snapshot.key, root);
    if (!field || field.disabled) return false;
    focusDraftField(field);
    if (snapshot.selection && draftFieldSupportsSelection(field) && typeof field.setSelectionRange === "function") {
      try {
        field.setSelectionRange(snapshot.selection.start, snapshot.selection.end, snapshot.selection.direction || "none");
      } catch (_error) {
        // Ignore unsupported selection restoration for non-text controls.
      }
    }
    return document.activeElement === field;
  }

  function renderAppPreservingDraftFocus() {
    renderWithPreservedDraftFocus(() => {
      renderApp();
    });
  }

  function renderWithPreservedDraftFocus(renderFn, root = document) {
    if (typeof renderFn !== "function") return;
    const snapshot = captureDraftFocusSnapshot(root);
    renderFn();
    restoreDraftFocusSnapshot(snapshot, root);
  }

  function usageSummary() {
    return state.usage && state.usage.report ? state.usage.report.summary || null : null;
  }

  function usageNavCount() {
    const summary = usageSummary();
    if (!summary) return "0";
    return formatTokenCompact(summary.totals && summary.totals.sessions || 0);
  }

  function toDateTimeLocal(value) {
    if (!value) return "";
    const date = new Date(value);
    if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) return "";
    const year = date.getFullYear();
    const month = String(date.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0");
    const day = String(date.getDate()).padStart(2, "0");
    const hours = String(date.getHours()).padStart(2, "0");
    const minutes = String(date.getMinutes()).padStart(2, "0");
    return `${year}-${month}-${day}T${hours}:${minutes}`;
  }

  function fromDateTimeLocal(value) {
    if (!value) return "";
    const date = new Date(value);
    if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) return "";
    return date.toISOString();
  }

  function sameLocalDate(left, right) {
    return left.getFullYear() === right.getFullYear()
      && left.getMonth() === right.getMonth()
      && left.getDate() === right.getDate();
  }

  function schedulerTomorrowAnchor() {
    const date = new Date();
    date.setDate(date.getDate() + 1);
    date.setHours(9, 0, 0, 0);
    return date;
  }

  function schedulerNextMondayAnchor() {
    const date = new Date();
    const day = date.getDay();
    let delta = (8 - day) % 7;
    if (delta === 0) delta = 7;
    date.setDate(date.getDate() + delta);
    date.setHours(9, 0, 0, 0);
    return date;
  }

  function schedulerLaterAnchor() {
    const date = new Date();
    date.setDate(date.getDate() + 14);
    date.setHours(9, 0, 0, 0);
    return date;
  }

  function schedulerScheduleAtForBucket(bucketID) {
    switch (bucketID) {
      case "tomorrow":
        return schedulerTomorrowAnchor().toISOString();
      case "next-week":
        return schedulerNextMondayAnchor().toISOString();
      case "later":
        return schedulerLaterAnchor().toISOString();
      default:
        return "";
    }
  }

  function schedulerBucketForItem(item) {
    const value = defaultString(item && item.schedule_at, "");
    if (!value) return "ready-now";
    const scheduled = new Date(value);
    if (Number.isNaN(scheduled.getTime())) return "ready-now";
    const now = new Date();
    if (scheduled.getTime() <= now.getTime()) return "ready-now";
    const tomorrow = schedulerTomorrowAnchor();
    if (sameLocalDate(scheduled, tomorrow)) return "tomorrow";
    const nextWeek = schedulerNextMondayAnchor();
    if (scheduled.getTime() <= nextWeek.getTime()) return "next-week";
    return "later";
  }

  function schedulerBucketSortKey(bucketID) {
    const index = SCHEDULER_BUCKETS.findIndex((bucket) => bucket.id === bucketID);
    return index === -1 ? SCHEDULER_BUCKETS.length : index;
  }

  function schedulerIssueNumber(targetURL) {
    const match = String(targetURL || "").match(/\/issues\/(\d+)(?:\/)?$/);
    return match ? Number.parseInt(match[1], 10) : 0;
  }

  function schedulerPriorityTone(priority) {
    const value = Number(priority);
    if (value <= 1) return "high";
    if (value <= 3) return "medium";
    return "low";
  }

  function schedulerCardLabels(item) {
    const labels = [`P${Number(item.priority ?? 5)}`];
    if (item.state === "failed") labels.push("Failed");
    return labels;
  }

  function schedulerCardDescription(item) {
    const issueNumber = schedulerIssueNumber(item.target_url);
    const scheduleText = defaultString(item.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(item.schedule_at) : "", "Ready now");
    return issueNumber > 0
      ? `#${issueNumber} · ${scheduleText}`
      : scheduleText;
  }

  function issuePickModeToAutomationMode(value) {
    switch (String(value || "").trim()) {
      case "label":
        return "labeled";
      case "auto":
        return "auto";
      default:
        return "manual";
    }
  }

  function automationModeToIssuePickMode(value) {
    switch (String(value || "").trim()) {
      case "labeled":
        return "label";
      case "auto":
        return "auto";
      default:
        return "manual";
    }
  }

  function repoModeToPublishTarget(value) {
    switch (String(value || "").trim()) {
      case "fork":
        return "fork";
      case "repo":
        return "repo";
      case "disabled":
        return "";
      default:
        return "local-branch";
    }
  }

  function publishTargetToRepoMode(value) {
    switch (String(value || "").trim()) {
      case "fork":
        return "fork";
      case "repo":
        return "repo";
      default:
        return "local";
    }
  }

  function repoOnboardingPayload() {
    const onboarding = state.repoOnboarding || defaultRepoOnboardingState();
    const draft = onboarding.draft || defaultRepoOnboardingState().draft;
    return {
      repo_slug: String(draft.repo_slug || "").trim(),
      repo_mode: defaultString(draft.repo_mode, "local"),
      issue_pick_mode: defaultString(draft.issue_pick_mode, "manual"),
      pr_forward_mode: defaultString(draft.pr_forward_mode, "approve"),
      fork_issues_mode: issuePickModeToAutomationMode(draft.issue_pick_mode),
      implement_mode: issuePickModeToAutomationMode(draft.issue_pick_mode),
      publish_target: repoModeToPublishTarget(draft.repo_mode),
    };
  }

  function sortedRepos() {
    const source = (state.overview && Array.isArray(state.overview.repos) && state.overview.repos.length)
      ? state.overview.repos
      : (state.repoList.items || []);
    return [ ...source ].sort((left, right) => {
      return left.repo_slug.localeCompare(right.repo_slug);
    });
  }

  function repoSummaryBySlug(repoSlug) {
    const normalized = String(repoSlug || "").trim();
    if (!normalized) return null;
    const overviewSummary = state.overview && Array.isArray(state.overview.repos)
      ? state.overview.repos.find((repo) => repo.repo_slug === normalized) || null
      : null;
    const repoListSummary = (state.repoList.items || []).find((repo) => repo.repo_slug === normalized) || null;
    if (!overviewSummary) return repoListSummary;
    if (!repoListSummary) return overviewSummary;
    return {
      ...overviewSummary,
      ...repoListSummary,
      state: repoListSummary.state || overviewSummary.state || null,
    };
  }

  function canRenderWithoutOverview(view) {
    return view === "usage"
      || view === "issues"
      || view === "investigations"
      || view === "feedback"
      || view === "approvals";
  }

  function selectedRepoSummary() {
    if (!state.selectedRepo) return null;
    return repoSummaryBySlug(state.selectedRepo);
  }

  function ensureTaskComposerRepo() {
    const repos = sortedRepos();
    if (!repos.length) {
      state.taskComposer.repoSlug = "";
      return null;
    }
    const preferred = defaultString(state.taskComposer.repoSlug, defaultString(state.selectedRepo, repos[0].repo_slug));
    const match = repos.find((repo) => repo.repo_slug === preferred) || repos[0];
    state.taskComposer.repoSlug = match.repo_slug;
    return match;
  }

  function selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary() {
    const repo = ensureTaskComposerRepo();
    if (!repo) return null;
    return repoSummaryBySlug(repo.repo_slug) || repo;
  }

  function selectedTaskTemplate() {
    const templates = state.investigations.templates || [];
    if (!templates.length) return null;
    return templates.find((item) => item.id === state.taskComposer.templateID) || templates[0] || null;
  }

  function taskComposerKindFromTemplate(template) {
    const hint = defaultString(template && template.launch_kind_hint, "");
    if (hint === "investigation") return "investigation";
    if (hint === "manual_scout") return "manual_scout";
    if (hint === "local_work") return "coding";
    return "";
  }

  function taskTemplateScoutPromptPreview(template) {
    if (!template || defaultString(template.launch_kind_hint, "") !== "manual_scout") return "";
    return String(template.scout_prompt_preview || "").trim();
  }

  function taskComposerCanSavePreset(template) {
    return !template || defaultString(template.id, "template:custom") === "template:custom";
  }

  function taskTemplateHelpText(template) {
    if (!template) return "";
    return defaultString(taskTemplateScoutPromptPreview(template), String(template.description || "").trim());
  }

  function applyTaskComposerTemplate(template, options = {}) {
    if (!template) return;
    state.taskComposer.templateID = defaultString(template.id, "template:custom");
    const hintedKind = taskComposerKindFromTemplate(template);
    if (hintedKind) {
      state.taskComposer.kind = hintedKind;
    }
    if (template && template.scout_role_hint) {
      reconcileTaskComposerScoutRole(selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary(), {
        role: String(template.scout_role_hint || ""),
        resetSessionLimit: true,
      });
    } else if (state.taskComposer.kind === "manual_scout") {
      reconcileTaskComposerScoutRole(selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary());
    }
    const workTypeHint = defaultString(template && template.work_type_hint, "");
    if (workTypeHint) {
      state.taskComposer.codingWorkType = workTypeHint;
    }
    const priorityHint = Number.parseInt(String(template && template.default_priority), 10);
    if (Number.isFinite(priorityHint) && priorityHint >= 0 && priorityHint <= 5) {
      state.taskComposer.codingPriority = String(priorityHint);
    }
    const templateDescription = String(template && template.description || "").trim();
    if (!templateDescription) return;
    if (state.taskComposer.kind === "investigation") {
      if (!String(state.taskComposer.investigationQuery || "").trim() || options.overwriteText) {
        state.taskComposer.investigationQuery = templateDescription;
      }
      return;
    }
    if (!String(state.taskComposer.description || "").trim() || options.overwriteText) {
      state.taskComposer.description = templateDescription;
    }
  }

  function taskComposerPresetDescription() {
    const description = String(state.taskComposer.description || "").trim();
    if (description) return description;
    if (state.taskComposer.kind === "investigation") {
      return String(state.taskComposer.investigationQuery || "").trim();
    }
    if (state.taskComposer.kind === "manual_scout") {
      const focus = String(state.taskComposer.scoutFocus || "").trim();
      if (focus) return `Scout focus: ${focus}`;
    }
    return String(state.taskComposer.title || "").trim();
  }

  function taskComposerPresetBaseTemplateID() {
    if (state.taskComposer.kind === "manual_scout") {
      const repo = selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary();
      const selection = reconcileTaskComposerScoutRole(repo);
      if (selection.role) {
        return `template:scout:${selection.role}`;
      }
    }
    if (state.taskComposer.kind === "investigation") {
      return "template:investigation";
    }
    if (state.taskComposer.kind === "coding") {
      return "template:implementation";
    }
    const template = selectedTaskTemplate();
    return defaultString(template && template.id, "template:custom");
  }

  function selectedTaskScopeRepoSummary() {
    if (!state.selectedRepo) return null;
    return selectedRepoSummary();
  }

  function selectedIssueRecord() {
    const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
    if (!repo || !repo.state) return null;
    return (repo.state.issues || {})[state.selectedIssue] || null;
  }

  function ensureRepoScheduler(repo) {
    const repoSlug = repo ? repo.repo_slug : "";
    if (state.repoScheduler.repoSlug !== repoSlug) {
      state.repoScheduler = {
        ...defaultRepoSchedulerState(),
        repoSlug,
      };
    }
    reconcileRepoScheduler(repo);
  }

  function reconcileRepoScheduler(repo) {
    if (!repo) {
      state.repoScheduler = defaultRepoSchedulerState();
      return;
    }
    const scheduled = trackedIssuePlannedItems(repo);
    if (!state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID || !scheduled.some((item) => item.id === state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID)) {
      state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID = scheduled[0] ? scheduled[0].id : "";
    }
    state.repoScheduler.results = (state.repoScheduler.results || []).map((item) => {
      const planned = trackedIssuePlannedItemForURL(repo, item.target_url);
      return {
        ...item,
        scheduled: Boolean(planned),
        planned_item_id: planned ? planned.id : "",
        planned_state: planned ? planned.state : "",
        schedule_at: planned ? planned.schedule_at : "",
      };
    });
  }

  function trackedIssuePlannedItems(repo) {
    if (!repo || !repo.state) return [];
    return Object.values(repo.state.planned_items || {})
      .filter((item) => item.launch_kind === "tracked_issue" && (item.state === "queued" || item.state === "failed"))
      .sort((left, right) => {
        const leftBucket = schedulerBucketSortKey(schedulerBucketForItem(left));
        const rightBucket = schedulerBucketSortKey(schedulerBucketForItem(right));
        if (leftBucket !== rightBucket) return leftBucket - rightBucket;
        if ((left.priority ?? 5) !== (right.priority ?? 5)) return (left.priority ?? 5) - (right.priority ?? 5);
        return timestamp(right.updated_at) - timestamp(left.updated_at);
      });
  }

  function trackedIssuePlannedItemForURL(repo, targetURL) {
    if (!repo || !repo.state || !targetURL) return null;
    return trackedIssuePlannedItems(repo).find((item) => defaultString(item.target_url, "") === defaultString(targetURL, "")) || null;
  }

  function selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(repo) {
    const items = trackedIssuePlannedItems(repo);
    if (!items.length) return null;
    if (!state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID) return items[0];
    return items.find((item) => item.id === state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID) || items[0];
  }

  function selectedIssueQueueItem() {
    if (!state.issueQueue.selectedID) return state.issueQueue.items[0] || null;
    return state.issueQueue.items.find((item) => item.id === state.issueQueue.selectedID) || state.issueQueue.items[0] || null;
  }

  function selectedInvestigationSummary() {
    if (!state.investigations.selectedRunID) return state.investigations.items[0] || null;
    return state.investigations.items.find((item) => item.run_id === state.investigations.selectedRunID) || state.investigations.items[0] || null;
  }

  function investigationSelectionFromHash() {
    const params = new URLSearchParams(String(window.location.hash || "").replace(/^#/, ""));
    const requestedView = defaultString(params.get("view"), state.currentView);
    const nextRepo = params.has("repo") ? defaultString(params.get("repo"), state.selectedRepo) : state.selectedRepo;
    const requestedRepoTab = defaultString(params.get("tab"), requestedView === "repo" ? state.repoTab : "overview");
    const route = normalizeRouteContext(requestedView, nextRepo, requestedRepoTab);
    if (route.view !== "investigations") return "";
    return defaultString(params.get("task"), defaultString(params.get("investigation"), ""));
  }

  function selectedApprovalItem(items) {
    const source = items || state.approvals.items || [];
    if (!state.approvals.selectedID) return source[0] || null;
    return source.find((item) => item.id === state.approvals.selectedID) || source[0] || null;
  }

  function selectedIssueQueueItemFrom(items) {
    const source = items || state.issueQueue.items || [];
    if (!state.issueQueue.selectedID) return source[0] || null;
    return source.find((item) => item.id === state.issueQueue.selectedID) || source[0] || null;
  }

  function activeFilterCount(filter) {
    if (!filter) return 0;
    return (String(filter.query || "").trim() ? 1 : 0) +
      (filter.kind && filter.kind !== "all" ? 1 : 0) +
      (filter.attention && filter.attention !== "all" ? 1 : 0);
  }

  function resetFilter(view) {
    state.filters[view] = defaultScopedViewFilter(state.selectedRepo);
  }

  function normalizeRouteContext(view, repoSlug, repoTab) {
    const normalized = {
      view: defaultString(view, "home"),
      repoSlug: defaultString(repoSlug, ""),
      repoTab: defaultString(repoTab, "overview"),
    };
    if (normalized.view === "repo" && normalized.repoTab === "findings") {
      normalized.view = "investigations";
      normalized.repoTab = "overview";
    }
    if (normalized.view !== "repo") {
      normalized.repoTab = "overview";
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  function buildRouteHash() {
    const route = normalizeRouteContext(state.currentView, state.selectedRepo, state.repoTab);
    const params = new URLSearchParams();
    params.set("view", route.view);
    if (route.repoSlug) {
      params.set("repo", route.repoSlug);
    }
    if (route.view === "repo" && route.repoSlug) {
      params.set("tab", route.repoTab);
    } else if (route.view === "feedback") {
      params.set("tab", state.feedbackTab);
    }
    if (route.view === "issues" && state.issueQueue.selectedID) {
      params.set("issue", state.issueQueue.selectedID);
    }
    if (route.view === "investigations" && state.investigations.selectedRunID) {
      params.set("task", state.investigations.selectedRunID);
    }
    if (route.view === "approvals" && state.approvals.selectedID) {
      params.set("approval", state.approvals.selectedID);
    }
    return params.toString();
  }

  function syncHashState() {
    if (!state.hashReady) return;
    const nextHash = buildRouteHash();
    const normalizedCurrent = String(window.location.hash || "").replace(/^#/, "");
    if (normalizedCurrent === nextHash) return;
    const targetURL = nextHash ? `#${nextHash}` : window.location.pathname;
    window.history.replaceState(null, "", targetURL);
  }

  function applyHashState() {
    const params = new URLSearchParams(String(window.location.hash || "").replace(/^#/, ""));
    const hasTaskSelection = params.has("task") || params.has("investigation");
    const requestedView = defaultString(params.get("view"), state.currentView);
    const nextRepo = params.has("repo") ? defaultString(params.get("repo"), "") : "";
    const requestedRepoTab = defaultString(params.get("tab"), requestedView === "repo" ? state.repoTab : "overview");
    const route = normalizeRouteContext(requestedView, nextRepo, requestedRepoTab);
    clearDraftsForRouteTransition({
      view: route.view,
      repoSlug: route.repoSlug,
      repoTab: route.repoTab,
    });
    state.currentView = route.view;
    state.selectedRepo = route.repoSlug;
    state.repoTab = route.repoTab;
    syncWorkspaceRepoFilters(state.selectedRepo);
    if (state.selectedRepo) {
      state.taskComposer.repoSlug = state.selectedRepo;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "feedback") {
      state.feedbackTab = defaultString(params.get("tab"), state.feedbackTab);
    }
    state.issueQueue.selectedID = defaultString(params.get("issue"), state.issueQueue.selectedID);
    if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
      state.investigations.selectedRunID = hasTaskSelection
        ? defaultString(params.get("task"), defaultString(params.get("investigation"), ""))
        : "";
    }
    state.approvals.selectedID = defaultString(params.get("approval"), state.approvals.selectedID);
  }

  function filterState(view) {
    if (!state.filters[view]) {
      state.filters[view] = defaultViewFilter();
    }
    return state.filters[view];
  }

  function updateFilter(view, field, value) {
    filterState(view)[field] = value;
  }

  function matchesAttentionFilter(item, value) {
    if (!value || value === "all") return true;
    return defaultString(item && item.attention_state, "") === value;
  }

  function matchesRepoFilter(item, value) {
    if (!value) return true;
    return defaultString(item && item.repo_slug, "") === value;
  }

  function matchesKindFilter(item, value) {
    if (!value || value === "all") return true;
    return defaultString(item && item.kind, defaultString(item && item.backend, "")) === value;
  }

  function matchesTaskStatusFilter(item, value) {
    if (!value || value === "all") return true;
    return defaultString(item && item.attention_state, "") === value;
  }

  function matchesQuery(item, fields, query) {
    const normalized = String(query || "").trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!normalized) return true;
    return fields.some((field) => defaultString(item && item[field], "").toLowerCase().includes(normalized));
  }

  function buildWorkspaceScopeNotice() {
    const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
    if (!repo) return "";
    return `
      <div class="scope-banner">
        <div class="scope-banner-copy">
          <span class="scope-banner-label">Repo Scope</span>
          <strong>${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}</strong>
          <p>This page is filtered to the repo selected in the header picker.</p>
        </div>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-clear-workspace-scope="true">All repos</button>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function buildFilterToolbar(view, options = {}) {
    const filter = filterState(view);
    const activeCount = activeFilterCount(filter);
    const attentionOptions = [
      { value: "all", label: "All states" },
      { value: "failed", label: "Failed" },
      { value: "blocked", label: "Blocked" },
      { value: "active", label: "Active" },
      { value: "queued", label: "Queued" },
      { value: "completed", label: "Completed" },
    ].map((option) => {
      const selected = filter.attention === option.value ? "selected" : "";
      return `<option value="${escapeHTML(option.value)}" ${selected}>${escapeHTML(option.label)}</option>`;
    }).join("");
    const kindSelect = Array.isArray(options.kindOptions) && options.kindOptions.length
      ? `
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Kind</span>
          <select data-view-filter="${escapeHTML(view)}" data-view-filter-name="kind">
            ${options.kindOptions.map((option) => {
              const selected = filter.kind === option.value ? "selected" : "";
              return `<option value="${escapeHTML(option.value)}" ${selected}>${escapeHTML(option.label)}</option>`;
            }).join("")}
          </select>
        </label>
      `
      : "";
    return `
      ${buildWorkspaceScopeNotice()}
      <details class="filter-disclosure" ${activeCount ? "open" : ""}>
        <summary class="filter-summary">
          <span class="filter-summary-copy">
            <span>Filters</span>
            <span class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(String(activeCount))} active</span>
          </span>
        </summary>
        <div class="filter-panel">
          <div class="config-actions">
            <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm filter-reset" type="button" data-view-filter-reset="${escapeHTML(view)}">Clear</button>
          </div>
          <div class="config-grid workspace-filters">
            <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
              <span>Search</span>
              <input type="text" value="${escapeHTML(filter.query)}" placeholder="${escapeHTML(defaultString(options.placeholder, "Search"))}" data-view-filter="${escapeHTML(view)}" data-view-filter-name="query" />
            </label>
            <label class="selector config-selector">
              <span>Status</span>
              <select data-view-filter="${escapeHTML(view)}" data-view-filter-name="attention">${attentionOptions}</select>
            </label>
            ${kindSelect}
          </div>
        </div>
      </details>
    `;
  }

  const SCOUT_ROLE_ORDER = ["improvement", "enhancement", "backend-performance", "ui"];
  const SCOUT_ROLE_META = {
    improvement: { label: "Improvement Scout", defaultSchedule: "when_resolved", defaultSessionLimit: 0 },
    enhancement: { label: "Enhancement Scout", defaultSchedule: "when_resolved", defaultSessionLimit: 0 },
    "backend-performance": { label: "Backend Performance Scout", defaultSchedule: "when_resolved", defaultSessionLimit: 4 },
    ui: { label: "UI Scout", defaultSchedule: "when_resolved", defaultSessionLimit: 4 },
  };

  function normalizeScoutRoleKey(roleKey) {
    return String(roleKey || "").replace("-scout", "");
  }

  function serverScoutCatalog(repo) {
    if (repo && Array.isArray(repo.scout_catalog) && repo.scout_catalog.length) return repo.scout_catalog;
    if (state.overview && Array.isArray(state.overview.scout_catalog) && state.overview.scout_catalog.length) return state.overview.scout_catalog;
    return [];
  }

  function repoScoutCatalog(repo) {
    const catalog = serverScoutCatalog(repo);
    if (catalog.length) return catalog;
    return SCOUT_ROLE_ORDER.map((roleKey) => ({
      role: `${roleKey}-scout`,
      config_key: roleKey,
      display_label: SCOUT_ROLE_META[roleKey].label,
      default_schedule: SCOUT_ROLE_META[roleKey].defaultSchedule,
      default_session_limit: SCOUT_ROLE_META[roleKey].defaultSessionLimit,
      supports_session_limit: SCOUT_ROLE_META[roleKey].defaultSessionLimit > 0,
    }));
  }

  function repoScoutMeta(roleKey, repo) {
    const key = normalizeScoutRoleKey(roleKey);
    const match = repoScoutCatalog(repo).find((entry) => entry.config_key === key);
    if (match) {
      return {
        label: defaultString(match.display_label, SCOUT_ROLE_META[key] ? SCOUT_ROLE_META[key].label : key),
        defaultSchedule: defaultString(match.default_schedule, SCOUT_ROLE_META[key] ? SCOUT_ROLE_META[key].defaultSchedule : "when_resolved"),
        defaultSessionLimit: Number(match.default_session_limit) > 0 ? Number(match.default_session_limit) : 0,
        supportsSessionLimit: Boolean(match.supports_session_limit),
      };
    }
    return SCOUT_ROLE_META[key] || SCOUT_ROLE_META.improvement;
  }

  function defaultTaskComposerScoutSessionLimit(meta) {
    const parsed = Number.parseInt(String(meta && meta.defaultSessionLimit || "0"), 10);
    if (!Number.isFinite(parsed) || parsed < 1) return "1";
    return String(Math.min(parsed, 6));
  }

  function normalizeTaskComposerScoutSessionLimit(meta, currentValue, options = {}) {
    if (!meta || !meta.supportsSessionLimit) {
      return "";
    }
    const parsed = Number.parseInt(String(currentValue || "").trim(), 10);
    if (!options.reset && parsed >= 1 && parsed <= 6) {
      return String(parsed);
    }
    return defaultTaskComposerScoutSessionLimit(meta);
  }

  function reconcileTaskComposerScoutRole(repo, options = {}) {
    const catalog = repoScoutCatalog(repo);
    if (!catalog.length) {
      state.taskComposer.scoutRole = "";
      state.taskComposer.scoutSessionLimit = "";
      return {
        role: "",
        meta: repoScoutMeta("", repo),
      };
    }
    const requestedRole = defaultString(options.role, state.taskComposer.scoutRole);
    const nextRole = catalog.some((entry) => entry.role === requestedRole)
      ? requestedRole
      : defaultString(catalog[0] && catalog[0].role, "");
    const roleChanged = nextRole !== String(state.taskComposer.scoutRole || "").trim();
    state.taskComposer.scoutRole = nextRole;
    const meta = repoScoutMeta(nextRole, repo);
    state.taskComposer.scoutSessionLimit = normalizeTaskComposerScoutSessionLimit(meta, state.taskComposer.scoutSessionLimit, {
      reset: Boolean(options.resetSessionLimit) || roleChanged,
    });
    return { role: nextRole, meta };
  }

  function repoScoutConfigsByRole(repo) {
    if (repo && repo.scouts_by_role) return repo.scouts_by_role;
    const fallback = {};
    const scouts = repo && repo.scouts;
    repoScoutCatalog(repo).forEach((entry) => {
      fallback[entry.config_key] = scouts && scouts[entry.config_key] ? scouts[entry.config_key] : {};
    });
    return fallback;
  }

  function repoScoutSnapshot(role, config) {
    const labels = Array.isArray(config && config.labels) ? config.labels.filter((label) => String(label || "").trim()) : [];
    const meta = repoScoutMeta(role);
    const defaultSessionLimit = meta.defaultSessionLimit;
    return {
      enabled: Boolean(config && config.enabled),
      policy_path: defaultString(config && config.policy_path, ""),
      mode: defaultString(config && config.mode, "auto"),
      schedule: defaultString(config && config.schedule, defaultString(meta.defaultSchedule, "when_resolved")),
      issue_destination: defaultString(config && config.issue_destination, "local"),
      fork_repo: defaultString(config && config.fork_repo, ""),
      labels,
      session_limit: Number(config && config.session_limit) > 0 ? Number(config.session_limit) : defaultSessionLimit,
    };
  }

  function repoConfigSnapshot(repo) {
    if (!repo) return null;
    const issuePickMode = defaultString(repo.issue_pick_mode, "manual");
    const repoMode = defaultString(repo.repo_mode, "local");
    const scouts = {};
    repoScoutCatalog(repo).forEach((entry) => {
      scouts[entry.config_key] = repoScoutSnapshot(entry.config_key, repoScoutConfigsByRole(repo)[entry.config_key]);
    });
    const fixedScouts = {};
    Object.keys(scouts).forEach((roleKey) => {
      fixedScouts[roleKey] = scouts[roleKey];
    });
    return {
      repo_mode: repoMode,
      issue_pick_mode: issuePickMode,
      pr_forward_mode: defaultString(repo.pr_forward_mode, "approve"),
      fork_issues_mode: defaultString(repo.fork_issues_mode, issuePickModeToAutomationMode(issuePickMode)),
      implement_mode: defaultString(repo.implement_mode, issuePickModeToAutomationMode(issuePickMode)),
      publish_target: repoMode === "disabled"
        ? ""
        : defaultString(repo.publish_target, repoModeToPublishTarget(repoMode)),
      scout_catalog: repoScoutCatalog(repo),
      scouts_by_role: scouts,
      scouts: fixedScouts,
    };
  }

  function repoConfigSnapshotKey(config) {
    return JSON.stringify(config || {});
  }

  function cloneConfigSnapshot(config) {
    return config ? JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(config)) : null;
  }

  function configDraftFieldRawValue(draft) {
    if (!draft || typeof draft !== "object") return null;
    if (draft.kind === "checkbox" || draft.kind === "radio") {
      return draft.checked ? "true" : "false";
    }
    if (draft.kind === "select-multiple") {
      return Array.isArray(draft.values) ? draft.values.join(", ") : "";
    }
    if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(draft, "value")) {
      return String(draft.value ?? "");
    }
    return null;
  }

  function activeConfigFieldsForRepo(repo) {
    const fields = new Set([
      "repo_mode",
      "issue_pick_mode",
      "pr_forward_mode",
      "fork_issues_mode",
      "implement_mode",
      "publish_target",
    ]);
    repoScoutCatalog(repo).forEach((entry) => {
      const roleKey = entry.config_key;
      fields.add(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.enabled`);
      fields.add(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.mode`);
      fields.add(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.schedule`);
      fields.add(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.issue_destination`);
      fields.add(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.fork_repo`);
      fields.add(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.labels`);
      if (repoScoutMeta(roleKey, repo).supportsSessionLimit) {
        fields.add(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.session_limit`);
      }
    });
    return fields;
  }

  function applyConfigDraftValue(target, repo, field, rawValue, options = {}) {
    const value = parseConfigFieldValue(field, rawValue);
    setNestedConfigValue(target, field, value);
    const trackOverrides = options.trackOverrides !== false;
    switch (field) {
      case "repo_mode":
        if (trackOverrides) {
          state.configEditor.overridePublish = false;
        }
        if (value === "disabled") {
          target.publish_target = "";
        } else {
          target.publish_target = repoModeToPublishTarget(value);
        }
        break;
      case "publish_target":
        if (trackOverrides) {
          state.configEditor.overridePublish = true;
        }
        target.repo_mode = publishTargetToRepoMode(value);
        break;
      case "issue_pick_mode": {
        const automationMode = issuePickModeToAutomationMode(value);
        if (trackOverrides) {
          state.configEditor.overrideForkIssues = false;
          state.configEditor.overrideImplement = false;
        }
        target.fork_issues_mode = automationMode;
        target.implement_mode = automationMode;
        break;
      }
      case "fork_issues_mode":
        if (trackOverrides) {
          state.configEditor.overrideForkIssues = true;
        }
        target.issue_pick_mode = effectiveIssuePickFromAdvanced(target);
        break;
      case "implement_mode":
        if (trackOverrides) {
          state.configEditor.overrideImplement = true;
        }
        target.issue_pick_mode = effectiveIssuePickFromAdvanced(target);
        break;
      default:
        if (field.startsWith("scouts_by_role.")) {
          const parts = field.split(".");
          const roleKey = parts[1];
          const scout = (target.scouts_by_role && target.scouts_by_role[roleKey]) || null;
          if (scout) {
            scout.policy_path = configScoutPolicyPath(repo, roleKey);
            if (parts[2] === "issue_destination" && value !== "fork") {
              scout.fork_repo = "";
            }
          }
        }
        break;
    }
  }

  function prettyJSON(value) {
    return JSON.stringify(value || {}, null, 2);
  }

  function resetConfigEditorForRepo(repo) {
    const snapshot = repoConfigSnapshot(repo);
    state.configEditor = {
      ...defaultConfigEditor(),
      repoSlug: repo ? repo.repo_slug : "",
      server: snapshot,
      serverKey: repoConfigSnapshotKey(snapshot),
      draft: cloneConfigSnapshot(snapshot),
    };
  }

  function ensureConfigEditor(repo) {
    if (!repo) {
      state.configEditor = defaultConfigEditor();
      return;
    }
    const snapshot = repoConfigSnapshot(repo);
    const serverKey = repoConfigSnapshotKey(snapshot);
    if (state.configEditor.repoSlug !== repo.repo_slug) {
      resetConfigEditorForRepo(repo);
      return;
    }
    state.configEditor.server = snapshot;
    if (!state.configEditor.dirty) {
      state.configEditor.serverKey = serverKey;
      state.configEditor.draft = cloneConfigSnapshot(snapshot);
      state.configEditor.remoteChanged = false;
      return;
    }
    if (serverKey !== state.configEditor.serverKey) {
      state.configEditor.remoteChanged = true;
    }
  }

  function syncConfigEditorTransientDrafts(repo) {
    if (!repo || state.configEditor.repoSlug !== repo.repo_slug || !state.configEditor.draft) {
      return;
    }
    const draftScope = repoConfigFocusScope(repo);
    const draftFields = state.formDrafts[draftScope];
    const activeFields = activeConfigFieldsForRepo(repo);
    let removedAny = false;
    if (draftFields) {
      Object.keys(draftFields).forEach((key) => {
        if (!key.startsWith("config:")) return;
        const field = key.slice("config:".length);
        if (activeFields.has(field)) return;
        delete draftFields[key];
        removedAny = true;
      });
      if (Object.keys(draftFields).length === 0) {
        delete state.formDrafts[draftScope];
      }
    }
    const currentDraftFields = state.formDrafts[draftScope];
    if (!currentDraftFields && !removedAny) {
      return;
    }
    const next = cloneConfigSnapshot(state.configEditor.server || repoConfigSnapshot(repo));
    Object.entries(currentDraftFields || {}).forEach(([key, draft]) => {
      if (!key.startsWith("config:")) return;
      const field = key.slice("config:".length);
      if (!activeFields.has(field)) return;
      const rawValue = configDraftFieldRawValue(draft);
      if (rawValue === null) return;
      applyConfigDraftValue(next, repo, field, rawValue, { trackOverrides: false });
    });
    const removeNormalizedField = (field) => {
      if (!currentDraftFields) return;
      const key = `config:${field}`;
      if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(currentDraftFields, key)) return;
      delete currentDraftFields[key];
      removedAny = true;
    };
    if (!state.configEditor.overridePublish) {
      removeNormalizedField("publish_target");
    } else {
      removeNormalizedField("repo_mode");
    }
    if (!state.configEditor.overrideForkIssues && !state.configEditor.overrideImplement) {
      removeNormalizedField("fork_issues_mode");
      removeNormalizedField("implement_mode");
    } else {
      removeNormalizedField("issue_pick_mode");
    }
    Object.entries(next.scouts_by_role || {}).forEach(([roleKey, scout]) => {
      if (defaultString(scout && scout.issue_destination, "local") !== "fork") {
        removeNormalizedField(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.fork_repo`);
      }
    });
    if (currentDraftFields && Object.keys(currentDraftFields).length === 0) {
      delete state.formDrafts[draftScope];
    }
    const finalDraft = cloneConfigSnapshot(state.configEditor.server || repoConfigSnapshot(repo));
    Object.entries(state.formDrafts[draftScope] || {}).forEach(([key, draft]) => {
      if (!key.startsWith("config:")) return;
      const field = key.slice("config:".length);
      if (!activeFields.has(field)) return;
      const rawValue = configDraftFieldRawValue(draft);
      if (rawValue === null) return;
      applyConfigDraftValue(finalDraft, repo, field, rawValue, { trackOverrides: false });
    });
    syncCompatibilityScouts(finalDraft);
    if (!removedAny && configDraftEquals(finalDraft, state.configEditor.draft)) {
      return;
    }
    state.configEditor.draft = finalDraft;
    state.configEditor.dirty = !configDraftEquals(finalDraft, state.configEditor.server);
    if (!state.configEditor.dirty) {
      state.configEditor.remoteChanged = false;
      state.configEditor.overridePublish = false;
      state.configEditor.overrideForkIssues = false;
      state.configEditor.overrideImplement = false;
    }
  }

  function effectiveIssuePickFromAdvanced(draft) {
    if (!draft) return "manual";
    return automationModeToIssuePickMode(draft.implement_mode) ||
      automationModeToIssuePickMode(draft.fork_issues_mode) ||
      "manual";
  }

  function configDraftEquals(left, right) {
    return repoConfigSnapshotKey(left) === repoConfigSnapshotKey(right);
  }

  function resetScoutItemsState(repo) {
    state.scoutItems = {
      ...defaultScoutItemsState(),
      repoSlug: repo ? repo.repo_slug : "",
      lastRepoScoutRefreshKey: repoScoutItemsRefreshKey(repo),
    };
  }

  function ensureScoutItemsState(repo) {
    if (!repo) {
      state.scoutItems = defaultScoutItemsState();
      return;
    }
    if (state.scoutItems.repoSlug !== repo.repo_slug) {
      resetScoutItemsState(repo);
      return;
    }
    if (state.scoutItems.loaded && repoScoutItemsRefreshKey(repo) !== state.scoutItems.lastRepoScoutRefreshKey && !state.scoutItems.loading) {
      loadScoutItems(repo.repo_slug, { silent: true });
    }
  }

  function selectedScoutItem() {
    if (!state.scoutItems.selectedItemID) return state.scoutItems.items[0] || null;
    return state.scoutItems.items.find((item) => item.id === state.scoutItems.selectedItemID) || state.scoutItems.items[0] || null;
  }

  function selectedScoutItemIDs() {
    return (state.scoutItems.selectedItemIDs || []).filter((itemID) => state.scoutItems.items.some((item) => item.id === itemID));
  }

  function allScoutItemIDs() {
    return state.scoutItems.items
      .map((item) => String(item.id || ""))
      .filter(Boolean);
  }

  function setSelectedScoutItemIDs(itemIDs) {
    const allowed = new Set(state.scoutItems.items.map((item) => item.id));
    const seen = new Set();
    state.scoutItems.selectedItemIDs = (itemIDs || []).filter((itemID) => {
      const id = String(itemID || "");
      if (!allowed.has(id) || seen.has(id)) return false;
      seen.add(id);
      return true;
    });
  }

  function selectAllScoutItems() {
    const itemIDs = allScoutItemIDs();
    setSelectedScoutItemIDs(itemIDs);
    if (itemIDs.length && !itemIDs.includes(state.scoutItems.selectedItemID)) {
      state.scoutItems.selectedItemID = itemIDs[0];
    }
  }

  function clearScoutItemSelection() {
    setSelectedScoutItemIDs([]);
  }

  function repoScoutItemsRefreshKey(repo) {
    if (!repo) return "";
    return JSON.stringify({
      scout_jobs: (repo.state && repo.state.scout_jobs) || {},
      planned_items: (repo.state && repo.state.planned_items) || {},
      scout_job_counts: repo.scout_job_counts || {},
      planned_item_counts: repo.planned_item_counts || {},
    });
  }

  function toggleScoutItemSelection(itemID, checked) {
    const current = new Set(selectedScoutItemIDs());
    if (checked) {
      current.add(itemID);
    } else {
      current.delete(itemID);
    }
    setSelectedScoutItemIDs(Array.from(current));
  }

  function scoutActionableSelection(action) {
    return selectedScoutItemIDs().filter((itemID) => {
      const item = state.scoutItems.items.find((entry) => entry.id === itemID);
      return item && (item.available_actions || []).includes(action);
    });
  }

  function applyScoutItemsPayload(repoSlug, payload) {
    if (payload.repo) {
      mergeRepoSummary(payload.repo, { rerender: false, resetScouts: false });
    }
    state.scoutItems.repoSlug = repoSlug;
    state.scoutItems.items = payload.items || [];
    state.scoutItems.loading = false;
    state.scoutItems.loaded = true;
    state.scoutItems.error = "";
    state.scoutItems.lastRepoScoutRefreshKey = payload.repo ? repoScoutItemsRefreshKey(payload.repo) : state.scoutItems.lastRepoScoutRefreshKey;
    if (!state.scoutItems.selectedItemID || !state.scoutItems.items.some((item) => item.id === state.scoutItems.selectedItemID)) {
      state.scoutItems.selectedItemID = state.scoutItems.items[0] ? state.scoutItems.items[0].id : "";
    }
    setSelectedScoutItemIDs(state.scoutItems.selectedItemIDs || []);
  }

  function loadScoutItems(repoSlug, options = {}) {
    if (!repoSlug) return Promise.resolve();
    state.scoutItems.repoSlug = repoSlug;
    state.scoutItems.loading = true;
    if (!options.silent) {
      state.scoutItems.error = "";
    }
    if (!options.silent || !state.scoutItems.items.length) {
      rerenderScoutSurface();
    }
    return api(`/api/v1/repos/${repoSlug}/scout-items`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.scoutItems.repoSlug !== repoSlug) return;
      applyScoutItemsPayload(repoSlug, payload);
      rerenderScoutSurface();
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.scoutItems.repoSlug !== repoSlug) return;
      state.scoutItems.loading = false;
      state.scoutItems.error = error.message;
      rerenderScoutSurface();
      if (!options.silent) {
        toast("danger", "Scout items failed", error.message);
      }
    });
  }

  function mutateScoutItem(repoSlug, itemID, action) {
    return api(`/api/v1/repos/${repoSlug}/scout-items/${encodeURIComponent(itemID)}/${action}`, {
      method: "POST",
    }).then((payload) => {
      applyScoutItemsPayload(repoSlug, payload);
      rerenderScoutSurface();
      return payload;
    }).catch((error) => {
      toast("danger", "Scout item action failed", error.message);
      throw error;
    });
  }

  function mutateScoutItemsBulk(repoSlug, itemIDs, action) {
    const selectedBefore = new Set(selectedScoutItemIDs());
    return api(`/api/v1/repos/${repoSlug}/scout-items/batch`, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        action,
        item_ids: itemIDs,
      }),
    }).then((payload) => {
      applyScoutItemsPayload(repoSlug, payload);
      const successfulIDs = new Set((payload.results || [])
        .filter((result) => result.status === "ok")
        .map((result) => result.item_id));
      const nextSelection = Array.from(selectedBefore).filter((itemID) => !successfulIDs.has(itemID));
      setSelectedScoutItemIDs(nextSelection);
      rerenderScoutSurface();
      return payload;
    }).catch((error) => {
      toast("danger", "Scout bulk action failed", error.message);
      throw error;
    });
  }

  function taskFindingsRefreshKey(repo) {
    if (!repo) return "";
    return JSON.stringify({
      findings: (repo.state && repo.state.findings) || {},
      planned_items: (repo.state && repo.state.planned_items) || {},
    });
  }

  function resetTaskFindingsState(repo) {
    state.taskFindings = {
      ...defaultTaskFindingsState(),
      repoSlug: repo ? repo.repo_slug : "",
      lastRepoFindingRefreshKey: taskFindingsRefreshKey(repo),
    };
  }

  function ensureTaskFindingsState(repo) {
    if (!repo) {
      state.taskFindings = defaultTaskFindingsState();
      return;
    }
    if (state.taskFindings.repoSlug !== repo.repo_slug) {
      resetTaskFindingsState(repo);
      return;
    }
    if (state.taskFindings.loaded && taskFindingsRefreshKey(repo) !== state.taskFindings.lastRepoFindingRefreshKey && !state.taskFindings.loading) {
      loadTaskFindings(repo.repo_slug, { silent: true });
    }
  }

  function selectedTaskFinding() {
    if (!state.taskFindings.selectedFindingID) return state.taskFindings.items[0] || null;
    return state.taskFindings.items.find((item) => item.id === state.taskFindings.selectedFindingID) || state.taskFindings.items[0] || null;
  }

  function applyTaskFindingsPayload(repoSlug, payload) {
    if (payload.repo) {
      mergeRepoSummary(payload.repo, { rerender: false, resetScouts: false });
    }
    state.taskFindings.repoSlug = repoSlug;
    state.taskFindings.items = payload.items || [];
    state.taskFindings.loading = false;
    state.taskFindings.loaded = true;
    state.taskFindings.error = "";
    state.taskFindings.lastRepoFindingRefreshKey = payload.repo ? taskFindingsRefreshKey(payload.repo) : state.taskFindings.lastRepoFindingRefreshKey;
    if (!state.taskFindings.selectedFindingID || !state.taskFindings.items.some((item) => item.id === state.taskFindings.selectedFindingID)) {
      state.taskFindings.selectedFindingID = state.taskFindings.items[0] ? state.taskFindings.items[0].id : "";
    }
  }

  function loadTaskFindings(repoSlug, options = {}) {
    if (!repoSlug) return Promise.resolve();
    state.taskFindings.repoSlug = repoSlug;
    state.taskFindings.loading = true;
    if (!options.silent) {
      state.taskFindings.error = "";
    }
    if (!options.silent || !state.taskFindings.items.length) {
      renderInvestigationsPage();
    }
    return api(`/api/v1/repos/${repoSlug}/findings`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.taskFindings.repoSlug !== repoSlug) return;
      applyTaskFindingsPayload(repoSlug, payload);
      renderInvestigationsPage();
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.taskFindings.repoSlug !== repoSlug) return;
      state.taskFindings.loading = false;
      state.taskFindings.error = error.message;
      renderInvestigationsPage();
      if (!options.silent) {
        toast("danger", "Findings load failed", error.message);
      }
    });
  }

  function saveTaskFinding(repoSlug, findingID, payload) {
    state.taskFindings.saving = true;
    renderInvestigationsPage();
    return api(`/api/v1/repos/${repoSlug}/findings/${encodeURIComponent(findingID)}`, {
      method: "PATCH",
      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
    }).then((response) => {
      state.taskFindings.saving = false;
      if (response.state) {
        mergeRepoState(response.state);
      }
      return loadTaskFindings(repoSlug, { silent: true }).then(() => response);
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.taskFindings.saving = false;
      renderInvestigationsPage();
      toast("danger", "Finding save failed", error.message);
      throw error;
    });
  }

  function mutateTaskFinding(repoSlug, findingID, action) {
    return api(`/api/v1/repos/${repoSlug}/findings/${encodeURIComponent(findingID)}/${action}`, {
      method: "POST",
    }).then((payload) => {
      if (payload.state) {
        mergeRepoState(payload.state);
      }
      return loadTaskFindings(repoSlug, { silent: true }).then(() => payload);
    }).catch((error) => {
      toast("danger", "Finding action failed", error.message);
      throw error;
    });
  }

  function findingImportsRefreshKey(repo) {
    if (!repo) return "";
    return JSON.stringify({
      import_sessions: (repo.state && repo.state.import_sessions) || {},
      findings: (repo.state && repo.state.findings) || {},
    });
  }

  function resetFindingImportsState(repo) {
    state.findingImports = {
      ...defaultFindingImportsState(),
      repoSlug: repo ? repo.repo_slug : "",
      lastRepoImportRefreshKey: findingImportsRefreshKey(repo),
    };
  }

  function ensureFindingImportsState(repo) {
    if (!repo) {
      state.findingImports = defaultFindingImportsState();
      return;
    }
    if (state.findingImports.repoSlug !== repo.repo_slug) {
      resetFindingImportsState(repo);
      return;
    }
    if (state.findingImports.loaded && findingImportsRefreshKey(repo) !== state.findingImports.lastRepoImportRefreshKey && !state.findingImports.loading) {
      loadFindingImports(repo.repo_slug, { silent: true });
    }
  }

  function selectedFindingImportSession() {
    if (!state.findingImports.selectedSessionID) return state.findingImports.items[0] || null;
    return state.findingImports.items.find((item) => item.id === state.findingImports.selectedSessionID) || state.findingImports.items[0] || null;
  }

  function selectedFindingImportCandidate() {
    const session = selectedFindingImportSession();
    if (!session || !Array.isArray(session.candidates)) return null;
    if (!state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID) return session.candidates[0] || null;
    return session.candidates.find((candidate) => candidate.candidate_id === state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID) || session.candidates[0] || null;
  }

  function applyFindingImportsPayload(repoSlug, payload) {
    if (payload.repo) {
      mergeRepoSummary(payload.repo, { rerender: false, resetScouts: false });
    }
    state.findingImports.repoSlug = repoSlug;
    state.findingImports.items = payload.items || [];
    state.findingImports.loading = false;
    state.findingImports.loaded = true;
    state.findingImports.error = "";
    state.findingImports.lastRepoImportRefreshKey = payload.repo ? findingImportsRefreshKey(payload.repo) : state.findingImports.lastRepoImportRefreshKey;
    if (!state.findingImports.selectedSessionID || !state.findingImports.items.some((item) => item.id === state.findingImports.selectedSessionID)) {
      state.findingImports.selectedSessionID = state.findingImports.items[0] ? state.findingImports.items[0].id : "";
    }
    const session = selectedFindingImportSession();
    if (session && (!state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID || !session.candidates.some((candidate) => candidate.candidate_id === state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID))) {
      state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID = session.candidates[0] ? session.candidates[0].candidate_id : "";
    }
  }

  function loadFindingImports(repoSlug, options = {}) {
    if (!repoSlug) return Promise.resolve();
    state.findingImports.repoSlug = repoSlug;
    state.findingImports.loading = true;
    if (!options.silent) {
      state.findingImports.error = "";
    }
    if (!options.silent || !state.findingImports.items.length) {
      renderInvestigationsPage();
    }
    return api(`/api/v1/repos/${repoSlug}/finding-import-sessions`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.findingImports.repoSlug !== repoSlug) return;
      applyFindingImportsPayload(repoSlug, payload);
      renderInvestigationsPage();
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.findingImports.repoSlug !== repoSlug) return;
      state.findingImports.loading = false;
      state.findingImports.error = error.message;
      renderInvestigationsPage();
      if (!options.silent) {
        toast("danger", "Import sessions failed", error.message);
      }
    });
  }

  function createFindingImportSession(repoSlug, filePath, markdown) {
    state.findingImports.importing = true;
    renderInvestigationsPage();
    return api(`/api/v1/repos/${repoSlug}/finding-import-sessions`, {
      method: "POST",
      body: JSON.stringify({ file_path: filePath, markdown }),
    }).then((payload) => {
      state.findingImports.importing = false;
      return loadFindingImports(repoSlug, { silent: true }).then(() => {
        if (payload.session && payload.session.id) {
          state.findingImports.selectedSessionID = payload.session.id;
          state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID = payload.session.candidates && payload.session.candidates[0] ? payload.session.candidates[0].candidate_id : "";
        }
        renderInvestigationsPage();
        return payload;
      });
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.findingImports.importing = false;
      renderInvestigationsPage();
      toast("danger", "Markdown import failed", error.message);
      throw error;
    });
  }

  function mutateFindingImportCandidate(repoSlug, sessionID, candidateID, method, actionOrPayload) {
    const options = method === "PATCH"
      ? { method, body: JSON.stringify(actionOrPayload) }
      : { method: "POST" };
    const suffix = method === "PATCH" ? "" : `/${actionOrPayload}`;
    return api(`/api/v1/repos/${repoSlug}/finding-import-sessions/${encodeURIComponent(sessionID)}/candidates/${encodeURIComponent(candidateID)}${suffix}`, options).then((payload) => {
      if (payload.state) {
        mergeRepoState(payload.state);
      }
      return loadFindingImports(repoSlug, { silent: true }).then(() => {
        state.findingImports.selectedSessionID = sessionID;
        state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID = candidateID;
        renderInvestigationsPage();
        return payload;
      });
    }).catch((error) => {
      toast("danger", "Candidate action failed", error.message);
      throw error;
    });
  }

  function rerenderScoutSurface() {
    if (state.currentView === "repo" && state.repoTab === "scouts") {
      renderRepoScoutsPage(selectedRepoSummary());
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
      renderInvestigationsPage();
    }
  }

  function loadIssueQueue(options = {}) {
    state.issueQueue.loading = true;
    if (!options.silent) {
      state.issueQueue.error = "";
    }
    if (state.currentView === "issues") {
      renderIssuesPage();
    }
    return api("/api/v1/issues").then((payload) => {
      state.issueQueue.items = payload.items || [];
      state.issueQueue.loading = false;
      state.issueQueue.loaded = true;
      state.issueQueue.error = "";
      if (!state.issueQueue.selectedID || !state.issueQueue.items.some((item) => item.id === state.issueQueue.selectedID)) {
        state.issueQueue.selectedID = state.issueQueue.items[0] ? state.issueQueue.items[0].id : "";
      }
      if (state.currentView === "issues") {
        renderIssuesPage();
      }
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.issueQueue.loading = false;
      state.issueQueue.error = error.message;
      if (state.currentView === "issues") {
        renderIssuesPage();
      }
      if (!options.silent) {
        toast("danger", "Issues failed", error.message);
      }
    });
  }

  function loadInvestigations(options = {}) {
    state.investigations.loading = true;
    if (!options.silent) {
      state.investigations.error = "";
    }
    if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
      renderInvestigationsPage();
    }
    return api("/api/v1/tasks").then((payload) => {
      state.investigations.items = payload.items || [];
      state.investigations.loading = false;
      state.investigations.loaded = true;
      state.investigations.error = "";
      if (!state.investigations.selectedRunID || !state.investigations.items.some((item) => item.id === state.investigations.selectedRunID)) {
        const explicitSelection = investigationSelectionFromHash();
        if (explicitSelection) {
          state.investigations.selectedRunID = explicitSelection;
        } else {
          state.investigations.selectedRunID = state.investigations.items[0] ? defaultString(state.investigations.items[0].id, "") : "";
        }
      }
      if (state.investigations.selectedRunID) {
        return loadInvestigationDetail(state.investigations.selectedRunID, { silent: true });
      }
      state.investigations.detail = null;
      state.investigations.detailLoading = false;
      if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
        renderInvestigationsPage();
      }
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.investigations.loading = false;
      state.investigations.error = error.message;
      if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
        renderInvestigationsPage();
      }
      if (!options.silent) {
        toast("danger", "Investigations failed", error.message);
      }
    });
  }

  function loadInvestigationDetail(runID, options = {}) {
    const taskID = defaultString(runID, state.investigations.selectedRunID);
    if (!taskID) {
      state.investigations.detail = null;
      if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
        renderInvestigationsPage();
      }
      return Promise.resolve();
    }
    const currentDetailID = defaultString(
      state.investigations.detail && state.investigations.detail.summary && state.investigations.detail.summary.id,
      defaultString(state.investigations.detail && state.investigations.detail.summary && state.investigations.detail.summary.run_id, "")
    );
    state.investigations.selectedRunID = taskID;
    if (currentDetailID !== taskID) {
      state.investigations.detail = null;
    }
    syncHashState();
    state.investigations.detailLoading = true;
    if (!options.silent) {
      state.investigations.error = "";
    }
    if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
      renderInvestigationsPage();
    }
    return api(`/api/v1/tasks/${encodeURIComponent(taskID)}`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.investigations.selectedRunID !== taskID) return;
      state.investigations.detail = payload;
      state.investigations.detailLoading = false;
      renderTaskDetailModal();
      if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
        renderInvestigationsPage();
      }
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.investigations.selectedRunID !== taskID) return;
      state.investigations.detail = null;
      state.investigations.detailLoading = false;
      state.investigations.error = error.message;
      renderTaskDetailModal();
      if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
        renderInvestigationsPage();
      }
      if (!options.silent) {
        toast("danger", "Task detail failed", error.message);
      }
    });
  }

  function loadTaskTemplates(options = {}) {
    const repo = selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary();
    const repoSlug = repo ? repo.repo_slug : "";
    state.investigations.templatesLoading = true;
    if (!options.silent) {
      state.investigations.templatesError = "";
    }
    if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
      renderInvestigationsPage();
    }
    const query = repoSlug ? `?repo_slug=${encodeURIComponent(repoSlug)}` : "";
    return api(`/api/v1/tasks/templates${query}`).then((payload) => {
      state.investigations.templates = payload.items || [];
      state.investigations.templatesLoading = false;
      state.investigations.templatesLoaded = true;
      state.investigations.templatesRepoSlug = repoSlug;
      state.investigations.templatesError = "";
      if (!selectedTaskTemplate()) {
        state.taskComposer.templateID = state.investigations.templates[0] ? state.investigations.templates[0].id : "template:custom";
      }
      if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
        renderInvestigationsPage();
      }
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.investigations.templatesLoading = false;
      state.investigations.templatesError = error.message;
      if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
        renderInvestigationsPage();
      }
      if (!options.silent) {
        toast("danger", "Task presets failed", error.message);
      }
    });
  }

  function saveTaskTemplateFromComposer() {
    const repo = selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary();
    const description = taskComposerPresetDescription();
    if (!repo || !description) {
      toast("warning", "Missing preset details", "Add task context before saving a preset.");
      return;
    }
    state.taskComposer.savingTemplate = true;
    renderInvestigationsPage();
    api("/api/v1/tasks/templates", {
      method: "POST",
      body: JSON.stringify({
        repo_slug: repo.repo_slug,
        description,
        base_template_id: taskComposerPresetBaseTemplateID(),
      }),
    }).then((payload) => {
      state.taskComposer.savingTemplate = false;
      if (payload.template && payload.template.id) {
        state.taskComposer.templateID = payload.template.id;
      }
      toast("success", "Preset saved", payload.template && payload.template.name || "Task preset");
      return loadTaskTemplates({ silent: true });
    }).then(() => {
      if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
        renderInvestigationsPage();
      }
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.taskComposer.savingTemplate = false;
      if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
        renderInvestigationsPage();
      }
      toast("danger", "Preset save failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function loadFeedback(options = {}) {
    state.feedback.loading = true;
    if (!options.silent) {
      state.feedback.error = "";
    }
    if (state.currentView === "feedback") {
      renderFeedbackPage();
    }
    return Promise.all([
      api("/api/v1/reviews"),
      api("/api/v1/replies"),
    ]).then(([reviewsPayload, repliesPayload]) => {
      state.feedback.reviews = reviewsPayload.items || [];
      state.feedback.replies = repliesPayload.items || [];
      state.feedback.loading = false;
      state.feedback.loaded = true;
      state.feedback.error = "";
      if (state.currentView === "feedback") {
        renderFeedbackPage();
      }
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.feedback.loading = false;
