      state.feedback.error = error.message;
      if (state.currentView === "feedback") {
        renderFeedbackPage();
      }
      if (!options.silent) {
        toast("danger", "Feedback failed", error.message);
      }
    });
  }

  function loadApprovals(options = {}) {
    state.approvals.loading = true;
    if (!options.silent) {
      state.approvals.error = "";
    }
    if (state.currentView === "approvals") {
      renderApprovalsPage();
    }
    return api("/api/v1/approvals").then((payload) => {
      state.approvals.items = payload.items || [];
      state.approvals.loading = false;
      state.approvals.loaded = true;
      state.approvals.error = "";
      if (!state.approvals.selectedID || !state.approvals.items.some((item) => item.id === state.approvals.selectedID)) {
        state.approvals.selectedID = state.approvals.items[0] ? state.approvals.items[0].id : "";
      }
      if (state.currentView === "approvals") {
        renderApprovalsPage();
      }
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.approvals.loading = false;
      state.approvals.error = error.message;
      if (state.currentView === "approvals") {
        renderApprovalsPage();
      }
      if (!options.silent) {
        toast("danger", "Approvals failed", error.message);
      }
    });
  }

  function usageQueryString() {
    const params = new URLSearchParams();
    const filters = state.usage.filters || {};
    if (filters.since && filters.since !== "all") params.set("since", filters.since);
    if (state.currentView === "usage" && state.selectedRepo) params.set("repo", state.selectedRepo);
    if (filters.root && filters.root !== "all") params.set("root", filters.root);
    if (filters.activity) params.set("activity", filters.activity);
    if (filters.phase) params.set("phase", filters.phase);
    if (filters.model) params.set("model", filters.model);
    return params.toString();
  }

  function fetchUsageReport() {
    const query = usageQueryString();
    const path = query ? `/api/v1/usage?${query}` : "/api/v1/usage";
    return api(path);
  }

  function fetchOverview() {
    return api("/api/v1/overview");
  }

  function fetchRepos() {
    return api("/api/v1/repos").then((payload) => payload.repos || []);
  }

  function applyOverviewPayload(payload) {
    state.overview = payload;
    state.overviewError = "";
    if (Array.isArray(payload && payload.repos)) {
      const existing = Array.isArray(state.repoList.items) ? state.repoList.items : [];
      state.repoList.items = payload.repos.map((repo) => {
        const match = existing.find((item) => item.repo_slug === repo.repo_slug);
        if (!match) return repo;
        return {
          ...repo,
          ...match,
          state: match.state || repo.state || null,
        };
      });
    }
    if (state.currentView === "repo" && !state.repoList.loaded && !state.repoList.error) {
      return;
    }
    renderAppPreservingDraftFocus();
  }

  function applyOverviewError(error, options = {}) {
    state.overviewError = error.message;
    if (state.currentView === "usage") {
      renderAppPreservingDraftFocus();
    } else if (!state.overview && error && error.code === "work_db_repair_required") {
      announce(error.message);
      document.getElementById("page-body").innerHTML = buildMaintenanceNotice(error.message, error.repairCommand);
    } else if (!state.overview) {
      document.getElementById("page-body").innerHTML = `
        <section class="surface empty-surface">
          <div class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(error.message)}</div>
        </section>
      `;
    }
    if (!options.silent) {
      toast("danger", "Overview failed", error.message);
    }
  }

  function loadOverview(options = {}) {
    return fetchOverview().then((payload) => {
      applyOverviewPayload(payload);
      return payload;
    }).catch((error) => {
      applyOverviewError(error, options);
      throw error;
    });
  }

  function applyRepoListPayload(repos) {
    const existing = new Map((state.repoList.items || []).map((item) => [item.repo_slug, item]));
    state.repoList.items = (Array.isArray(repos) ? repos : []).map((repo) => {
      const current = existing.get(repo.repo_slug);
      return {
        ...current,
        ...repo,
        state: repo.state || current && current.state || null,
      };
    });
    state.repoList.loading = false;
    state.repoList.loaded = true;
    state.repoList.error = "";
    if (state.overview) {
      renderApp();
    }
  }

  function applyRepoListError(error, options = {}) {
    state.repoList.loading = false;
    state.repoList.error = error.message;
    if (state.overview) {
      renderApp();
    }
    if (!options.silent) {
      toast("danger", "Repos failed", error.message);
    }
  }

  function loadRepos(options = {}) {
    state.repoList.loading = true;
    if (!options.silent) {
      state.repoList.error = "";
    }
    return fetchRepos().then((repos) => {
      applyRepoListPayload(repos);
      return repos;
    }).catch((error) => {
      applyRepoListError(error, options);
      throw error;
    });
  }

  function applySelectedRepoPayload(repo) {
    if (!repo || !repo.repo_slug) return;
    const items = Array.isArray(state.repoList.items) ? [ ...state.repoList.items ] : [];
    const index = items.findIndex((item) => item.repo_slug === repo.repo_slug);
    if (index === -1) {
      items.push(repo);
    } else {
      items[index] = {
        ...items[index],
        ...repo,
        state: repo.state || items[index].state || null,
      };
    }
    state.repoList.items = items;
    state.repoList.loading = false;
    state.repoList.loaded = true;
    state.repoList.error = "";
    if (state.overview && Array.isArray(state.overview.repos)) {
      const overviewIndex = state.overview.repos.findIndex((item) => item.repo_slug === repo.repo_slug);
      if (overviewIndex >= 0) {
        state.overview.repos[overviewIndex] = {
          ...state.overview.repos[overviewIndex],
          ...repo,
          state: repo.state || state.overview.repos[overviewIndex].state || null,
        };
      }
    }
    renderApp();
  }

  function loadSelectedRepoSummary(options = {}) {
    if (!state.selectedRepo) {
      return Promise.resolve(null);
    }
    return api(`/api/v1/repos/${state.selectedRepo}/start-state`).then((repo) => {
      applySelectedRepoPayload(repo);
      return repo;
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (!options.silent) {
        toast("danger", "Repo state failed", error.message);
      }
      throw error;
    });
  }

  function applyUsagePayload(payload) {
    state.usage.report = payload;
    state.usage.loading = false;
    state.usage.loaded = true;
    state.usage.error = "";
    state.usage.lastLoadedAt = Date.now();
    if (!state.overview && state.currentView === "usage") {
      renderApp();
      return;
    }
    renderSidebar();
    if (state.currentView === "usage") {
      renderUsagePage();
    }
  }

  function applyUsageError(error, options = {}) {
    state.usage.loading = false;
    state.usage.error = error.message;
    if (!state.overview && state.currentView === "usage") {
      renderApp();
    } else {
      renderSidebar();
      if (state.currentView === "usage") {
        renderUsagePage();
      }
    }
    if (!options.silent) {
      toast("danger", "Usage failed", error.message);
    }
  }

  function loadUsage(options = {}) {
    state.usage.loading = true;
    if (!options.silent) {
      state.usage.error = "";
    }
    if (state.currentView === "usage") {
      renderUsagePage();
    }
    return fetchUsageReport().then((payload) => {
      applyUsagePayload(payload);
    }).catch((error) => {
      applyUsageError(error, options);
    });
  }

  function ensureViewData(view) {
    if ((!state.overview || !Array.isArray(state.overview.repos) || !state.overview.repos.length) && !state.repoList.loaded && !state.repoList.loading) {
      loadRepos({ silent: true });
    }
    switch (view) {
      case "issues":
        if (!state.issueQueue.loaded && !state.issueQueue.loading) {
          loadIssueQueue({ silent: true });
        }
        break;
      case "investigations":
        if (!state.investigations.loaded && !state.investigations.loading) {
          loadInvestigations({ silent: true });
        }
        {
          const composerRepo = selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary();
          const composerRepoSlug = composerRepo ? composerRepo.repo_slug : "";
          if ((!state.investigations.templatesLoaded || state.investigations.templatesRepoSlug !== composerRepoSlug) && !state.investigations.templatesLoading) {
            loadTaskTemplates({ silent: true });
          }
        }
        {
          const repo = selectedTaskScopeRepoSummary();
          if (repo) {
            ensureTaskFindingsState(repo);
            ensureFindingImportsState(repo);
            if (!state.taskFindings.loaded && !state.taskFindings.loading) {
              loadTaskFindings(repo.repo_slug, { silent: true });
            }
            if (!state.findingImports.loaded && !state.findingImports.loading) {
              loadFindingImports(repo.repo_slug, { silent: true });
            }
          }
        }
        break;
      case "feedback":
        if (!state.feedback.loaded && !state.feedback.loading) {
          loadFeedback({ silent: true });
        }
        break;
      case "approvals":
        if (!state.approvals.loaded && !state.approvals.loading) {
          loadApprovals({ silent: true });
        }
        break;
      case "usage":
        {
          const liveUsageVersion = defaultString(state.liveVersions.usage, "");
          const currentUsageVersion = defaultString(state.usage.report && state.usage.report.version, "");
          const staleUsage = liveUsageVersion && liveUsageVersion !== currentUsageVersion;
          if ((!state.usage.loaded || staleUsage) && !state.usage.loading) {
            loadUsage({ silent: true });
          }
        }
        break;
      default:
        break;
    }
  }

  function refreshCurrentView(options = {}) {
    switch (state.currentView) {
      case "issues":
        return loadIssueQueue(options);
      case "investigations":
        return loadInvestigations(options);
      case "feedback":
        return loadFeedback(options);
      case "approvals":
        return loadApprovals(options);
      case "usage":
        return loadUsage(options);
      case "repo":
        return loadSelectedRepoSummary(options);
      default:
        return Promise.resolve();
    }
  }

  function currentRunSummary(runID) {
    if (!state.overview) return null;
    return (state.overview.work_runs || []).find((run) => run.run_id === runID) || null;
  }

  function currentWorkItemSummary(itemID) {
    if (!state.overview) return null;
    return (state.overview.work_items || []).find((item) => item.id === itemID) || null;
  }

  function sortRuns(runs) {
    return [ ...runs ].sort((left, right) => {
      const leftRank = attentionOrder[left.attention_state] ?? attentionOrder.active;
      const rightRank = attentionOrder[right.attention_state] ?? attentionOrder.active;
      if (leftRank !== rightRank) return leftRank - rightRank;
      const updatedDiff = timestamp(right.updated_at) - timestamp(left.updated_at);
      if (updatedDiff !== 0) return updatedDiff;
      return left.run_id.localeCompare(right.run_id);
    });
  }

  function pendingRuns() {
    if (!state.overview) return [];
    return sortRuns((state.overview.work_runs || []).filter((run) => run.pending));
  }

  function sortWorkItems(items) {
    return [ ...(items || []) ].sort((left, right) => {
      const leftRank = attentionOrder[left.attention_state] ?? attentionOrder.active;
      const rightRank = attentionOrder[right.attention_state] ?? attentionOrder.active;
      if (leftRank !== rightRank) return leftRank - rightRank;
      const updatedDiff = timestamp(right.updated_at) - timestamp(left.updated_at);
      if (updatedDiff !== 0) return updatedDiff;
      return left.id.localeCompare(right.id);
    });
  }

  function pendingWorkItems() {
    if (!state.overview) return [];
    return sortWorkItems((state.overview.work_items || []).filter((item) => item.pending));
  }

  function pendingRunsForRepo(repoSlug) {
    return pendingRuns().filter((run) => run.repo_slug === repoSlug);
  }

  function pendingWorkItemsForRepo(repoSlug) {
    return pendingWorkItems().filter((item) => item.repo_slug === repoSlug);
  }

  function repoScoutQueueCount(repo) {
    return (repo.scout_job_counts.queued || 0) +
      (repo.scout_job_counts.running || 0) +
      (repo.scout_job_counts.failed || 0);
  }

  function repoDismissedScoutCount(repo) {
    return repo.scout_job_counts.dismissed || 0;
  }

  function repoManualPlannedQueueCount(repo) {
    return (repo.planned_item_counts.queued || 0) +
      (repo.planned_item_counts.launching || 0);
  }

  function outstandingRepoCount(repo) {
    return (repo.issue_counts.queued || 0) +
      (repo.issue_counts.blocked || 0) +
      (repo.service_task_counts.queued || 0) +
      (repo.service_task_counts.running || 0) +
      repoScoutQueueCount(repo) +
      repoManualPlannedQueueCount(repo) +
      pendingRunsForRepo(repo.repo_slug).length +
      pendingWorkItemsForRepo(repo.repo_slug).length;
  }

  function syncWorkspaceRepoFilters(repoSlug) {
    ["issues", "investigations", "work", "feedback", "approvals"].forEach((view) => {
      filterState(view).repo = defaultString(repoSlug, "");
    });
  }

  function openRepoOnboardingFlow() {
    initRepoOnboardingDrawer();
    renderRepoPicker();
    renderRepoOnboardingDrawer();
    state.repoOnboardingDrawer.open();
    window.setTimeout(() => {
      const input = document.getElementById("repo-onboard-slug");
      if (input) input.focus();
    }, 0);
  }

  function setWorkspaceRepoScope(repoSlug) {
    const normalized = String(repoSlug || "").trim();
    const nextRepo = normalized && sortedRepos().some((repo) => repo.repo_slug === normalized)
      ? normalized
      : "";
    const nextView = nextRepo
      ? ((state.currentView === "home" || state.currentView === "repo") ? "repo" : state.currentView)
      : (state.currentView === "repo" ? "home" : state.currentView);
    const nextRepoTab = nextRepo ? defaultString(state.repoTab, "overview") : "overview";
    clearDraftsForRouteTransition({
      view: nextView,
      repoSlug: nextRepo,
      repoTab: nextRepoTab,
    });
    state.selectedRepo = nextRepo;
    state.selectedIssue = "";
    if (nextRepo) {
      state.taskComposer.repoSlug = nextRepo;
    }
    syncWorkspaceRepoFilters(nextRepo);
    state.currentView = nextView;
    state.repoTab = nextRepoTab;
    renderApp();
    if (state.currentView === "repo") {
      refreshCurrentView({ silent: true }).catch(() => {});
    } else if (state.currentView === "usage") {
      loadUsage({ silent: true });
    }
  }

  function ensureSelection() {
    const repos = sortedRepos();
    if (state.selectedRepo && repos.some((repo) => repo.repo_slug === state.selectedRepo)) {
      return;
    }
    state.selectedRepo = "";
    syncWorkspaceRepoFilters("");
    if (state.currentView === "repo") {
      state.currentView = "home";
      state.repoTab = "overview";
    }
  }

  function openRepoView(repoSlug, tab = "overview") {
    syncWorkspaceRepoFilters(repoSlug);
    state.taskComposer.repoSlug = repoSlug || state.taskComposer.repoSlug;
    clearDraftsForRouteTransition({
      view: "repo",
      repoSlug: repoSlug || "",
      repoTab: defaultString(tab, "overview"),
    });
    state.currentView = "repo";
    state.repoTab = defaultString(tab, "overview");
    state.selectedRepo = repoSlug || "";
    state.selectedIssue = "";
    renderApp();
    refreshCurrentView({ silent: true }).catch(() => {});
  }

  function destroyWidgets() {
    Object.values(state.widgets).forEach((widget) => {
      destroyWidget(widget);
    });
    state.widgets = {};
    state.widgetStateKeys = {};
    destroyForm("issueForm");
    destroyForm("plannedForm");
  }

  function replaceWidget(key, widget) {
    destroyWidget(state.widgets[key]);
    state.widgets[key] = widget;
  }

  function destroyWidget(widget) {
    if (widget && typeof widget.destroy === "function") {
      widget.destroy();
    }
  }

  function destroyForm(key) {
    destroyWidget(state[key]);
    state[key] = null;
  }

  function ensureBodyStructure(signature, html) {
    if (state.pageSignature === signature) {
      return;
    }
    destroyWidgets();
    document.getElementById("page-body").innerHTML = html;
    state.pageSignature = signature;
  }

  function buildMetricCards(cards) {
    return cards.map((card) => {
      return `
        <article class="metric-card">
          <span class="metric-label">${escapeHTML(card.label)}</span>
          <strong class="metric-value">${escapeHTML(card.value)}</strong>
          <p class="metric-note">${escapeHTML(card.note)}</p>
        </article>
      `;
    }).join("");
  }

  function buildQueueSummary(items) {
    return items.map((item) => {
      return `
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">${escapeHTML(item.label)}</span>
          <strong class="queue-value">${escapeHTML(item.value)}</strong>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(item.note)}</p>
        </article>
      `;
    }).join("");
  }

  function buildInlineNotice(message) {
    return `<div class="inline-notice"><span class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(message)}</span></div>`;
  }

  function buildMaintenanceNotice(message, repairCommand) {
    return `
      <section class="surface empty-surface">
        <div class="stack gap-sm">
          <div class="status-pill">Maintenance required</div>
          <p>${escapeHTML(message)}</p>
          <code>${escapeHTML(defaultString(repairCommand, "nana work db-repair"))}</code>
        </div>
      </section>
    `;
  }

  function buildBreadcrumbs() {
    const items = [{ label: "Workspace" }];
    if (state.currentView === "home") {
      items.push({ label: "All Repos", current: true });
      return items;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "repo") {
      const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
      items.push({ label: repo ? repo.repo_slug : "Repo" });
      items.push({ label: defaultString(state.repoTab, "overview").replace(/^./, (value) => value.toUpperCase()), current: true });
      return items;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "feedback") {
      items.push({ label: "Feedback" });
      items.push({ label: state.feedbackTab === "reviews" ? "Reviews" : "Replies", current: true });
      return items;
    }
    const viewLabel = defaultString(state.currentView, "home").replace(/^./, (value) => value.toUpperCase());
    items.push({ label: viewLabel, current: true });
    return items;
  }

  function renderBreadcrumbs() {
    const host = document.getElementById("page-breadcrumb");
    if (!host) return;
    host.innerHTML = `
      <ol class="breadcrumb-list">
        ${buildBreadcrumbs().map((item) => `
          <li>${item.current ? `<span class="breadcrumb-current">${escapeHTML(item.label)}</span>` : `<span>${escapeHTML(item.label)}</span>`}</li>
        `).join("")}
      </ol>
    `;
  }

  function tabButtonMarkup(group, id, label, selected, index, total) {
    // Static identifiers retained for start_ui asset tests:
    // data-repo-tab="overview"
    // data-repo-tab="scouts"
    // data-repo-tab="config"
    // data-repo-tab="controls"
    // data-feedback-tab="reviews"
    // data-feedback-tab="replies"
    const legacyAttr = group === "repo"
      ? ` data-repo-tab="${escapeHTML(id)}"`
      : group === "feedback"
        ? ` data-feedback-tab="${escapeHTML(id)}"`
        : "";
    return `
      <button
        class="page-tab ${selected ? "page-tab-active" : ""}"
        type="button"
        role="tab"
        id="${escapeHTML(group)}-tab-${escapeHTML(id)}"
        aria-selected="${selected ? "true" : "false"}"
        aria-controls="page-body"
        tabindex="${selected ? "0" : "-1"}"
        data-tab-group="${escapeHTML(group)}"
        data-tab-id="${escapeHTML(id)}"
        data-tab-index="${escapeHTML(index)}"
        data-tab-count="${escapeHTML(total)}"
        ${legacyAttr}
      >${escapeHTML(label)}</button>
    `;
  }

  function requestConfirmation(options) {
    const next = {
      ...defaultConfirmDialog(),
      ...options,
      open: true,
    };
    state.confirmDialog = next;
    renderConfirmDialog();
  }

  function closeConfirmationDialog() {
    const dialog = document.getElementById("confirm-dialog");
    if (dialog && dialog.open) {
      dialog.close("cancel");
    }
    const selector = state.confirmDialog.returnFocusSelector;
    const focusID = state.confirmDialog.returnFocusID;
    state.confirmDialog = defaultConfirmDialog();
    if (selector) {
      document.querySelector(selector)?.focus();
    } else if (focusID) {
      document.querySelector(`[data-focus-id="${focusID}"]`)?.focus();
    }
  }

  function renderConfirmDialog() {
    const dialog = document.getElementById("confirm-dialog");
    if (!dialog) return;
    const title = document.getElementById("confirm-dialog-title");
    const message = document.getElementById("confirm-dialog-message");
    const confirm = document.getElementById("confirm-dialog-confirm");
    if (!title || !message || !confirm) return;
    title.textContent = defaultString(state.confirmDialog.title, "Confirm Action");
    message.textContent = defaultString(state.confirmDialog.message, "Review this action before continuing.");
    confirm.textContent = defaultString(state.confirmDialog.confirmLabel, "Confirm");
    confirm.className = state.confirmDialog.tone === "danger" ? "tx-btn tx-btn-danger" : "tx-btn tx-btn-primary";
    if (state.confirmDialog.open && !dialog.open) {
      dialog.showModal();
      confirm.focus();
      return;
    }
    if (!state.confirmDialog.open && dialog.open) {
      dialog.close("cancel");
    }
  }

  function renderStatePill(attentionState, status) {
    return `<span class="run-state-pill run-state-${escapeHTML(defaultString(attentionState, "active"))}">${escapeHTML(defaultString(status, "-"))}</span>`;
  }

  function pauseStateSummary(pauseUntil, pauseReason) {
    const until = String(pauseUntil || "").trim();
    const reason = String(pauseReason || "").trim();
    const parts = [];
    if (until) {
      const formatted = formatDateTime(until);
      parts.push(formatted || until);
    }
    if (reason) {
      parts.push(reason);
    }
    return parts.join(" · ");
  }

  function renderStatePillWithPause(attentionState, status, pauseUntil, pauseReason) {
    const detail = pauseStateSummary(pauseUntil, pauseReason);
    if (!detail) {
      return renderStatePill(attentionState, status);
    }
    return `${renderStatePill(attentionState, status)}<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(detail)}</span>`;
  }

  function runRepoDisplay(run) {
    if (run && String(run.repo_slug || "").trim()) {
      return String(run.repo_slug).trim();
    }
    return defaultString(run && run.repo_label, defaultString(run && run.repo_name, "Standalone"));
  }

  function dropRepo(repoSlug) {
    const slug = String(repoSlug || "").trim();
    if (!slug) return;
    requestConfirmation({
      title: `Drop ${slug}?`,
      message: "This removes tracked repo state, queued work, and managed sandboxes from the workspace.",
      confirmLabel: "Drop Repo",
      tone: "danger",
      onConfirm() {
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${slug}/drop`, {
          method: "POST",
        }).then(() => {
          if (state.logDrawer) {
            state.logDrawer.close();
          }
          if (state.workItemDrawer) {
            state.workItemDrawer.close();
          }
          const refreshes = [load()];
          if (state.issueQueue.loaded) {
            refreshes.push(loadIssueQueue({ silent: true }));
          }
          if (state.investigations.loaded) {
            refreshes.push(loadInvestigations({ silent: true }));
          }
          if (state.feedback.loaded) {
            refreshes.push(loadFeedback({ silent: true }));
          }
          if (state.approvals.loaded) {
            refreshes.push(loadApprovals({ silent: true }));
          }
          Promise.allSettled(refreshes);
          toast("success", "Repo dropped", slug);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Repo drop failed", error.message);
        });
      },
    });
  }

  function renderSurface(title, copy, bodyHTML, options = {}) {
    const extraClass = options.className ? ` ${options.className}` : "";
    return `
      <section class="surface${extraClass}">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>${escapeHTML(title)}</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(copy)}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${bodyHTML}
      </section>
    `;
  }

  function renderSurfacePair(sections) {
    const items = sections.filter(Boolean);
    if (!items.length) return "";
    if (items.length === 1) return items[0];
    return `<section class="layout-two-col">${items.join("")}</section>`;
  }

  function renderSidebar() {
    const nav = document.getElementById("sidebar-nav");
    const totals = state.overview ? state.overview.totals || {} : {};
    const homeActive = state.currentView === "home";
    const homeCount = pendingRuns().length + pendingWorkItems().length + Number(totals.approval_items || 0);
    const taskCount = Number(totals.investigations || 0) + Number(totals.planned_queued || 0) + Number(totals.planned_launching || 0);
    nav.innerHTML = `
      <div class="sidebar-nav-shell">
        <div class="nav-main-links" role="navigation" aria-label="Workspace views">
          <button class="nav-item ${homeActive ? "nav-item-active" : ""}" type="button" data-nav-view="home" aria-current="${homeActive ? "page" : "false"}">
            <span class="nav-label">All Repos</span>
            <span class="nav-count">${homeCount}</span>
          </button>
          <button class="nav-item ${state.currentView === "issues" ? "nav-item-active" : ""}" type="button" data-nav-view="issues" aria-current="${state.currentView === "issues" ? "page" : "false"}">
            <span class="nav-label">Issues</span>
            <span class="nav-count">${Number(totals.issues_queued || 0) + Number(totals.blocked_issues || 0) + Number(totals.issues_in_progress || 0)}</span>
          </button>
          <button class="nav-item ${state.currentView === "investigations" ? "nav-item-active" : ""}" type="button" data-nav-view="investigations" aria-current="${state.currentView === "investigations" ? "page" : "false"}">
            <span class="nav-label">Tasks</span>
            <span class="nav-count">${taskCount}</span>
          </button>
          <button class="nav-item ${state.currentView === "usage" ? "nav-item-active" : ""}" type="button" data-nav-view="usage" aria-current="${state.currentView === "usage" ? "page" : "false"}">
            <span class="nav-label">Usage</span>
            <span class="nav-count">${usageNavCount()}</span>
          </button>
          <button class="nav-item ${state.currentView === "feedback" ? "nav-item-active" : ""}" type="button" data-nav-view="feedback" aria-current="${state.currentView === "feedback" ? "page" : "false"}">
            <span class="nav-label">Feedback</span>
            <span class="nav-count">${Number(totals.review_items || 0) + Number(totals.reply_items || 0)}</span>
          </button>
          <button class="nav-item ${state.currentView === "approvals" ? "nav-item-active" : ""}" type="button" data-nav-view="approvals" aria-current="${state.currentView === "approvals" ? "page" : "false"}">
            <span class="nav-label">Approvals</span>
            <span class="nav-count">${Number(totals.approval_items || 0)}</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function renderHeader() {
    const title = document.getElementById("page-title");
    const subtitle = document.getElementById("page-subtitle");
    const updated = document.getElementById("overview-updated");
    if (!title || !updated) return;
    const setTitle = (value) => {
      title.textContent = value;
    };
    const setUpdated = (value) => {
      updated.textContent = value;
    };
    const setSubtitle = (value) => {
      if (subtitle) subtitle.textContent = value;
    };

    if (!state.overview) {
      if (state.currentView === "usage") {
        setTitle("Usage");
        if (state.overviewError) {
          setSubtitle("Usage data can still load while the workspace overview is unavailable.");
          setUpdated("Overview unavailable.");
        } else if (state.usage.error) {
          setSubtitle("Usage data failed while the workspace overview is still loading.");
          setUpdated("Overview still loading.");
        } else if (state.usage.loaded) {
          setSubtitle("Usage data is ready while the workspace overview is still loading.");
          setUpdated("Overview still loading.");
        } else {
          setSubtitle("Loading usage data and workspace overview.");
          setUpdated("Waiting for state...");
        }
      } else if (state.currentView === "issues") {
        setTitle("Issues");
        setSubtitle("Tracked issues, triage evidence, scheduling, and direct launch actions.");
        setUpdated(state.overviewError ? "Overview unavailable." : "Overview still loading.");
      } else if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
        setTitle("Nana Mission Control");
        setSubtitle("");
        setUpdated(state.overviewError ? "Overview unavailable." : "Overview still loading.");
      } else if (state.currentView === "feedback") {
        setTitle("Feedback");
        setSubtitle(state.feedbackTab === "reviews"
          ? "Review requests and drafted PR feedback."
          : "Drafted thread replies and comment follow-ups.");
        setUpdated(state.overviewError ? "Overview unavailable." : "Overview still loading.");
      } else if (state.currentView === "approvals") {
        setTitle("Approvals");
        setSubtitle("Human-gate queue across publication, feedback submission, and planned launches.");
        setUpdated(state.overviewError ? "Overview unavailable." : "Overview still loading.");
      } else {
        setTitle("All Repos");
        setSubtitle(state.overviewError ? "Workspace overview is unavailable." : "Waiting for state...");
        setUpdated(state.overviewError ? "Overview unavailable." : "Waiting for state...");
      }
      return;
    }

    setUpdated(`Updated ${formatDateTime(state.overview.generated_at)}`);

    if (state.currentView === "home") {
      setTitle("All Repos");
      setSubtitle("Assistant queue across issues, runs, feedback, approvals, and repo automation.");
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "issues") {
      setTitle("Issues");
      setSubtitle(state.selectedRepo
        ? `Tracked issues, triage evidence, scheduling, and direct launch actions for ${state.selectedRepo}.`
        : "Tracked issues, triage evidence, scheduling, and direct launch actions.");
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
      setTitle("Nana Mission Control");
      setSubtitle("");
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "work") {
      setTitle("Work");
      setSubtitle(state.selectedRepo
        ? `Local and GitHub-backed work runs for ${state.selectedRepo}.`
        : "Local and GitHub-backed work runs with detail, state, and logs.");
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "usage") {
      setTitle("Usage");
      setSubtitle("Token spend across NANA-managed sessions, lanes, phases, and activity buckets.");
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "feedback") {
      setTitle("Feedback");
      setSubtitle(state.feedbackTab === "reviews"
        ? (state.selectedRepo ? `Review requests and drafted PR feedback for ${state.selectedRepo}.` : "Review requests and drafted PR feedback.")
        : (state.selectedRepo ? `Drafted thread replies and comment follow-ups for ${state.selectedRepo}.` : "Drafted thread replies and comment follow-ups."));
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "approvals") {
      setTitle("Approvals");
      setSubtitle(state.selectedRepo
        ? `Human-gate queue across publication, feedback submission, and planned launches for ${state.selectedRepo}.`
        : "Human-gate queue across publication, feedback submission, and planned launches.");
      return;
    }

    const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
    if (!repo) {
      setTitle("All Repos");
      setSubtitle("Assistant queue across issues, runs, feedback, approvals, and repo automation.");
      return;
    }

    setTitle(repo.repo_slug);
    setSubtitle(state.repoTab === "controls"
      ? "GitHub issue search, tracked issue scheduling, and planned launch controls."
      : state.repoTab === "findings"
        ? "Persisted findings, markdown imports, and promotion into executable work."
      : state.repoTab === "scouts"
        ? "Scout-discovered items, proposal details, and repo-local management actions."
      : state.repoTab === "config"
        ? "Start-facing repo configuration and participation controls."
        : "Repo queue posture, pending jobs, and tracked work.");
  }

  function renderRepoPicker() {
    const host = document.getElementById("repo-picker-host");
    if (!host) return;
    const repos = sortedRepos();
    const selected = selectedRepoSummary();
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="repo-picker-dropdown">
        <label class="sr-only" for="repo-scope-select">Repo scope</label>
          <select id="repo-scope-select" data-repo-picker="true">
            <optgroup label="Scope">
              <option value="${WORKSPACE_SCOPE_ALL}" ${selected ? "" : "selected"}>All repos</option>
              ${repos.map((repo) => `<option value="${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}" ${selected && selected.repo_slug === repo.repo_slug ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}</option>`).join("")}
            </optgroup>
            <optgroup label="Actions">
              <option value="${WORKSPACE_SCOPE_ONBOARD}">Onboard new repo...</option>
            </optgroup>
          </select>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function renderTabs() {
    const host = document.getElementById("page-tabs");
    if (state.currentView === "feedback") {
      host.setAttribute("role", "tablist");
      host.setAttribute("aria-label", "Feedback sections");
      host.innerHTML = [
        tabButtonMarkup("feedback", "reviews", "Reviews", state.feedbackTab === "reviews", 0, 2),
        tabButtonMarkup("feedback", "replies", "Replies", state.feedbackTab === "replies", 1, 2),
      ].join("");
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView !== "repo" || !selectedRepoSummary()) {
      host.removeAttribute("role");
      host.removeAttribute("aria-label");
      host.innerHTML = "";
      return;
    }
    host.setAttribute("role", "tablist");
    host.setAttribute("aria-label", "Repo sections");
    host.innerHTML = [
      tabButtonMarkup("repo", "overview", "Overview", state.repoTab === "overview", 0, 4),
      tabButtonMarkup("repo", "scouts", "Scouts", state.repoTab === "scouts", 1, 4),
      tabButtonMarkup("repo", "config", "Config", state.repoTab === "config", 2, 4),
      tabButtonMarkup("repo", "controls", "Controls", state.repoTab === "controls", 3, 4),
    ].join("");
  }

  function repoOverviewRows() {
    return sortedRepos().map((repo) => ({
      repo_slug: repo.repo_slug,
      mode: `${defaultString(repo.repo_mode, "unknown")} / ${defaultString(repo.issue_pick_mode, "unknown")}`,
      queued_issues: repo.issue_counts.queued || 0,
      blocked_issues: repo.issue_counts.blocked || 0,
      service_queue: (repo.service_task_counts.queued || 0) + (repo.service_task_counts.running || 0),
      scout_queue: repoScoutQueueCount(repo),
      planned_queue: repoManualPlannedQueueCount(repo),
      pending_runs: pendingRunsForRepo(repo.repo_slug).length,
    }));
  }

  function runGridRows(runs, includeRepo) {
    return runs.map((run) => {
      const row = {
        run_id: run.run_id,
        backend: defaultString(run.backend, "-"),
        work_type: workTypeLabel(run.work_type),
        status: defaultString(run.status, "active"),
        attention_state: defaultString(run.attention_state, "active"),
        pause_reason: defaultString(run.pause_reason, ""),
        pause_until: defaultString(run.pause_until, ""),
        current_phase: defaultString(run.current_phase, "Awaiting phase"),
        current_round: run.current_round || 0,
        updated_at: formatDateTime(run.updated_at),
      };
      if (row.pause_until) {
        row.current_phase = `Retry ${formatDateTime(row.pause_until)}`;
      } else if (row.current_round > 0) {
        row.current_phase = `${row.current_phase} · Round ${row.current_round}`;
      }
      if (includeRepo) {
        row.repo_slug = runRepoDisplay(run);
      }
      return row;
    });
  }

  function workItemRows(items, includeRepo) {
    return items.map((item) => {
      const row = {
        id: item.id,
        source: `${defaultString(item.source, "-")}/${defaultString(item.source_kind, "-")}`,
        work_type: workTypeLabel(item.work_type),
        status: defaultString(item.status, "-"),
        attention_state: defaultString(item.attention_state, "active"),
        pause_reason: defaultString(item.pause_reason, ""),
        pause_until: defaultString(item.pause_until, ""),
        subject: defaultString(item.subject, "(no subject)"),
        updated_at: formatDateTime(item.updated_at),
        draft_kind: defaultString(item.draft_kind, "-"),
      };
      if (includeRepo) {
        row.repo_slug = defaultString(item.repo_slug, "Standalone");
      }
      return row;
    });
  }

  function pendingRunColumns(includeRepo) {
    const columns = [];
    if (includeRepo) {
      columns.push({ field: "repo_slug", label: "Repo" });
    }
    columns.push(
      { field: "backend", label: "Backend" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
      { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePillWithPause(row.attention_state, row.status, row.pause_until, row.pause_reason) },
      { field: "current_phase", label: "Phase" },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
      { field: "run_id", label: "Logs", action: true, template: '<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-log-run-id="{{run_id}}">Logs</button>' },
    );
    return columns;
  }

  function workRunRows(runs, includeRepo) {
    return runs.map((run) => {
      const row = {
        run_id: run.run_id,
        backend: defaultString(run.backend, "-"),
        kind: defaultString(run.backend, "-"),
        status: defaultString(run.status, "active"),
        attention_state: defaultString(run.attention_state, "active"),
        pause_reason: defaultString(run.pause_reason, ""),
        pause_until: defaultString(run.pause_until, ""),
        current_phase: defaultString(run.current_phase, "Awaiting phase"),
        current_round: run.current_round || 0,
        target_url: defaultString(run.target_url, "-"),
        updated_at: formatDateTime(run.updated_at),
        can_stop: Boolean(run.stop_allowed),
        can_sync: run.backend === "github",
        can_rerun: Boolean(run.rerun_allowed),
        can_resolve: Boolean(run.resolve_allowed),
      };
      if (row.pause_until) {
        row.current_phase = `Retry ${formatDateTime(row.pause_until)}`;
      } else if (row.current_round > 0) {
        row.current_phase = `${row.current_phase} · Round ${row.current_round}`;
      }
      if (includeRepo) {
        row.repo_slug = runRepoDisplay(run);
      }
      return row;
    });
  }

  function workRunColumns(includeRepo) {
    const columns = [];
    if (includeRepo) {
      columns.push({ field: "repo_slug", label: "Repo" });
    }
    columns.push(
      { field: "backend", label: "Backend" },
      { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePillWithPause(row.attention_state, row.status, row.pause_until, row.pause_reason) },
      { field: "current_phase", label: "Phase" },
      { field: "target_url", label: "Target" },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
      { field: "run_id", label: "Open", action: true, template: '<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-log-run-id="{{run_id}}">Open</button>' },
      {
        field: "run_id",
        label: "Sync",
        action: true,
        render(row) {
          if (!row.can_sync) {
            return '<span class="data-value-text">N/A</span>';
          }
          return `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-run-sync="${escapeHTML(row.run_id)}">Sync</button>`;
        },
      },
      {
        field: "run_id",
        label: "Stop",
        action: true,
        render(row) {
          if (!row.can_stop) {
            return '<span class="data-value-text">N/A</span>';
          }
          return `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-run-stop="${escapeHTML(row.run_id)}">Stop</button>`;
        },
      },
      {
        field: "run_id",
        label: "Resolve",
        action: true,
        render(row) {
          if (!row.can_resolve) {
            return '<span class="data-value-text">N/A</span>';
          }
          return `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-run-resolve="${escapeHTML(row.run_id)}">Resolve</button>`;
        },
      },
      {
        field: "run_id",
        label: "Re-run",
        action: true,
        render(row) {
          if (!row.can_rerun) {
            return '<span class="data-value-text">N/A</span>';
          }
          return `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-run-rerun="${escapeHTML(row.run_id)}">Re-run</button>`;
        },
      },
      {
        field: "run_id",
        label: "Drop",
        action: true,
        render(row) {
          return `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-run-drop="${escapeHTML(row.run_id)}">Drop</button>`;
        },
      },
    );
    return columns;
  }

  function interpolateTemplate(template, row) {
    return String(template || "").replace(/\{\{\s*([^}\s]+)\s*\}\}/g, (_, key) => {
      const value = row && Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(row, key) ? row[key] : "";
      return escapeHTML(value);
    });
  }

  function rowSelectionMeta(row, options) {
    if (typeof options.rowSelect !== "function") {
      return null;
    }
    return options.rowSelect(row);
  }

  function renderGridCell(column, row, view) {
    if (typeof column.render === "function") {
      return column.render(row, view);
    }
    if (column.template) {
      return interpolateTemplate(column.template, row);
    }
    return `<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(defaultString(row[column.field], "-"))}</span>`;
  }

  function renderGrid(target, columns, data, options = {}) {
    const host = document.getElementById(target);
    if (!host) return;
    const nextRenderKey = defaultString(options.renderKey, "");
    if (nextRenderKey && host.getAttribute("data-grid-render-key") === nextRenderKey) {
      return;
    }
    const preserveScroll = options.preserveScroll !== false;
    const currentTableWrap = preserveScroll ? host.querySelector(".data-table-wrap") : null;
    const currentCards = preserveScroll ? host.querySelector(".data-cards") : null;
    const tableScrollTop = currentTableWrap ? currentTableWrap.scrollTop : 0;
    const tableScrollLeft = currentTableWrap ? currentTableWrap.scrollLeft : 0;
    const cardsScrollTop = currentCards ? currentCards.scrollTop : 0;
    host.innerHTML = "";
    if (!columns.length || !data.length) {
      host.innerHTML = buildInlineNotice(options.emptyMessage || "No data yet");
      if (nextRenderKey) {
        host.setAttribute("data-grid-render-key", nextRenderKey);
      } else {
        host.removeAttribute("data-grid-render-key");
      }
      return;
    }
    const tableRows = data.map((row) => {
      const selection = rowSelectionMeta(row, options);
      const attrs = selection
        ? ` class="data-row-selectable ${selection.selected ? "data-row-selected" : ""}" tabindex="0" role="button" data-row-select-kind="${escapeHTML(selection.kind)}" data-row-select-id="${escapeHTML(selection.value)}" aria-pressed="${selection.selected ? "true" : "false"}"`
        : "";
      return `
        <tr${attrs}>
          ${columns.map((column) => `<td>${renderGridCell(column, row, "table")}</td>`).join("")}
        </tr>
      `;
    }).join("");
    const cardRows = data.map((row) => {
      const selection = rowSelectionMeta(row, options);
      const detailRows = columns.filter((column) => !column.action).map((column) => {
        return `
          <div class="data-card-row">
            <span class="data-card-label">${escapeHTML(column.label)}</span>
            <div class="data-card-value">${renderGridCell(column, row, "card")}</div>
          </div>
        `;
      }).join("");
      const actionRows = columns.filter((column) => column.action).map((column) => renderGridCell(column, row, "card")).join("");
      return `
        <article class="data-card ${selection ? `data-card-selectable ${selection.selected ? "data-card-selected" : ""}` : ""}" ${selection ? `tabindex="0" role="button" data-row-select-kind="${escapeHTML(selection.kind)}" data-row-select-id="${escapeHTML(selection.value)}" aria-pressed="${selection.selected ? "true" : "false"}"` : ""}>
          ${detailRows}
          ${actionRows ? `<div class="data-card-actions">${actionRows}</div>` : ""}
        </article>
      `;
    }).join("");
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="data-panel">
        <div class="data-table-wrap" style="max-height: ${escapeHTML(options.maxHeight || "420px")};">
          <table class="data-table">
            <thead>
              <tr>${columns.map((column) => `<th>${escapeHTML(column.label)}</th>`).join("")}</tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>${tableRows}</tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
        <div class="data-cards">${cardRows}</div>
      </div>
    `;
    if (nextRenderKey) {
      host.setAttribute("data-grid-render-key", nextRenderKey);
    } else {
      host.removeAttribute("data-grid-render-key");
    }
    if (preserveScroll) {
      const nextTableWrap = host.querySelector(".data-table-wrap");
      const nextCards = host.querySelector(".data-cards");
      if (nextTableWrap) {
        nextTableWrap.scrollTop = tableScrollTop;
        nextTableWrap.scrollLeft = tableScrollLeft;
      }
      if (nextCards) {
        nextCards.scrollTop = cardsScrollTop;
      }
    }
  }

  function renderPendingJobsChart(target, runs) {
    const host = document.getElementById(target);
    if (!host) return;
    const grouped = {};
    runs.forEach((run) => {
      const key = runRepoDisplay(run);
      grouped[key] = (grouped[key] || 0) + 1;
    });
    const data = Object.entries(grouped)
      .map(([label, count]) => ({ label, count }))
      .sort((left, right) => right.count - left.count || left.label.localeCompare(right.label));
    if (!data.length) {
      destroyWidget(state.widgets[target]);
      delete state.widgets[target];
      delete state.widgetStateKeys[target];
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">No pending jobs are active.</div>';
      return;
    }
    const chartOptions = {
      type: "bar",
      height: 300,
      title: "Pending jobs by repo",
      xAxis: { title: "Repo" },
      yAxis: { title: "Jobs" },
      series: [
        {
          name: "Pending jobs",
          data: data.map((item) => ({ x: item.label, y: item.count })),
        },
      ],
    };
    const nextKey = JSON.stringify(chartOptions.series);
    if (state.widgets[target] && state.widgetStateKeys[target] === nextKey) {
      return;
    }
    if (state.widgets[target] && typeof state.widgets[target].update === "function") {
      state.widgets[target].update(chartOptions);
      state.widgetStateKeys[target] = nextKey;
      return;
    }
    replaceWidget(target, Teryx.chart(`#${target}`, chartOptions));
    state.widgetStateKeys[target] = nextKey;
  }

  function renderUsageChart(target, chartOptions, emptyMessage) {
    const host = document.getElementById(target);
    if (!host) return;
    const hasData = Array.isArray(chartOptions.series) && chartOptions.series.some((series) => Array.isArray(series.data) && series.data.length);
    if (!hasData) {
      destroyWidget(state.widgets[target]);
      delete state.widgets[target];
      delete state.widgetStateKeys[target];
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(defaultString(emptyMessage, "No usage data is available."))}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    const nextKey = JSON.stringify(chartOptions.series);
    if (state.widgets[target] && state.widgetStateKeys[target] === nextKey) {
      return;
    }
    if (state.widgets[target] && typeof state.widgets[target].update === "function") {
      state.widgets[target].update(chartOptions);
      state.widgetStateKeys[target] = nextKey;
      return;
    }
    replaceWidget(target, Teryx.chart(`#${target}`, chartOptions));
    state.widgetStateKeys[target] = nextKey;
  }

  function usageGroupChartData(groups, limit = 8) {
    return (groups || []).slice(0, limit).map((item) => ({
      x: item.key,
      y: Number(item.total_tokens || 0),
      label: item.key,
    }));
  }

  function usageDayChartData(groups) {
    return [ ...(groups || []) ]
      .sort((left, right) => String(left.key || "").localeCompare(String(right.key || "")))
      .map((item) => ({
        x: item.key,
        y: Number(item.total_tokens || 0),
        label: item.key,
      }));
  }

  function usageInsightsMarkup(insights) {
    if (!Array.isArray(insights) || !insights.length) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">No usage insights are available yet.</div>';
    }
    return `<ul class="usage-insights">${insights.map((insight) => `
      <li class="usage-insight">
        <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(insight.title, "Insight"))}</strong>
        <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(insight.summary, "(none)"))}</span>
        ${insight.command_hint ? `<code>${escapeHTML(insight.command_hint)}</code>` : ""}
      </li>
    `).join("")}</ul>`;
  }

  function syncUsageFilterControl(id, value) {
    const control = document.getElementById(id);
    if (!control || document.activeElement === control) return;
    const nextValue = String(value ?? "");
    if (control.value !== nextValue) {
      control.value = nextValue;
    }
  }

  function syncUsagePageState(filters) {
    const statusPill = document.getElementById("usage-status-pill");
    if (statusPill) {
      statusPill.textContent = state.usage.loading ? "Refreshing" : "Ready";
    }

    const submitButton = document.getElementById("usage-apply-button");
    if (submitButton) {
      submitButton.textContent = state.usage.loading ? "Refreshing..." : "Apply Filters";
      submitButton.disabled = Boolean(state.usage.loading);
    }

    const errorHost = document.getElementById("usage-error-host");
    if (errorHost) {
      errorHost.innerHTML = state.usage.error
        ? `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.usage.error)}</div>`
        : "";
    }

    syncUsageFilterControl("usage-filter-since", defaultString(filters.since, "30d"));
    syncUsageFilterControl("usage-filter-root", defaultString(filters.root, "all"));
    syncUsageFilterControl("usage-filter-activity", filters.activity || "");
    syncUsageFilterControl("usage-filter-phase", filters.phase || "");
    syncUsageFilterControl("usage-filter-model", filters.model || "");
  }

  function initRepoOnboardingDrawer() {
    if (state.repoOnboardingDrawer) return;
    state.repoOnboardingDrawer = Teryx.drawer({
      title: "Onboard Repo",
      position: "right",
      size: "560px",
      content: '<div id="repo-onboarding-drawer-content" class="drawer-shell repo-onboarding-shell"></div>',
    });
  }

  function renderRepoOnboardingDrawer() {
    const host = document.getElementById("repo-onboarding-drawer-content");
    if (!host) return;
    renderWithPreservedDraftFocus(() => {
      const onboarding = state.repoOnboarding || defaultRepoOnboardingState();
      const draft = onboarding.draft || defaultRepoOnboardingState().draft;
      const repoCount = sortedRepos().length;
      const summaryCopy = repoCount
        ? "Add another GitHub repo to the workspace. Advanced routing and scout policies stay editable in the repo Config tab."
        : "No repos are onboarded yet. Add an owner/repo slug or GitHub repo URL to start managing it from this workspace.";
      host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">Workspace</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">Onboard Repo</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(summaryCopy)}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Tracked Repos</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(repoCount ? `${repoCount}` : "0")}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Mode</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.repo_mode, "local"))}</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      ${onboarding.error ? `<div id="repo-onboard-error" class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(onboarding.error)}</div>` : `<div id="repo-onboard-error"></div>`}
      <form id="repo-onboard-form" class="config-form" data-focus-scope="${escapeHTML(repoOnboardingFocusScope())}">
        <div class="config-grid">
          <label class="selector config-field-wide">
            <span>Repo Slug</span>
            <input id="repo-onboard-slug" name="repo_slug" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(draft.repo_slug || "")}" placeholder="owner/repo or https://github.com/owner/repo" data-repo-onboard-field="repo_slug" />
          </label>
          <label class="selector">
            <span>Repo Mode</span>
            <select name="repo_mode" data-repo-onboard-field="repo_mode">
              ${["local", "fork", "repo", "disabled"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(draft.repo_mode, "local") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(value)}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="selector">
            <span>Issue Pick</span>
            <select name="issue_pick_mode" data-repo-onboard-field="issue_pick_mode">
              ${["manual", "label", "auto"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(draft.issue_pick_mode, "manual") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(value)}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="selector">
            <span>PR Forward</span>
            <select name="pr_forward_mode" data-repo-onboard-field="pr_forward_mode">
              ${["approve", "auto"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(draft.pr_forward_mode, "approve") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(value)}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
        </div>
        <div class="config-actions">
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="submit" ${onboarding.submitting ? "disabled" : ""}>${escapeHTML(onboarding.submitting ? "Onboarding..." : "Onboard Repo")}</button>
        </div>
      </form>
    `;
    }, host);
  }

  function submitRepoOnboarding() {
    const payload = repoOnboardingPayload();
    if (!payload.repo_slug) {
      state.repoOnboarding.error = "Enter an owner/repo slug or GitHub repo URL.";
      renderRepoOnboardingDrawer();
      toast("warning", "Repo slug required", "Use owner/repo or a GitHub repo URL.");
      return;
    }
    state.repoOnboarding.submitting = true;
    state.repoOnboarding.error = "";
    renderRepoOnboardingDrawer();
    api("/api/v1/repos", {
      method: "POST",
      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
    }).then((response) => {
      const repo = response.repo || null;
      const created = Boolean(response.created);
      state.repoOnboarding = defaultRepoOnboardingState();
      renderRepoOnboardingDrawer();
      if (state.repoOnboardingDrawer) {
        state.repoOnboardingDrawer.close();
      }
      if (repo && repo.repo_slug) {
        applySelectedRepoPayload(repo);
        openRepoView(repo.repo_slug, "config");
      }
      loadOverview({ silent: true });
      loadRepos({ silent: true });
      toast(created ? "success" : "warning", created ? "Repo onboarded" : "Repo already onboarded", repo && repo.repo_slug ? repo.repo_slug : payload.repo_slug);
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.repoOnboarding.submitting = false;
      state.repoOnboarding.error = error.message;
      renderRepoOnboardingDrawer();
      toast("danger", "Repo onboarding failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function renderRepoCards(target, repos) {
    const host = document.getElementById(target);
    if (!host) return;
    if (!repos.length) {
      host.innerHTML = buildInlineNotice("No repo overview is available yet.");
      return;
    }
    host.innerHTML = `<div class="repo-card-grid">${repos.map((repo) => {
      return `
        <article class="repo-card">
          <div class="repo-card-title-row">
            <div>
              <h3 class="repo-card-title">${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}</h3>
              <p class="repo-card-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(repo.repo_mode, "unknown"))} repo mode · ${escapeHTML(defaultString(repo.issue_pick_mode, "unknown"))} issue pick</p>
            </div>
            <span class="mini-count">${pendingRunsForRepo(repo.repo_slug).length}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="repo-card-metrics">
            <div class="repo-card-metric">
              <span>Queued</span>
              <strong>${repo.issue_counts.queued || 0}</strong>
            </div>
            <div class="repo-card-metric">
              <span>Blocked</span>
              <strong>${repo.issue_counts.blocked || 0}</strong>
            </div>
            <div class="repo-card-metric">
              <span>Service</span>
              <strong>${(repo.service_task_counts.queued || 0) + (repo.service_task_counts.running || 0)}</strong>
            </div>
            <div class="repo-card-metric">
              <span>Scouts</span>
              <strong>${repoScoutQueueCount(repo)}</strong>
            </div>
            <div class="repo-card-metric">
              <span>Dismissed</span>
              <strong>${repoDismissedScoutCount(repo)}</strong>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="repo-card-actions">
            <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary repo-card-button" type="button" data-open-repo="${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}">Open Repo</button>
            ${repoDismissedScoutCount(repo) > 0 ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary repo-card-button" type="button" data-open-repo="${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}" data-open-repo-tab="scouts">Open Scouts</button>` : ""}
          </div>
        </article>
      `;
    }).join("")}</div>`;
  }

  function renderGlobalPage() {
    const runs = pendingRuns();
    const workItems = pendingWorkItems();
    const recentRuns = sortRuns(state.overview.work_runs || []).slice(0, 5);
    const showWorkItems = workItems.length > 0;
    ensureBodyStructure("global", `
      <section id="global-metrics" class="metrics-grid"></section>
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Pending Jobs Chart</h3>
              <p>Work runs that still need operator attention.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="global-pending-chart" class="chart-host"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Repo Overview</h3>
              <p>Queue posture across onboarded repos.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="global-repo-grid"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <section class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Runs</h3>
            <p>Active work first, then the most recent history.</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface-stack">
          <section class="stack-section">
            <div class="stack-section-head">
              <h4>Needs Attention</h4>
              <p>Runs that still need operator action.</p>
            </div>
            <div id="global-pending-grid"></div>
          </section>
          <section class="stack-section">
            <div class="stack-section-head">
              <h4>Recent</h4>
              <p>Latest five local and GitHub-backed runs.</p>
            </div>
            <div id="global-work-grid"></div>
          </section>
        </div>
      </section>
      ${showWorkItems ? `
        <section class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Work Items</h3>
              <p>Drafted or queued replies, reviews, and routed execution requests.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="global-work-item-grid"></div>
        </section>
      ` : ""}
      <details class="surface diagnostics-surface">
        <summary class="details-summary">Diagnostics</summary>
        <div class="details-body">
          <p class="queue-copy">Current orchestration state from the shared HUD snapshot.</p>
          <pre id="hud-json" class="hud-json"></pre>
        </div>
      </details>
    `);

    const metricCards = [
      { label: "Repos", value: state.overview.totals.repos, note: "Onboarded and visible in the console." },
      { label: "Queued Issues", value: state.overview.totals.issues_queued, note: "Tracked issues waiting for work." },
      { label: "Scout Queue", value: (state.overview.totals.scout_queued || 0) + (state.overview.totals.scout_running || 0) + (state.overview.totals.scout_failed || 0), note: "Local scout jobs waiting, paused, active, or failed." },
      { label: "Dismissed Scouts", value: state.overview.totals.scout_dismissed || 0, note: "Saved scout proposals that can be revived from each repo's Scouts tab." },
      { label: "Pending Jobs", value: runs.length, note: "Work runs still in flight or blocked." },
      { label: "Approvals", value: state.overview.totals.approval_items || 0, note: "Human-gate work waiting for review or launch." },
      { label: "Service Queue", value: state.overview.totals.service_queued + state.overview.totals.service_running, note: "Scouts, triage, sync, and reconcile tasks." },
    ];
    if (showWorkItems) {
      metricCards.splice(3, 0, { label: "Work Items", value: state.overview.totals.pending_work_items, note: "Inbound requests waiting for review or submission." });
    }
    const metricsHost = document.getElementById("global-metrics");
    metricsHost.className = showWorkItems ? "metrics-grid metrics-grid-wide" : "metrics-grid";
    metricsHost.innerHTML = buildMetricCards(metricCards);
    renderPendingJobsChart("global-pending-chart", runs);
    renderRepoCards("global-repo-grid", sortedRepos());
    renderGrid("global-pending-grid", pendingRunColumns(true), runGridRows(runs, true), {
      maxHeight: "420px",
      emptyMessage: "No pending jobs are active.",
    });
    renderGrid("global-work-grid", pendingRunColumns(true), runGridRows(recentRuns, true), {
      maxHeight: "320px",
      emptyMessage: "No work runs have been indexed yet.",
    });
    if (showWorkItems) {
      renderGrid("global-work-item-grid", [
        { field: "source", label: "Source" },
        { field: "repo_slug", label: "Repo" },
        { field: "subject", label: "Subject" },
        { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
        { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePillWithPause(row.attention_state, row.status, row.pause_until, row.pause_reason) },
        { field: "draft_kind", label: "Kind" },
        { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
        { field: "id", label: "Review", action: true, template: '<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-work-item-show="{{id}}">Open</button>' },
      ], workItemRows(workItems, true), {
        maxHeight: "360px",
        emptyMessage: "No queued or paused work items are waiting.",
      });
    }
    document.getElementById("hud-json").textContent = JSON.stringify(state.overview.hud || {}, null, 2);
  }

  function renderUsagePage() {
    const report = state.usage.report;
    const summary = report ? report.summary || {} : null;
    const totals = summary && summary.totals ? summary.totals : null;
    const inputSide = totals ? Number(totals.input_tokens || 0) + Number(totals.cached_input_tokens || 0) : 0;
    const outputSide = totals ? Number(totals.output_tokens || 0) + Number(totals.reasoning_output_tokens || 0) : 0;
    const inputShare = totals && Number(totals.total_tokens || 0) > 0 ? (inputSide * 100) / Number(totals.total_tokens || 0) : 0;
    const outputShare = totals && Number(totals.total_tokens || 0) > 0 ? (outputSide * 100) / Number(totals.total_tokens || 0) : 0;
    const filters = state.usage.filters || defaultUsageState().filters;
    const draftScope = usageFiltersDraftScope();

    ensureBodyStructure(`usage:${defaultString(state.selectedRepo, "all")}`, `
      ${buildWorkspaceScopeNotice()}
      <section class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Usage Filters</h3>
            <p>Focus the charts by time window, root, activity, phase, or model.</p>
          </div>
          <span id="usage-status-pill" class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(state.usage.loading ? "Refreshing" : "Ready")}</span>
        </div>
        <form id="usage-filters-form" class="usage-filter-form" data-draft-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}">
          <div class="config-grid usage-filter-grid">
            <label class="selector config-selector">
              <span>Since</span>
              <select id="usage-filter-since">
                ${[
                  { value: "24h", label: "24 hours" },
                  { value: "7d", label: "7 days" },
                  { value: "30d", label: "30 days" },
                  { value: "90d", label: "90 days" },
                  { value: "all", label: "All time" },
                ].map((option) => `<option value="${option.value}" ${filters.since === option.value ? "selected" : ""}>${option.label}</option>`).join("")}
              </select>
            </label>
            <label class="selector config-selector">
              <span>Root</span>
              <select id="usage-filter-root">
                ${[
                  { value: "all", label: "All roots" },
                  { value: "main", label: "Main" },
                  { value: "investigate", label: "Investigate" },
                  { value: "work", label: "Work" },
                  { value: "local-work", label: "Local Work" },
                  { value: "start", label: "Start" },
                ].map((option) => `<option value="${option.value}" ${filters.root === option.value ? "selected" : ""}>${option.label}</option>`).join("")}
              </select>
            </label>
            <label class="selector config-selector">
              <span>Activity</span>
              <input id="usage-filter-activity" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(filters.activity || "")}" placeholder="work, scout, investigate..." />
            </label>
            <label class="selector config-selector">
              <span>Phase</span>
              <input id="usage-filter-phase" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(filters.phase || "")}" placeholder="implementation, review..." />
            </label>
            <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
              <span>Model</span>
              <input id="usage-filter-model" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(filters.model || "")}" placeholder="gpt-5.4" />
            </label>
          </div>
          <div class="config-actions">
            <button id="usage-apply-button" class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="submit" ${state.usage.loading ? "disabled" : ""}>${escapeHTML(state.usage.loading ? "Refreshing..." : "Apply Filters")}</button>
            <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-usage-reset="true">Reset</button>
          </div>
        </form>
        <div id="usage-error-host">${state.usage.error ? `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.usage.error)}</div>` : ""}</div>
      </section>
      <section id="usage-metrics" class="metrics-grid metrics-grid-wide"></section>
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Root Breakdown</h3>
              <p>Token split across main, work, investigate, start, and local-work roots.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="usage-root-chart" class="chart-host"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Phase Breakdown</h3>
              <p>Implementation, review, validation, triage, and scout burden.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="usage-phase-chart" class="chart-host"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Activity Cost</h3>
              <p>Token spend by high-level activity bucket.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="usage-activity-chart" class="chart-host"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Daily Trend</h3>
              <p>Token spend over time for the current filter window.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="usage-day-chart" class="chart-host"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Top Lanes</h3>
              <p>Highest token spend across leader, reviewer, validator, and specialist lanes.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="usage-lane-chart" class="chart-host"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Analytics</h3>
              <p>High-signal summaries from the current filtered data set.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="usage-insights"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <section class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Top Sessions</h3>
            <p>Most expensive sessions in the current filtered scope.</p>
          </div>
          <span class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(report && Array.isArray(report.top_sessions) ? String(report.top_sessions.length) : "0")} rows</span>
        </div>
        <div id="usage-sessions-grid"></div>
      </section>
    `);

    syncUsagePageState(filters);

    document.getElementById("usage-metrics").innerHTML = buildMetricCards([
      { label: "Total Tokens", value: formatTokenCompact(totals && totals.total_tokens || 0), note: "All token spend in the current filter scope." },
      { label: "Sessions", value: String(totals && totals.sessions || 0), note: "Sessions that matched the current filters." },
      { label: "Roots Scanned", value: String(summary && summary.session_roots_scanned || 0), note: "Distinct session trees inspected for this report." },
      { label: "Input Share", value: formatPercent(inputShare), note: "Input plus cached-input percentage of total tokens." },
      { label: "Output Tokens", value: formatTokenCompact(outputSide), note: "Output plus reasoning-output token total." },
      { label: "Missing Telemetry", value: String(totals && totals.missing_telemetry || 0), note: "Sessions with no token_count snapshots." },
    ]);

    renderUsageChart("usage-root-chart", {
      type: "donut",
      height: 300,
      title: "Tokens by root",
      legend: { position: "right" },
      series: [{ name: "Tokens", data: usageGroupChartData(report ? report.by_root : [], 8) }],
    }, state.usage.loading ? "Loading usage breakdown..." : "No root data is available.");

    renderUsageChart("usage-phase-chart", {
      type: "donut",
      height: 300,
      title: "Tokens by phase",
      legend: { position: "right" },
      series: [{ name: "Tokens", data: usageGroupChartData(report ? report.by_phase : [], 8) }],
    }, state.usage.loading ? "Loading phase data..." : "No phase data is available.");

    renderUsageChart("usage-activity-chart", {
      type: "bar",
      height: 320,
      title: "Tokens by activity",
      xAxis: { title: "Activity" },
      yAxis: { title: "Tokens" },
      series: [{ name: "Tokens", data: usageGroupChartData(report ? report.by_activity : [], 8) }],
    }, state.usage.loading ? "Loading activity data..." : "No activity data is available.");

    renderUsageChart("usage-day-chart", {
      type: "area",
      height: 320,
      title: "Daily token trend",
      xAxis: { title: "Day" },
      yAxis: { title: "Tokens" },
      series: [{ name: "Tokens", data: usageDayChartData(report ? report.by_day : []) }],
    }, state.usage.loading ? "Loading trend data..." : "No daily trend is available.");

    renderUsageChart("usage-lane-chart", {
      type: "bar",
      height: 320,
      title: "Top lanes",
      xAxis: { title: "Lane" },
      yAxis: { title: "Tokens" },
      series: [{ name: "Tokens", data: usageGroupChartData((report ? report.by_lane : []).filter((item) => defaultString(item.key, "") !== "(unknown)"), 8) }],
    }, state.usage.loading ? "Loading lane data..." : "No lane data is available.");

    const insightsHost = document.getElementById("usage-insights");
    if (insightsHost) {
      insightsHost.innerHTML = usageInsightsMarkup(report ? report.insights : []);
    }

    renderGrid("usage-sessions-grid", [
      { field: "session_id", label: "Session" },
      { field: "root", label: "Root" },
      { field: "activity", label: "Activity" },
      { field: "phase", label: "Phase" },
      { field: "lane", label: "Lane" },
      { field: "model", label: "Model" },
      { field: "total_tokens", label: "Tokens", render: (row) => `<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(formatTokenCompact(row.total_tokens))}</span>` },
      { field: "timestamp", label: "Updated", render: (row) => `<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(row.timestamp))}</span>` },
      { field: "cwd", label: "Workspace" },
    ], (report && report.top_sessions || []).map((session) => ({
      session_id: defaultString(session.session_id, "(unknown)"),
      root: defaultString(session.root, "(unknown)"),
      activity: defaultString(session.activity, "(unknown)"),
      phase: defaultString(session.phase, "(unknown)"),
      lane: defaultString(session.lane, "(unknown)"),
      model: defaultString(session.model, "(unknown)"),
      total_tokens: Number(session.total_tokens || 0),
      timestamp: defaultString(session.timestamp, ""),
      cwd: defaultString(session.cwd, "(unknown)"),
    })), {
      maxHeight: "420px",
      emptyMessage: state.usage.loading ? "Loading top sessions..." : defaultString(state.usage.error, "No sessions matched these usage filters."),
    });
    restoreDraftScope(draftScope, document.getElementById("usage-filters-form"));
  }

  function filteredIssueQueueItems() {
    const filter = filterState("issues");
    return (state.issueQueue.items || []).filter((item) => {
      return matchesRepoFilter(item, filter.repo) &&
        matchesAttentionFilter(item, filter.attention) &&
        matchesQuery(item, ["title", "repo_slug", "source_url", "triage_rationale", "blocked_reason"], filter.query);
    });
  }

  function filteredInvestigations() {
    const filter = filterState("investigations");
    return (state.investigations.items || []).filter((item) => {
      return matchesRepoFilter(item, filter.repo) &&
        matchesTaskStatusFilter(item, filter.status) &&
        matchesAttentionFilter(item, filter.attention) &&
        matchesKindFilter(item, filter.kind) &&
        matchesQuery(item, ["id", "kind", "title", "summary", "description", "repo_slug", "run_id", "status", "raw_status", "attention_state", "work_type"], filter.query);
    });
  }

  function filteredWorkRuns() {
    const filter = filterState("work");
    return sortRuns(state.overview ? state.overview.work_runs || [] : []).filter((item) => {
      return matchesRepoFilter(item, filter.repo) &&
        matchesAttentionFilter(item, filter.attention) &&
        matchesKindFilter(item, filter.kind) &&
        matchesQuery(item, ["repo_slug", "run_id", "target_url", "current_phase", "status", "backend", "pause_reason", "pause_until"], filter.query);
    });
  }

  function filteredFeedbackItems() {
    const filter = filterState("feedback");
    const sourceItems = state.feedbackTab === "reviews" ? state.feedback.reviews : state.feedback.replies;
    return (sourceItems || []).filter((item) => {
      return matchesRepoFilter(item, filter.repo) &&
        matchesAttentionFilter(item, filter.attention) &&
        matchesQuery(item, ["subject", "repo_slug", "draft_summary", "draft_body", "target_url", "comment_path", "pause_reason", "pause_until"], filter.query);
    });
  }

  function filteredApprovalItems() {
    const filter = filterState("approvals");
    return (state.approvals.items || []).filter((item) => {
      return matchesRepoFilter(item, filter.repo) &&
        matchesAttentionFilter(item, filter.attention) &&
        matchesKindFilter(item, filter.kind) &&
        matchesQuery(item, ["subject", "repo_slug", "reason", "next_action", "target_url"], filter.query);
    });
  }

  function renderIssuesPage() {
    const items = filteredIssueQueueItems();
    const selected = selectedIssueQueueItemFrom(items);
    const draftScope = issuesDetailDraftScope(selected);
    ensureBodyStructure(`issues:${defaultString(state.selectedRepo, "all")}`, `
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Tracked Issues</h3>
              <p>Mirrored issues across onboarded repos.</p>
            </div>
            <span class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(String(items.length))} items</span>
          </div>
          ${buildFilterToolbar("issues", { placeholder: "Search title, triage rationale, URL, or blocked reason" })}
          <div id="issues-grid"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface detail-surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Issue Detail</h3>
              <p>Triage evidence, publication state, and launch actions.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="issue-detail"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
    `);
    renderGrid("issues-grid", [
      { field: "repo_slug", label: "Repo" },
      { field: "source_number", label: "#" },
      { field: "title", label: "Title" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
