      { field: "priority_label", label: "Priority" },
      { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePill(row.attention_state, row.status) },
      { field: "triage_status", label: "Triage" },
      { field: "schedule_at", label: "Scheduled", render: (row) => `<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(defaultString(row.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(row.schedule_at) : "", "Not scheduled"))}</span>` },
    ], items, {
      maxHeight: "520px",
      emptyMessage: state.issueQueue.loading ? "Loading tracked issues..." : defaultString(state.issueQueue.error, "No tracked issues are available."),
      rowSelect(row) {
        return {
          kind: "issue",
          value: row.id,
          selected: selected ? selected.id === row.id : false,
        };
      },
    });
    const host = document.getElementById("issue-detail");
    if (!host) return;
    renderWithPreservedDraftFocus(() => {
      if (state.issueQueue.error) {
        host.innerHTML = `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.issueQueue.error)}</div>`;
        return;
      }
      if (state.issueQueue.loading && !selected) {
        host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Loading issue detail...</div>';
        return;
      }
      if (!selected) {
        host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">No issue selected.</div>';
        return;
      }
      host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(selected.repo_slug)} #${escapeHTML(selected.source_number)}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(selected.title)}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.source_url, "No source URL captured."))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Priority</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(selected.priority_label)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Work Type</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(selected.work_type))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Status</span><span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePill(selected.attention_state, selected.status)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Triage</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.triage_status, "-"))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Updated</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(selected.updated_at))}</span></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="drawer-toolbar">
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-issue-investigate="${escapeHTML(selected.id)}">Investigate</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-issue-launch-work="${escapeHTML(selected.id)}">Start Work</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-issue-open-repo="${escapeHTML(selected.repo_slug)}">Open Repo</button>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Edit Issue</h3>
            <p>Override priority or schedule directly from the assistant workspace.</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="config-grid" data-draft-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}">
          <label class="selector config-selector">
            <span>Priority</span>
            <select id="issue-detail-priority">
              ${[0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((priority) => `<option value="${priority}" ${selected.priority === priority ? "selected" : ""}>P${priority}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="selector config-selector">
            <span>Schedule</span>
            <input id="issue-detail-schedule" type="datetime-local" value="${escapeHTML(toDateTimeLocal(selected.schedule_at))}" />
          </label>
          <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
            <span>Deferred Reason</span>
            <textarea id="issue-detail-deferred" rows="3" placeholder="Explain why this should wait.">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.deferred_reason, ""))}</textarea>
          </label>
        </div>
        <div class="config-actions">
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-issue-clear-schedule="${escapeHTML(selected.id)}">Clear Schedule</button>
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-issue-save="${escapeHTML(selected.id)}">Save Issue</button>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Priority Source</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.priority_source, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Work Type</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(selected.work_type))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Schedule</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(selected.schedule_at) : "", "Not scheduled"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Deferred Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.deferred_reason, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Blocked Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.blocked_reason, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Last Run</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.last_run_id, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Published PR</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.published_pr_url, "(none)"))}</p></article>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Triage Rationale</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.triage_updated_at ? formatDateTime(selected.triage_updated_at) : "", "No triage timestamp recorded."))}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.triage_rationale, "(none)"))}</p>
        ${selected.triage_error ? `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(selected.triage_error)}</div>` : ""}
      </div>
    `;
      restoreDraftScope(draftScope, host);
    }, host);
  }

  function taskLaunchKindLabel(value) {
    switch (String(value || "").trim()) {
      case "investigation":
        return "Investigation";
      case "manual_scout":
        return "Manual Scout";
      case "local_work":
        return "Coding";
      default:
        return defaultString(value, "Task");
    }
  }

  function taskScheduledItems(repo) {
    if (!repo || !repo.state) return [];
    return Object.values(repo.state.planned_items || {})
      .filter((item) => ["local_work", "investigation", "manual_scout"].includes(String(item.launch_kind || "").trim()))
      .sort((left, right) => timestamp(right.updated_at) - timestamp(left.updated_at));
  }

  function taskScheduledRows(repo) {
    return taskScheduledItems(repo).map((item) => ({
      id: item.id,
      title: defaultString(item.title, "(untitled)"),
      launch_kind: taskLaunchKindLabel(item.launch_kind),
      schedule_at: item.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(item.schedule_at) : "Ready now",
      state: defaultString(item.state, "queued"),
      updated_at: formatDateTime(item.updated_at),
      result: defaultString(item.launch_result || item.last_error, "-"),
      can_launch: item.state === "queued" || item.state === "failed",
      can_remove: item.state === "queued" || item.state === "failed",
    }));
  }

  function findingStatusLabel(status) {
    switch (String(status || "").trim()) {
      case "promoted":
        return "Promoted";
      case "dismissed":
        return "Dismissed";
      case "resolved":
        return "Resolved";
      default:
        return "Open";
    }
  }

  function findingSourceLabel(finding) {
    switch (String(finding && finding.source_kind || "").trim()) {
      case "manual_scout":
        return `Manual Scout · ${defaultString(finding.source_id, "-")}`;
      case "investigation":
        return `Investigation · ${defaultString(finding.source_id, "-")}`;
      case "coding":
        return `Coding Run · ${defaultString(finding.source_id, "-")}`;
      case "manual_import":
        return `Markdown Import · ${defaultString(finding.source_id, "-")}`;
      default:
        return defaultString(finding && finding.source_kind, "-");
    }
  }

  function findingParentTaskLabel(finding) {
    const kind = defaultString(finding && finding.parent_task_kind, "");
    const id = defaultString(finding && finding.parent_task_id, "");
    return kind && id ? `${kind} · ${id}` : "None";
  }

  function findingPromotedTaskLabel(finding) {
    return defaultString(finding && finding.promoted_task_id, "Not linked");
  }

  function taskFindingRows(items) {
    return (items || []).map((finding) => ({
      id: finding.id,
      title: defaultString(finding.title, "(untitled)"),
      source: findingSourceLabel(finding),
      parent_task: findingParentTaskLabel(finding),
      status: findingStatusLabel(finding.status),
      status_key: defaultString(finding.status, "open"),
      severity: defaultString(finding.severity, "medium"),
      work_type: workTypeLabel(finding.work_type),
      promoted_task: findingPromotedTaskLabel(finding),
      updated_at: formatDateTime(finding.updated_at),
      finding,
    }));
  }

  function renderTaskFindingDetail(repo, finding) {
    const host = document.getElementById("task-finding-detail");
    if (!host) return;
    renderWithPreservedDraftFocus(() => {
      if (state.taskFindings.error && !finding) {
        host.innerHTML = `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.taskFindings.error)}</div>`;
        return;
      }
      if (state.taskFindings.loading && !finding) {
        host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Loading findings...</div>';
        return;
      }
      if (!finding) {
        host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">No finding selected.</div>';
        return;
      }
      const draftScope = taskFindingDraftScope(repo, finding);
      host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(findingSourceLabel(finding))}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.title, "(untitled)"))}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.summary, "(no summary)"))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Status</span><span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePill(defaultString(finding.status, "open"), findingStatusLabel(finding.status))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Severity</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.severity, "medium"))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Work Type</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(finding.work_type))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Parent Task</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(findingParentTaskLabel(finding))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Promoted Task</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(findingPromotedTaskLabel(finding))}</span></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="config-grid" data-draft-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}">
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Title</span>
          <input id="task-finding-title" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.title, ""))}" />
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Summary</span>
          <textarea id="task-finding-summary" rows="3">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.summary, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Detail</span>
          <textarea id="task-finding-detail-input" rows="6">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.detail, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Evidence</span>
          <textarea id="task-finding-evidence" rows="4">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.evidence, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Severity</span>
          <select id="task-finding-severity">
            ${["low", "medium", "high", "critical"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(finding.severity, "medium") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${value}</option>`).join("")}
          </select>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Work Type</span>
          <select id="task-finding-work-type">
            ${["bug_fix", "refactor", "feature", "test_only"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(finding.work_type, "feature") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(value))}</option>`).join("")}
          </select>
        </label>
      </div>
      <div class="config-actions">
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-finding-dismiss="${escapeHTML(finding.id)}">Dismiss</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-finding-promote="${escapeHTML(finding.id)}" ${finding.promoted_task_id ? "disabled" : ""}>Promote</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-task-finding-save="${escapeHTML(finding.id)}" ${state.taskFindings.saving ? "disabled" : ""}>${escapeHTML(state.taskFindings.saving ? "Saving..." : "Save Finding")}</button>
      </div>
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Source Item</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.source_item_id, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Files</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML((finding.files || []).join(", ") || "(none)")}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Path</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.path, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Route / Page</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML([defaultString(finding.route, ""), defaultString(finding.page, "")].filter(Boolean).join(" / ") || "(none)")}</p></article>
      </div>
    `;
      restoreDraftScope(draftScope, host);
    }, host);
  }

  function findingImportSessionRows(items) {
    return (items || []).map((session) => ({
      id: session.id,
      file_path: defaultString(session.input_file_path, "(inline markdown)"),
      parse_status: defaultString(session.parse_status, "pending"),
      candidate_count: Array.isArray(session.candidates) ? session.candidates.length : 0,
      updated_at: formatDateTime(session.updated_at),
    }));
  }

  function findingImportCandidateRows(session) {
    if (!session || !Array.isArray(session.candidates)) return [];
    return session.candidates.map((candidate) => ({
      candidate_id: candidate.candidate_id,
      title: defaultString(candidate.title, "(untitled)"),
      status: defaultString(candidate.status, "candidate"),
      severity: defaultString(candidate.severity, "medium"),
      work_type: workTypeLabel(candidate.work_type),
    }));
  }

  function renderFindingImportDetail(repo, session, candidate) {
    const host = document.getElementById("task-import-detail");
    if (!host) return;
    renderWithPreservedDraftFocus(() => {
      if (state.findingImports.error && !session) {
        host.innerHTML = `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.findingImports.error)}</div>`;
        return;
      }
      if (state.findingImports.loading && !session) {
        host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Loading import sessions...</div>';
        return;
      }
      if (!session) {
        host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">No import session selected.</div>';
        return;
      }
      if (!candidate) {
        host.innerHTML = `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Session</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(session.id)}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">File</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(session.input_file_path, "(inline markdown)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Parse Status</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(session.parse_status, "pending"))}</p></article>
        </div>
        ${session.parse_error ? `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(session.parse_error)}</div>` : '<div class="status-pill">Select a candidate to review.</div>'}
      `;
        return;
      }
      const draftScope = findingImportCandidateDraftScope(repo, session, candidate);
      host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(session.id)}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(candidate.title, "(untitled)"))}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(candidate.summary, "(no summary)"))}</p>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="config-grid" data-draft-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}">
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Title</span>
          <input id="task-import-candidate-title" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(defaultString(candidate.title, ""))}" />
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Summary</span>
          <textarea id="task-import-candidate-summary" rows="3">${escapeHTML(defaultString(candidate.summary, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Detail</span>
          <textarea id="task-import-candidate-detail" rows="6">${escapeHTML(defaultString(candidate.detail, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Evidence</span>
          <textarea id="task-import-candidate-evidence" rows="4">${escapeHTML(defaultString(candidate.evidence, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Severity</span>
          <select id="task-import-candidate-severity">
            ${["low", "medium", "high", "critical"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(candidate.severity, "medium") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${value}</option>`).join("")}
          </select>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Work Type</span>
          <select id="task-import-candidate-work-type">
            ${["bug_fix", "refactor", "feature", "test_only"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(candidate.work_type, "feature") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(value))}</option>`).join("")}
          </select>
        </label>
      </div>
      <div class="config-actions">
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-import-candidate-drop="${escapeHTML(candidate.candidate_id)}" ${candidate.status === "candidate" ? "" : "disabled"}>Drop</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-import-candidate-promote="${escapeHTML(candidate.candidate_id)}" ${candidate.status === "candidate" ? "" : "disabled"}>Promote to Finding</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-task-import-candidate-save="${escapeHTML(candidate.candidate_id)}">Save Candidate</button>
      </div>
      ${session.parse_error ? `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(session.parse_error)}</div>` : ""}
    `;
      restoreDraftScope(draftScope, host);
    }, host);
  }

  function renderTaskInvestigationDetail(detail) {
    const host = document.getElementById("investigation-detail");
    if (!host) return;
    if (state.investigations.detailLoading && !detail) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Loading investigation detail...</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (state.investigations.error && !detail) {
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.investigations.error)}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    if (!detail || !detail.summary) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">No investigation selected.</div>';
      return;
    }
    const summary = detail.summary;
    const report = detail.final_report;
    const validator = detail.latest_validator_result;
    const investigationPauseSummary = pauseStateSummary(summary.pause_until, summary.pause_reason);
    const issueSections = report && Array.isArray(report.issues) && report.issues.length
      ? report.issues.map((issue) => `
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.id, "Issue"))}</span>
          <p class="queue-copy"><strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.short_explanation, "(none)"))}</strong></p>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.detailed_explanation, "(none)"))}</p>
          ${Array.isArray(issue.proofs) && issue.proofs.length ? `
            <ul class="status-list">${issue.proofs.map((proof) => `
              <li>
                <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.title, proof.kind))}</strong>
                <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.why_it_proves, "(no explanation)"))}</span>
                <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.path, defaultString(proof.link, "(no link)")))}</span>
              </li>
            `).join("")}</ul>
          ` : '<div class="status-pill">No proofs attached.</div>'}
        </article>
      `).join("")
      : '<div class="status-pill">No issue-level findings were recorded.</div>';
    const proofSections = report && Array.isArray(report.overall_proofs) && report.overall_proofs.length
      ? `<ul class="status-list">${report.overall_proofs.map((proof) => `
          <li>
            <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.title, proof.kind))}</strong>
            <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.why_it_proves, "(no explanation)"))}</span>
            <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.path, defaultString(proof.link, "(no link)")))}</span>
          </li>
        `).join("")}</ul>`
      : '<div class="status-pill">No overall proofs are available.</div>';
    const validatorContent = validator
      ? `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Accepted</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(String(Boolean(validator.accepted)))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Summary</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(validator.summary, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
        ${Array.isArray(validator.violations) && validator.violations.length ? `
          <ul class="status-list">${validator.violations.map((violation) => `
            <li>
              <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(violation.code, "violation"))}</strong>
              <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(violation.path, "$"))}</span>
              <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(violation.message, "(none)"))}</span>
            </li>
          `).join("")}</ul>
        ` : '<div class="status-pill">No validator violations.</div>'}
      `
      : '<div class="status-pill">No validator result available.</div>';
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.repo_slug, "Workspace"))}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.overall_status, summary.status))}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.query, "(no query)"))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Run</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(summary.run_id)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Accepted Round</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.accepted_round, "-"))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Issues</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.issue_count, 0))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Updated</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(summary.updated_at))}</span></div>
          ${investigationPauseSummary ? `<div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Retry</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(investigationPauseSummary)}</span></div>` : ""}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Summary</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.overall_short_explanation, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Workspace</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.workspace_root, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Final Report</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.final_report_path, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Last Error</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.last_error, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        ${summary.pause_until ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Pause Until</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(summary.pause_until))}</p></article>` : ""}
        ${summary.pause_reason ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Pause Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(summary.pause_reason)}</p></article>` : ""}
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Detailed Explanation</h3><p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.completed_at ? formatDateTime(summary.completed_at) : "", "Run not completed yet."))}</p></div></div>
        <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(report && report.overall_detailed_explanation, "(none)"))}</p>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Proofs</h3><p>Primary and supplementary proof links.</p></div></div>
        ${proofSections}
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Findings</h3><p>Issue-level conclusions for this investigation.</p></div></div>
        <div class="queue-summary">${issueSections}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Validator</h3><p>Latest validator result for this run.</p></div></div>
        ${validatorContent}
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function taskStatusLabel(status) {
    const value = defaultString(status, "");
    if (!value) return "Queued";
    return value.split("_").map((part) => part.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + part.slice(1)).join(" ");
  }

  function taskStatusTone(status) {
    switch (defaultString(status, "")) {
      case "running":
      case "active":
        return "active";
      case "failed":
        return "failed";
      case "paused":
      case "in_review":
      case "blocked":
        return "blocked";
      case "dismissed":
      case "completed":
        return "completed";
      default:
        return "queued";
    }
  }

  function taskItemsForStatus(items, status) {
    return (items || []).filter((item) => defaultString(item && item.attention_state, defaultString(item && item.status, "")) === status);
  }

  function taskTypeLabel(value) {
    return defaultString(String(value || "").replace(/_/g, " "), "task");
  }

  function taskKindOptions(items) {
    const values = new Set(["all"]);
    (items || []).forEach((item) => {
      const kind = defaultString(item && item.kind, "");
      if (kind) values.add(kind);
    });
    return Array.from(values).sort().map((kind) => ({
      value: kind,
      label: kind === "all" ? "All types" : taskTypeLabel(kind),
    }));
  }

  function taskRepoOptions(items) {
    const values = new Set();
    sortedRepos().forEach((repo) => values.add(repo.repo_slug));
    (items || []).forEach((item) => {
      const repo = defaultString(item && item.repo_slug, "");
      if (repo) values.add(repo);
    });
    return Array.from(values).sort();
  }

  function activeTaskFilterCount(filter) {
    if (!filter) return 0;
    return (String(filter.query || "").trim() ? 1 : 0) +
      (filter.status && filter.status !== "all" ? 1 : 0) +
      (filter.kind && filter.kind !== "all" ? 1 : 0) +
      (filter.repo ? 1 : 0);
  }

  function taskFilterChip(label, value, field) {
    if (!value || value === "all") return "";
    const text = field === "query" ? `"${value}"` : `${label}: ${value}`;
    return `<button class="mission-filter-chip" type="button" data-task-filter-clear="${escapeHTML(field)}">${escapeHTML(text)} ×</button>`;
  }

  function renderTaskToolbar(items) {
    const filter = filterState("investigations");
    const activeCount = activeTaskFilterCount(filter);
    const statusOptions = [{ id: "all", title: "All states" }, ...TASK_STATUS_GROUPS].map((option) => {
      const selected = filter.status === option.id ? "selected" : "";
      return `<option value="${escapeHTML(option.id)}" ${selected}>${escapeHTML(option.title)}</option>`;
    }).join("");
    const kindOptions = taskKindOptions(items).map((option) => {
      const selected = filter.kind === option.value ? "selected" : "";
      return `<option value="${escapeHTML(option.value)}" ${selected}>${escapeHTML(option.label)}</option>`;
    }).join("");
    const repoOptions = [`<option value="" ${filter.repo ? "" : "selected"}>All repos</option>`]
      .concat(taskRepoOptions(items).map((repo) => `<option value="${escapeHTML(repo)}" ${filter.repo === repo ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(repo)}</option>`))
      .join("");
    const chips = [
      taskFilterChip("Status", TASK_STATUS_GROUPS.find((item) => item.id === filter.status)?.title || "", "status"),
      taskFilterChip("Type", filter.kind !== "all" ? taskTypeLabel(filter.kind) : "", "kind"),
      taskFilterChip("Repo", filter.repo, "repo"),
      taskFilterChip("", String(filter.query || "").trim(), "query"),
    ].filter(Boolean).join("");
    return `
      <section class="mission-toolbar surface">
        <div class="mission-toolbar-main">
          <label class="mission-search">
            <span class="sr-only">Search tasks</span>
            <input type="search" value="${escapeHTML(filter.query)}" placeholder="Search tasks..." data-view-filter="investigations" data-view-filter-name="query" />
          </label>
          <label class="mission-select">
            <span>Status</span>
            <select data-view-filter="investigations" data-view-filter-name="status">${statusOptions}</select>
          </label>
          <label class="mission-select">
            <span>Type</span>
            <select data-view-filter="investigations" data-view-filter-name="kind">${kindOptions}</select>
          </label>
          <label class="mission-select mission-select-repo">
            <span>Repo</span>
            <select data-view-filter="investigations" data-view-filter-name="repo">${repoOptions}</select>
          </label>
          <span class="mission-filter-count">${activeCount ? `${activeCount} active` : "No filters"}</span>
          ${activeCount ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-task-filter-clear="all">Clear</button>` : ""}
          <button id="open-task-schedule-button" class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary mission-add-button" type="button">+ Task</button>
        </div>
        ${chips ? `<div class="mission-filter-chips">${chips}</div>` : ""}
      </section>
    `;
  }

  function taskStatusStrip(items) {
    return TASK_STATUS_GROUPS.map((group) => {
      const count = taskItemsForStatus(items, group.id).length;
      return `
        <button class="mission-status-chip ${filterState("investigations").status === group.id ? "mission-status-chip-active" : ""}" type="button" data-task-status-filter="${escapeHTML(group.id)}">
          <span>${escapeHTML(group.title)}</span>
          <strong>${count}</strong>
        </button>
      `;
    }).join("");
  }

  function taskPrimaryActionLabel(item) {
    if (item && item.can_open_job) return "Open Job";
    switch (defaultString(item && item.status, "")) {
      case "running":
        return "Logs";
      case "blocked":
        return "Resolve";
      case "queued":
        return "Details";
      case "in_review":
        return "Review";
      default:
        return "Details";
    }
  }

  function renderTaskFeedRow(item) {
    const selected = item.id === state.investigations.selectedRunID;
    const repo = defaultString(item.repo_slug, "Workspace");
    const priority = defaultString(item.priority_label, "P3");
    const kind = taskTypeLabel(item.kind);
    const schedule = item.schedule_at ? `scheduled ${formatDateTime(item.schedule_at)}` : `updated ${formatDateTime(item.updated_at)}`;
    const summary = defaultString(item.summary, item.description || "No summary recorded.");
    return `
      <button class="mission-task-row ${selected ? "mission-task-row-selected" : ""}" type="button" data-task-open="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">
        <span class="mission-task-priority">${escapeHTML(priority)}</span>
        <span class="mission-task-type">${escapeHTML(kind)}</span>
        <span class="mission-task-copy">
          <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.title, item.id))}</strong>
          <span>${escapeHTML(repo)} · ${escapeHTML(schedule)}</span>
          <em>${escapeHTML(summary)}</em>
        </span>
        <span class="mission-task-action">
          <span>${escapeHTML(taskPrimaryActionLabel(item))} ›</span>
          ${renderStatePill(taskStatusTone(defaultString(item.raw_status, item.status)), taskStatusLabel(defaultString(item.raw_status, item.status)))}
          ${item.run_id ? `<small>${escapeHTML(item.run_id)}</small>` : ""}
        </span>
      </button>
    `;
  }

  function renderTaskFeed(items) {
    const groups = TASK_STATUS_GROUPS.map((group) => ({
      ...group,
      items: taskItemsForStatus(items, group.id),
    })).filter((group) => group.items.length);
    if (!groups.length) {
      return `
        <section class="mission-empty-state">
          <h3>No tasks match these filters.</h3>
          <p>Clear filters or schedule a new task from the toolbar.</p>
        </section>
      `;
    }
    return groups.map((group) => `
      <section class="mission-task-group">
        <div class="mission-task-group-head">
          <div>
            <h3>${escapeHTML(group.title)}</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(group.copy)}</p>
          </div>
          <span>${group.items.length}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="mission-task-rows">${group.items.map(renderTaskFeedRow).join("")}</div>
      </section>
    `).join("");
  }

  function taskDetailSourceMarkup(detail) {
    if (!detail || !detail.summary) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">Task detail is unavailable.</div>';
    }
    if (detail.work_run) {
      const run = detail.work_run;
      return `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Phase</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(run.summary.current_phase, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Backend</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(run.summary.backend, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Target</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(run.summary.target_url, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Next Action</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(run.next_action, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
      `;
    }
    if (detail.work_item && detail.work_item.item) {
      const item = detail.work_item.item;
      return `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Source</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.source, "-"))}/${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.source_kind, "-"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Target</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.target_url, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Draft</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.latest_draft && item.latest_draft.summary, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Body</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.body, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
      `;
    }
    if (detail.investigation && detail.investigation.summary) {
      const item = detail.investigation.summary;
      return `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Query</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.query, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Result</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.overall_status, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Proofs</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.proof_count, 0))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Validator</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(detail.investigation.latest_validator_result && detail.investigation.latest_validator_result.accepted ? "accepted" : "", detail.investigation.latest_validator_result ? "rejected" : "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
      `;
    }
    if (detail.planned_item) {
      const item = detail.planned_item;
      return `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Findings Handling</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.findings_handling, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          ${item.investigation_query ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Investigation Query</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(item.investigation_query)}</p></article>` : ""}
          ${item.scout_role ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Scout Role</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(item.scout_role)}</p></article>` : ""}
          ${item.last_error ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Last Error</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(item.last_error)}</p></article>` : ""}
        </div>
      `;
    }
    if (detail.issue) {
      const item = detail.issue;
      return `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Issue</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.source_url, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Triage</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.triage_rationale, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Blocked Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.blocked_reason, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Priority Source</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.priority_source, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
      `;
    }
    if (detail.scout_job) {
      const item = detail.scout_job;
      return `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Role</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.role, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Summary</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.summary, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Evidence</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.evidence, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Last Error</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.last_error, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
      `;
    }
    if (detail.service_task) {
      const item = detail.service_task;
      return `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Kind</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.kind, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Queue</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.queue, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Last Error</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.last_error, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Result</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.result_summary, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
      `;
    }
    return '<div class="status-pill">No source detail is available for this task.</div>';
  }

  function renderMarkdownInline(text) {
    let rendered = escapeHTML(defaultString(text, ""));
    rendered = rendered.replace(/\*\*(.+?)\*\*/g, "<strong>$1</strong>");
    rendered = rendered.replace(/\*(.+?)\*/g, "<em>$1</em>");
    rendered = rendered.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, "<code>$1</code>");
    return rendered;
  }

  function renderMarkdownDocument(markdown) {
    const source = String(markdown || "").replace(/\r\n/g, "\n").trim();
    if (!source) return '<div class="status-pill">No description provided.</div>';

    const lines = source.split("\n");
    const blocks = [];
    let paragraph = [];
    let listItems = [];

    const flushParagraph = () => {
      if (!paragraph.length) return;
      const text = paragraph.join(" ").trim();
      if (text) {
        blocks.push(`<p>${renderMarkdownInline(text)}</p>`);
      }
      paragraph = [];
    };

    const flushList = () => {
      if (!listItems.length) return;
      blocks.push(`<ul>${listItems.map((item) => `<li>${renderMarkdownInline(item)}</li>`).join("")}</ul>`);
      listItems = [];
    };

    for (const rawLine of lines) {
      const line = rawLine.trimEnd();
      const trimmed = line.trim();
      if (!trimmed) {
        flushParagraph();
        flushList();
        continue;
      }

      const heading = trimmed.match(/^(#{1,6})\s+(.*)$/);
      if (heading) {
        flushParagraph();
        flushList();
        const level = heading[1].length;
        blocks.push(`<h${level}>${renderMarkdownInline(heading[2].trim())}</h${level}>`);
        continue;
      }

      const bullet = trimmed.match(/^[-*]\s+(.*)$/);
      if (bullet) {
        flushParagraph();
        listItems.push(bullet[1].trim());
        continue;
      }

      flushList();
      paragraph.push(trimmed);
    }

    flushParagraph();
    flushList();
    return blocks.join("");
  }

  function taskDetailContentMarkup(detail) {
    if (!detail || !detail.summary) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">Task detail is unavailable.</div>';
    }
    const summary = detail.summary;
    if (summary.kind === "planned_item" && detail.planned_item) {
      const item = detail.planned_item;
      const sourceMarkup = taskDetailSourceMarkup(detail);
      const descriptionMarkup = renderMarkdownDocument(defaultString(item.description, ""));
      return `
        ${sourceMarkup}
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="task-detail-markdown">${descriptionMarkup}</div>
        </div>
      `;
    }
    return `
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Task Detail</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.summary, summary.description || "No task summary recorded."))}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${taskDetailSourceMarkup(detail)}
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function taskDetailStartedAt(detail) {
    if (detail && detail.related_run && detail.related_run.started_at) {
      return detail.related_run.started_at;
    }
    if (detail && detail.work_run && detail.work_run.started_at) {
      return detail.work_run.started_at;
    }
    if (detail && detail.summary && detail.summary.created_at) {
      return detail.summary.created_at;
    }
    if (detail && detail.investigation && detail.investigation.summary && detail.investigation.summary.created_at) {
      return detail.investigation.summary.created_at;
    }
    return "";
  }

  function taskDetailTokens(detail) {
    if (detail && detail.related_run && detail.related_run.has_token_usage) {
      return {
        total: Number(detail.related_run.total_tokens || 0),
        sessions: Number(detail.related_run.sessions_accounted || 0),
      };
    }
    if (detail && detail.work_run && detail.work_run.has_token_usage) {
      return {
        total: Number(detail.work_run.total_tokens || 0),
        sessions: Number(detail.work_run.sessions_accounted || 0),
      };
    }
    return null;
  }

  function syncTaskDetailModalState() {
    const taskID = defaultString(state.investigations.selectedRunID, "");
    if (state.currentView !== "investigations" || !taskID) {
      if (state.taskDetailModal && state.taskDetailModal.isOpen()) {
        state.taskDetailModal.close();
      }
      return;
    }
    initTaskDetailModal();
    renderTaskDetailModal();
    if (!state.taskDetailModal.isOpen()) {
      state.taskDetailModal.open();
    }
    const currentDetailID = defaultString(state.investigations.detail && state.investigations.detail.summary && state.investigations.detail.summary.id, "");
    if (currentDetailID === taskID || state.investigations.detailLoading) {
      return;
    }
    state.investigations.detail = null;
    state.investigations.detailLoading = true;
    renderTaskDetailModal();
    loadInvestigationDetail(taskID, { silent: true });
  }

  function taskDetailOpenButtons(detail, summary) {
    if (!detail || !summary) return [];
    const buttons = [];
    const runID = defaultString(summary.run_id, defaultString(detail.related_run && detail.related_run.summary && detail.related_run.summary.run_id, ""));
    if (runID) {
      buttons.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-open-job="${escapeHTML(runID)}">Open Job</button>`);
    }
    if (summary.kind === "work_item" && detail.work_item && detail.work_item.item) {
      buttons.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-show="${escapeHTML(detail.work_item.item.id)}">Open Draft</button>`);
    }
    return buttons;
  }

  function taskDetailActionButtons(detail, summary) {
    if (!detail || !summary) return [];
    const actions = [];
    if (summary.kind === "work_run" && detail.work_run && detail.work_run.summary) {
      const runID = defaultString(detail.work_run.summary.run_id, "");
      if (!runID) return actions;
      if (detail.work_run.rerun_allowed) {
        actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-run-rerun="${escapeHTML(runID)}">Re-run</button>`);
      }
      actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-run-drop="${escapeHTML(runID)}">Drop Run</button>`);
      return actions;
    }
    if (summary.kind === "planned_item" && detail.planned_item && ["queued", "failed"].includes(defaultString(detail.planned_item.state, ""))) {
      actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-task-action="run-now" data-task-id="${escapeHTML(summary.id)}">Run Now</button>`);
      actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-action="dismiss" data-task-id="${escapeHTML(summary.id)}">Dismiss</button>`);
      return actions;
    }
    if (summary.kind === "work_item" && detail.work_item && detail.work_item.item) {
      const item = detail.work_item.item;
      const status = defaultString(item.status, "");
      if (["queued", "failed", "needs_routing"].includes(status)) {
        actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-task-action="run-now" data-task-id="${escapeHTML(summary.id)}">Run Now</button>`);
      }
      if (status === "paused") {
        actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-action="retry" data-task-id="${escapeHTML(summary.id)}">Retry</button>`);
      }
      if (!item.hidden && !["submitted", "dropped", "silenced"].includes(status)) {
        actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-action="dismiss" data-task-id="${escapeHTML(summary.id)}">Dismiss</button>`);
      }
      return actions;
    }
    if (summary.kind === "scout_job" && detail.scout_job) {
      if (detail.scout_job.status === "failed" || detail.scout_job.status === "dismissed") {
        actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-action="retry" data-task-id="${escapeHTML(summary.id)}">Retry</button>`);
      }
      if (detail.scout_job.status === "queued" || detail.scout_job.status === "failed") {
        actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-action="dismiss" data-task-id="${escapeHTML(summary.id)}">Dismiss</button>`);
      }
      return actions;
    }
    return actions;
  }

  function renderTaskDetailActionMenu(detail, summary) {
    const actions = taskDetailActionButtons(detail, summary);
    if (!actions.length) return "";
    return `
      <details class="drawer-action-menu">
        <summary class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary drawer-action-menu-summary">Actions</summary>
        <div class="drawer-action-menu-body">
          ${actions.join("")}
        </div>
      </details>
    `;
  }

  function renderTaskDetailModal() {
    const host = document.getElementById("task-detail-modal-content");
    if (!host) return;
    const detail = state.investigations.detail;
    if (!state.investigations.selectedRunID) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="log-empty">Choose a task to inspect it.</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (state.investigations.detailLoading && !detail) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="log-empty">Loading task detail...</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (state.investigations.error && !detail) {
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="log-empty">${escapeHTML(state.investigations.error)}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    if (!detail || !detail.summary) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="log-empty">Task detail is unavailable.</div>';
      return;
    }
    const summary = detail.summary;
    const startedAt = taskDetailStartedAt(detail);
    const tokenUsage = taskDetailTokens(detail);
    const taskReference = defaultString(summary.id, "Not available");
    const tokenValue = tokenUsage
      ? `${formatTokenCompact(tokenUsage.total)}${tokenUsage.sessions > 0 ? ` · ${tokenUsage.sessions} session${tokenUsage.sessions === 1 ? "" : "s"}` : ""}`
      : "Not available";
    const actionButtons = taskDetailOpenButtons(detail, summary);
    const actionMenuMarkup = renderTaskDetailActionMenu(detail, summary);
    const plannedItem = summary.kind === "planned_item" ? detail.planned_item : null;
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.kind, "task").replace(/_/g, " "))}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.title, summary.id))}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.repo_slug, "Workspace"))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Status</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePill(taskStatusTone(summary.status), taskStatusLabel(defaultString(summary.status, "queued")))}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Priority</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.priority_label, "P3"))}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Updated</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(summary.updated_at))}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Task Start</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(startedAt ? formatDateTime(startedAt) : "", "Not started"))}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Scheduled</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(summary.schedule_at) : "", "Now"))}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Token Spend</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(tokenValue)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Reference</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(taskReference)}</span>
          </div>
          ${plannedItem ? `
            <div class="drawer-summary-card">
              <span class="drawer-label">Launch Kind</span>
              <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(plannedItem.launch_kind, "(none)"))}</span>
            </div>
          ` : ""}
          ${plannedItem && plannedItem.work_type ? `
            <div class="drawer-summary-card">
              <span class="drawer-label">Work Type</span>
              <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(plannedItem.work_type))}</span>
            </div>
          ` : ""}
        </div>
      </div>
      ${actionButtons.length || actionMenuMarkup ? `<div class="drawer-toolbar">${actionButtons.join("")}${actionMenuMarkup}</div>` : ""}
      ${taskDetailContentMarkup(detail)}
    `;
  }

  function initTaskDetailModal() {
    if (state.taskDetailModal) return;
    state.taskDetailModal = Teryx.modal({
      title: "Task Detail",
      size: "xl",
      maximizable: true,
      width: "min(1120px, 92vw)",
      content: '<div id="task-detail-modal-content" class="drawer-shell"></div>',
      onClose() {
        state.investigations.selectedRunID = "";
        state.investigations.detail = null;
        state.investigations.detailLoading = false;
        syncHashState();
        if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
          renderInvestigationsPage();
        } else {
          renderAppPreservingDraftFocus();
        }
        renderTaskDetailModal();
      },
    });
  }

  function openTaskDetailModal(taskID) {
    state.investigations.selectedRunID = taskID;
    syncHashState();
    if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
      renderInvestigationsPage();
    }
    syncTaskDetailModalState();
  }

  function renderTaskScheduleModal() {
    const host = document.getElementById("task-schedule-modal-content");
    if (!host) return;
    const repos = sortedRepos();
    const composerRepo = selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary();
    const selectedTemplate = selectedTaskTemplate();
    const runMode = defaultString(state.taskComposer.runMode, state.taskComposer.scheduleAt ? "later" : "now");
    const scoutPromptPreview = taskTemplateScoutPromptPreview(selectedTemplate);
    const descriptionValue = scoutPromptPreview || state.taskComposer.description;
    const canSavePreset = taskComposerCanSavePreset(selectedTemplate);
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="mission-schedule-modal">
        <div class="config-grid task-composer-controls">
          <label class="config-field">
            <span class="config-label">Repo</span>
            <select id="task-composer-repo">
              ${repos.map((entry) => `<option value="${escapeHTML(entry.repo_slug)}" ${composerRepo && composerRepo.repo_slug === entry.repo_slug ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(entry.repo_slug)}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="config-field">
            <span class="config-label">Preset</span>
            <select id="task-composer-template">
              ${(state.investigations.templates || []).map((template) => `<option value="${escapeHTML(template.id)}" ${selectedTemplate && selectedTemplate.id === template.id ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(template.name)}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="config-field">
            <span class="config-label">Priority</span>
            <select id="task-composer-priority">
              ${[0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((priority) => `<option value="${priority}" ${String(state.taskComposer.priority) === String(priority) ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(`P${priority}`)}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="config-field">
            <span class="config-label">Run</span>
            <select id="task-composer-run-mode">
              <option value="now" ${runMode === "now" ? "selected" : ""}>Now</option>
              <option value="later" ${runMode === "later" ? "selected" : ""}>Later</option>
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="config-field ${runMode === "later" ? "" : "task-run-at-hidden"}">
            <span class="config-label">Run At</span>
            <input id="task-composer-schedule" type="datetime-local" value="${escapeHTML(state.taskComposer.scheduleAt)}" />
          </label>
        </div>
        <label class="config-field config-field-wide task-composer-description-field">
          <span class="config-label">Description</span>
          <textarea id="task-composer-description" rows="6" placeholder="Investigate why the task repo filter sometimes appears empty, then patch the UI if needed." ${scoutPromptPreview ? "readonly" : ""}>${escapeHTML(descriptionValue)}</textarea>
        </label>
        <div class="drawer-toolbar">
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-schedule-close="true">Cancel</button>
          <button id="task-save-template-button" class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" ${state.taskComposer.savingTemplate || !composerRepo || !canSavePreset ? "disabled" : ""}>${state.taskComposer.savingTemplate ? "Saving..." : "Save As Preset"}</button>
          <button id="task-schedule-button" class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" ${state.taskComposer.creating || !composerRepo ? "disabled" : ""}>${state.taskComposer.creating ? "Scheduling..." : "Schedule Task"}</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function initTaskScheduleModal() {
    if (state.taskScheduleModal) return;
    state.taskScheduleModal = Teryx.modal({
      title: "Schedule Task",
      size: "lg",
      width: "min(760px, 92vw)",
      bodyClass: "mission-schedule-modal-body",
      content: '<div id="task-schedule-modal-content" class="drawer-shell"></div>',
    });
  }

  function openTaskScheduleModal() {
    initTaskScheduleModal();
    selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary();
    renderTaskScheduleModal();
    state.taskScheduleModal.open();
  }

  function submitTaskSchedule() {
    const repo = selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary();
    if (!repo) {
      toast("warning", "No repo selected", "Pick a repo before scheduling a task.");
      return;
    }
    const selectedTemplate = selectedTaskTemplate();
    const scoutPromptPreview = taskTemplateScoutPromptPreview(selectedTemplate);
    const description = scoutPromptPreview ? "" : String(state.taskComposer.description || "").trim();
    if (!description && !scoutPromptPreview) {
      toast("warning", "Missing description", "Describe the task first.");
      return;
    }
    const priority = Number.parseInt(String(state.taskComposer.priority || "3"), 10);
    const scheduleAt = fromDateTimeLocal(state.taskComposer.scheduleAt);
    const idempotencyKey = defaultString(state.taskComposer.idempotencyKey, nextTaskComposerIdempotencyKey());
    state.taskComposer.idempotencyKey = idempotencyKey;
    state.taskComposer.creating = true;
    renderTaskScheduleModal();
    renderInvestigationsPage();
    api("/api/v1/tasks", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Idempotency-Key": idempotencyKey },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        repo_slug: repo.repo_slug,
        description,
        schedule_at: scheduleAt,
        priority,
        template_id: defaultString(state.taskComposer.templateID, "template:custom"),
        idempotency_key: idempotencyKey,
      }),
    }).then((response) => {
      state.taskComposer.creating = false;
      state.taskComposer.description = "";
      state.taskComposer.scheduleAt = "";
      state.taskComposer.runMode = "now";
      state.taskComposer.priority = "3";
      state.taskComposer.idempotencyKey = nextTaskComposerIdempotencyKey();
      if (state.taskScheduleModal && state.taskScheduleModal.isOpen()) {
        state.taskScheduleModal.close();
      }
      if (response.state) {
        mergeRepoState(response.state);
      } else {
        load();
      }
      loadApprovals({ silent: true });
      loadInvestigations({ silent: true });
      toast("success", "Task scheduled", response.planned_item && response.planned_item.title || (scoutPromptPreview ? defaultString(selectedTemplate && selectedTemplate.name, "Scout") : description));
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.taskComposer.creating = false;
      renderTaskScheduleModal();
      renderInvestigationsPage();
      toast("danger", "Task scheduling failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function saveTaskTemplateFromComposer() {
    const repo = selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary();
    const description = String(state.taskComposer.description || "").trim();
    const selectedTemplate = selectedTaskTemplate();
    if (!taskComposerCanSavePreset(selectedTemplate)) {
      toast("warning", "Preset selected", "Switch to Custom task before saving a new preset.");
      return;
    }
    if (!repo || !description) {
      toast("warning", "Missing preset description", "Write the preset description first.");
      return;
    }
    state.taskComposer.savingTemplate = true;
    renderTaskScheduleModal();
    renderInvestigationsPage();
    api("/api/v1/tasks/templates", {
      method: "POST",
      body: JSON.stringify({
        repo_slug: repo.repo_slug,
        description,
        base_template_id: defaultString(state.taskComposer.templateID, "template:custom"),
      }),
    }).then((payload) => {
      state.taskComposer.savingTemplate = false;
      toast("success", "Preset saved", payload.template && payload.template.name || "Custom preset");
      loadTaskTemplates({ silent: true });
      renderTaskScheduleModal();
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.taskComposer.savingTemplate = false;
      renderTaskScheduleModal();
      renderInvestigationsPage();
      toast("danger", "Preset save failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function renderInvestigationsPage() {
    const items = filteredInvestigations();
    const composerRepo = selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary();
    const composerRepoSlug = composerRepo ? composerRepo.repo_slug : "";
    if ((!state.investigations.templatesLoaded || state.investigations.templatesRepoSlug !== composerRepoSlug) && !state.investigations.templatesLoading) {
      loadTaskTemplates({ silent: true });
    }
    ensureBodyStructure(`investigations:${defaultString(state.selectedRepo, "all")}:${sortedRepos().length}`, `
      <section class="mission-control-shell">
        <div id="mission-toolbar-host"></div>
        <div id="mission-status-strip" class="mission-status-strip"></div>
        <section id="mission-feed" class="mission-feed"></section>
      </section>
    `);
    const toolbarHost = document.getElementById("mission-toolbar-host");
    if (toolbarHost) toolbarHost.innerHTML = renderTaskToolbar(state.investigations.items || []);
    const statusHost = document.getElementById("mission-status-strip");
    if (statusHost) statusHost.innerHTML = taskStatusStrip(state.investigations.items || []);
    const feedHost = document.getElementById("mission-feed");
    if (feedHost) feedHost.innerHTML = renderTaskFeed(items);
    renderTaskScheduleModal();
  }

  function renderWorkPage() {
    const runs = filteredWorkRuns();
    ensureBodyStructure(`work:${defaultString(state.selectedRepo, "all")}`, `
      <section class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Work Runs</h3>
            <p>Active and recent runs across local and GitHub-backed workflows.</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${buildFilterToolbar("work", {
          placeholder: "Search run id, repo, target URL, phase, or backend",
          kindOptions: [
            { value: "all", label: "All kinds" },
            { value: "github", label: "GitHub" },
            { value: "local", label: "Local" },
          ],
        })}
        <div id="work-runs-grid"></div>
      </section>
    `);
    renderGrid("work-runs-grid", workRunColumns(true), workRunRows(runs, true), {
      maxHeight: "620px",
      emptyMessage: "No work runs have been indexed yet.",
      rowSelect(row) {
        return {
          kind: "run",
          value: row.run_id,
          selected: state.logSelection.runID === row.run_id,
        };
      },
    });
  }

  function renderFeedbackPage() {
    const items = filteredFeedbackItems();
    ensureBodyStructure(`feedback:${state.feedbackTab}:${defaultString(state.selectedRepo, "all")}`, `
      <section class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>${state.feedbackTab === "reviews" ? "Review Drafts" : "Reply Drafts"}</h3>
            <p>${state.feedbackTab === "reviews" ? "Drafted PR reviews, inline comments, and review decisions." : "Drafted replies for GitHub review threads and issue comments."}</p>
          </div>
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" id="feedback-sync-button">Sync GitHub</button>
        </div>
        ${buildFilterToolbar("feedback", { placeholder: "Search subject, draft summary, target URL, or thread path" })}
        <div id="feedback-grid"></div>
      </section>
    `);
    renderGrid("feedback-grid", [
      { field: "repo_slug", label: "Repo", render: (row) => `<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(defaultString(row.repo_slug, "Standalone"))}</span>` },
      { field: "subject", label: "Subject" },
      { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePillWithPause(row.attention_state, row.status, row.pause_until, row.pause_reason) },
      { field: "draft_summary", label: "Draft" },
      { field: "review_event", label: state.feedbackTab === "reviews" ? "Event" : "Context" },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated", render: (row) => `<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(row.updated_at))}</span>` },
    ], items, {
      maxHeight: "620px",
      emptyMessage: state.feedback.loading ? "Loading feedback..." : defaultString(state.feedback.error, `No ${state.feedbackTab} are available.`),
      rowSelect(row) {
        return {
          kind: "work-item",
          value: row.id,
          selected: state.workItemSelection.itemID === row.id,
        };
      },
    });
  }

  function renderApprovalsPage() {
    const items = filteredApprovalItems();
    const selected = selectedApprovalItem(items);
    ensureBodyStructure(`approvals:${defaultString(state.selectedRepo, "all")}`, `
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Approval Queue</h3>
              <p>Human-gate work runs, draft submissions, and launchable planned work.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          ${buildFilterToolbar("approvals", {
            placeholder: "Search subject, reason, target URL, or next action",
            kindOptions: [
              { value: "all", label: "All kinds" },
              { value: "work_run", label: "Work runs" },
              { value: "work_item", label: "Drafts" },
              { value: "planned_item", label: "Planned launches" },
            ],
          })}
          <div id="approvals-grid"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface detail-surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Approval Detail</h3>
              <p>Exact next safe action for the selected approval item.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="approvals-detail"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
    `);
    renderGrid("approvals-grid", [
      { field: "kind", label: "Kind" },
      { field: "repo_slug", label: "Repo", render: (row) => `<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(defaultString(row.repo_slug, "Standalone"))}</span>` },
      { field: "subject", label: "Subject" },
      { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePill(row.attention_state, row.status) },
      { field: "reason", label: "Reason" },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated", render: (row) => `<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(row.updated_at))}</span>` },
      {
        field: "id",
        label: "Action",
        action: true,
        render(row) {
          if (row.kind === "work_item") {
            return `
              <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-work-item-submit="${escapeHTML(row.item_id)}">Approve</button>
              ${renderApprovalDropButton(row, "tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button")}
            `;
          }
          if (row.kind === "planned_item") {
            return `
              <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-approval-launch-planned="${escapeHTML(row.planned_item_id)}">Approve</button>
              ${renderApprovalDropButton(row, "tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button")}
            `;
          }
          if (row.kind === "scout_job") {
            return `
              <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-approval-retry-scout="${escapeHTML(row.scout_job_id)}">Retry</button>
              ${renderApprovalDropButton(row, "tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button")}
            `;
          }
          if (row.kind === "work_run") {
            const actions = [];
            if (row.external_url && row.action_kind === "review_on_github") {
              actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-open-external="${escapeHTML(row.external_url)}">Review</button>`);
            }
            if (row.run_id && row.action_kind === "resolve_run") {
              actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-run-resolve="${escapeHTML(row.run_id)}">Resolve</button>`);
            }
            if (row.run_id && row.action_kind === "sync_run") {
              actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-run-sync="${escapeHTML(row.run_id)}">Refresh</button>`);
            }
            const dropButton = renderApprovalDropButton(row, "tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button");
            if (dropButton) {
              actions.push(dropButton);
            }
            return actions.join("");
          }
          return '<span class="data-value-text">Select row</span>';
        },
      },
    ], items, {
      maxHeight: "620px",
      emptyMessage: state.approvals.loading ? "Loading approvals..." : defaultString(state.approvals.error, "No approvals are pending."),
      rowSelect(row) {
        return {
          kind: "approval",
          value: row.id,
          selected: selected ? selected.id === row.id : false,
        };
      },
    });
    const host = document.getElementById("approvals-detail");
    if (!host) return;
    if (state.approvals.error && !selected) {
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.approvals.error)}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    if (!selected) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">No approval item selected.</div>';
      return;
    }
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.repo_slug, "Standalone"))} · ${escapeHTML(selected.kind)}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(selected.subject)}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.reason, "(none)"))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Status</span><span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePill(selected.attention_state, selected.status)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Next Action</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.next_action, "(none)"))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Action Kind</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.action_kind, "(none)"))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Updated</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(selected.updated_at))}</span></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.reason, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Next Step</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.next_action, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">External URL</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(selected.external_url, defaultString(selected.target_url, "(none)")))}</p></article>
      </div>
      <div class="drawer-toolbar">
        ${renderApprovalActionButton(selected)}
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function renderApprovalDropButton(item, className = "tx-btn tx-btn-secondary") {
    if (!item) return "";
    let reference = "";
    switch (item.kind) {
      case "work_run":
        reference = item.run_id;
        break;
      case "work_item":
        reference = item.item_id;
        break;
      case "planned_item":
        reference = item.planned_item_id;
        break;
      case "scout_job":
        reference = item.scout_job_id;
        break;
      default:
        return "";
    }
    if (!reference) return "";
    return `<button class="${escapeHTML(className)}" type="button" data-approval-drop-kind="${escapeHTML(item.kind)}" data-approval-drop-id="${escapeHTML(reference)}" data-approval-drop-repo="${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.repo_slug, ""))}" data-approval-drop-subject="${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.subject, ""))}">Drop</button>`;
  }

  function renderApprovalActionButton(item) {
    if (!item) return '<span class="data-value-text">No action</span>';
    if (item.action_kind === "approve_work_item" && item.item_id) {
      return `
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-work-item-submit="${escapeHTML(item.item_id)}">Approve Draft</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-show="${escapeHTML(item.item_id)}">Open Draft</button>
        ${renderApprovalDropButton(item)}
      `;
    }
    if (item.action_kind === "approve_planned_item" && item.planned_item_id) {
      return `
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-approval-launch-planned="${escapeHTML(item.planned_item_id)}">Approve Launch</button>
        ${renderApprovalDropButton(item)}
      `;
    }
    if (item.action_kind === "retry_scout_job" && item.scout_job_id) {
      return `
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-approval-retry-scout="${escapeHTML(item.scout_job_id)}">Retry Scout Job</button>
        ${renderApprovalDropButton(item)}
      `;
    }
    if (item.action_kind === "review_on_github" && item.external_url) {
      return `
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-open-external="${escapeHTML(item.external_url)}">Review on GitHub</button>
        ${item.run_id ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-run-sync="${escapeHTML(item.run_id)}">Refresh Status</button>` : ""}
        ${renderApprovalDropButton(item)}
      `;
    }
    if (item.action_kind === "resolve_run" && item.run_id) {
      return `
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-run-resolve="${escapeHTML(item.run_id)}">Resolve Run</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-log-run-id="${escapeHTML(item.run_id)}">Open Run</button>
        ${renderApprovalDropButton(item)}
      `;
    }
    if (item.action_kind === "sync_run" && item.run_id) {
      return `
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-run-sync="${escapeHTML(item.run_id)}">Refresh Status</button>
        ${renderApprovalDropButton(item)}
      `;
    }
    if (item.action_kind === "open_run" && item.run_id) {
      return `
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-log-run-id="${escapeHTML(item.run_id)}">Open Run</button>
        ${renderApprovalDropButton(item)}
      `;
    }
    return '<span class="data-value-text">No action</span>';
  }

  function rerunWorkRunFromUI(runID) {
    requestConfirmation({
      title: "Re-run work?",
      message: `Start a fresh local work run from ${runID} using its stored task input and runtime settings.`,
      confirmLabel: "Re-run",
      onConfirm() {
        api(`/api/v1/work/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runID)}/rerun`, {
          method: "POST",
        }).then((payload) => {
          const nextRunID = defaultString(payload.run_id, defaultString(payload.detail && payload.detail.summary && payload.detail.summary.run_id, ""));
          load();
          loadApprovals({ silent: true });
          loadInvestigations({ silent: true });
          if (nextRunID) {
            openLogDrawer(nextRunID);
          }
          toast("success", "Run re-started", defaultString(nextRunID, runID));
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Run re-start failed", error.message);
        });
      },
    });
  }

  function dropApprovalItem(kind, reference, repoSlug, subject) {
