    const approvalLabel = defaultString(subject, reference);
    switch (kind) {
      case "work_run":
        requestConfirmation({
          title: "Drop approval item?",
          message: `Remove run ${reference} from the active workspace queue.`,
          confirmLabel: "Drop",
          tone: "danger",
          onConfirm() {
            api(`/api/v1/work/runs/${encodeURIComponent(reference)}/drop`, {
              method: "POST",
            }).then(() => {
              if (state.logSelection.runID === reference && state.logDrawer) {
                state.logDrawer.close();
              }
              load();
              loadApprovals({ silent: true });
              toast("success", "Approval dropped", approvalLabel);
            }).catch((error) => {
              toast("danger", "Drop failed", error.message);
            });
          },
        });
        return;
      case "work_item":
        requestConfirmation({
          title: "Drop approval item?",
          message: `Hide work item ${reference} from the active queue.`,
          confirmLabel: "Drop",
          tone: "danger",
          onConfirm() {
            api(`/api/v1/work-items/${encodeURIComponent(reference)}/drop`, {
              method: "POST",
            }).then(() => {
              load();
              loadApprovals({ silent: true });
              toast("success", "Approval dropped", approvalLabel);
            }).catch((error) => {
              toast("danger", "Drop failed", error.message);
            });
          },
        });
        return;
      case "planned_item":
        requestConfirmation({
          title: "Drop approval item?",
          message: `Remove planned item ${approvalLabel} from the approval queue.`,
          confirmLabel: "Drop",
          tone: "danger",
          onConfirm() {
            api(`/api/v1/planned-items/${encodeURIComponent(reference)}`, {
              method: "DELETE",
            }).then((payload) => {
              if (payload.state) {
                mergeRepoState(payload.state);
              }
              load();
              loadApprovals({ silent: true });
              toast("success", "Approval dropped", defaultString(payload.removed_item && payload.removed_item.title, approvalLabel));
            }).catch((error) => {
              toast("danger", "Drop failed", error.message);
            });
          },
        });
        return;
      case "scout_job":
        if (!repoSlug) {
          toast("warning", "Drop unavailable", "Scout job is missing repo context.");
          return;
        }
        requestConfirmation({
          title: "Drop approval item?",
          message: `Dismiss scout job ${approvalLabel} from the approval queue.`,
          confirmLabel: "Drop",
          tone: "danger",
          onConfirm() {
            mutateScoutItem(repoSlug, reference, "dismiss").then(() => {
              load();
              loadApprovals({ silent: true });
              toast("success", "Approval dropped", approvalLabel);
            }).catch(() => {});
          },
        });
        return;
      default:
        toast("warning", "Drop unavailable", `Approval kind ${defaultString(kind, "(unknown)")} cannot be dropped.`);
    }
  }

  function issueRows(repo) {
    if (!repo || !repo.state) return [];
    return Object.values(repo.state.issues || {}).sort((left, right) => {
      const leftPriority = left.manual_priority_updated_at ? left.manual_priority : (left.priority ?? 5);
      const rightPriority = right.manual_priority_updated_at ? right.manual_priority : (right.priority ?? 5);
      if (leftPriority !== rightPriority) return leftPriority - rightPriority;
      return left.source_number - right.source_number;
    }).map((issue) => ({
      source_number: issue.source_number,
      title: issue.title,
      work_type: workTypeLabel(issue.work_type),
      priority: issue.manual_priority_updated_at ? `P${issue.manual_priority}` : `P${issue.priority ?? 5}`,
      status: defaultString(issue.status, "-"),
      triage: defaultString(issue.triage_status, "-"),
      schedule_at: issue.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(issue.schedule_at) : "Not scheduled",
      deferred_reason: defaultString(issue.deferred_reason, "-"),
    }));
  }

  function serviceTaskRows(repo) {
    if (!repo || !repo.state) return [];
    return Object.values(repo.state.service_tasks || {}).map((task) => ({
      kind: defaultString(task.kind, "-"),
      status: defaultString(task.status, "-"),
      issue_key: defaultString(task.issue_key || task.planned_item_id, "-"),
      attempts: task.attempts || 0,
      updated_at: task.updated_at ? formatDateTime(task.updated_at) : "No update yet",
      result: defaultString(task.result_summary || task.last_error, "-"),
    }));
  }

  function plannedItemRows(repo) {
    if (!repo || !repo.state) return [];
    return Object.values(repo.state.planned_items || {}).sort((left, right) => {
      return timestamp(right.updated_at) - timestamp(left.updated_at);
    }).map((item) => ({
      id: item.id,
      title: item.title,
      work_type: workTypeLabel(item.work_type),
      launch_kind: defaultString(item.launch_kind, "-"),
      priority: `P${item.priority}`,
      schedule_at: item.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(item.schedule_at) : "Not scheduled",
      state: defaultString(item.state, "-"),
      launch_result: defaultString(item.launch_result || item.last_error, "-"),
    }));
  }

  function repoSchedulerSearchRows(repo) {
    ensureRepoScheduler(repo);
    return (state.repoScheduler.results || []).map((item) => ({
      id: item.id,
      number: item.number,
      title: item.title,
      labels: Array.isArray(item.labels) && item.labels.length ? item.labels.join(", ") : "-",
      work_type: workTypeLabel(item.work_type),
      priority_label: defaultString(item.priority_label, `P${item.priority ?? 3}`),
      updated_at: item.updated_at ? formatDateTime(item.updated_at) : "No update yet",
      target_url: defaultString(item.target_url, ""),
      action_label: item.scheduled ? "Open" : "Add",
      planned_item_id: defaultString(item.planned_item_id, ""),
      scheduled: Boolean(item.scheduled),
      schedule_at: defaultString(item.schedule_at, ""),
    }));
  }

  function renderRepoSchedulerSearchResults(repo) {
    const host = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-search-results");
    if (!host) return;
    host.innerHTML = '<div id="repo-scheduler-search-grid"></div>';
    if (state.repoScheduler.searching) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Searching GitHub issues...</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (state.repoScheduler.error) {
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.repoScheduler.error)}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    const rows = repoSchedulerSearchRows(repo);
    renderGrid("repo-scheduler-search-grid", [
      { field: "number", label: "#" },
      { field: "title", label: "Title" },
      { field: "labels", label: "Labels" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
      { field: "priority_label", label: "Priority" },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
      {
        field: "action_label",
        label: "Action",
        render: (row) => row.scheduled
          ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scheduler-open="${escapeHTML(row.planned_item_id)}">Open</button>`
          : `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scheduler-add="${escapeHTML(row.id)}">Add</button>`,
      },
    ], rows, {
      maxHeight: "420px",
      emptyMessage: state.repoScheduler.effectiveQuery
        ? "No open GitHub issues matched this query."
        : "Search the current repo with GitHub issue qualifiers like label:, assignee:, author:, milestone:, or sort:updated-desc.",
    });
  }

  function renderRepoSchedulerSearchPanel(repo) {
    const host = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-search-panel");
    if (!host) return;
    renderWithPreservedDraftFocus(() => {
      const draftScope = repoSchedulerSearchDraftScope(repo);
      host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="surface-head">
        <div>
          <h3>Search GitHub Issues</h3>
          <p>Scoped to ${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}. Use GitHub issue qualifiers like label:, assignee:, author:, milestone:, or sort:updated-desc.</p>
        </div>
        <span class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(defaultString(repo.issue_pick_mode, "manual"))}</span>
      </div>
      <form id="repo-scheduler-search-form" class="scheduler-search-form" data-draft-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}">
        <label class="selector config-field-wide">
          <span>GitHub Issue Search</span>
          <input id="repo-scheduler-search-query" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(state.repoScheduler.query)}" placeholder="label:bug assignee:octocat sort:updated-desc" />
        </label>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="submit" ${state.repoScheduler.searching ? "disabled" : ""}>${escapeHTML(state.repoScheduler.searching ? "Searching..." : "Search")}</button>
      </form>
      ${state.repoScheduler.effectiveQuery ? `<p class="queue-copy">Effective query: ${escapeHTML(state.repoScheduler.effectiveQuery)}</p>` : ""}
      <div id="repo-scheduler-search-results"></div>
    `;
      renderRepoSchedulerSearchResults(repo);
      restoreDraftScope(draftScope, document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-search-form"));
    }, host);
  }

  function renderRepoSchedulerBoard(repo) {
    const host = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-board");
    if (!host) return;
    const items = trackedIssuePlannedItems(repo);
    const widgetKey = "repo-scheduler-board";
    if (!items.length) {
      destroyWidget(state.widgets[widgetKey]);
      delete state.widgets[widgetKey];
      host.innerHTML = buildInlineNotice("No tracked issues are scheduled yet.");
      return;
    }
    const columns = SCHEDULER_BUCKETS.map((bucket) => ({
      id: bucket.id,
      title: bucket.title,
      items: items.filter((item) => schedulerBucketForItem(item) === bucket.id).map((item) => ({
        id: item.id,
        title: item.title,
        description: schedulerCardDescription(item),
        labels: schedulerCardLabels(item),
        priority: schedulerPriorityTone(item.priority),
      })),
    }));
    replaceWidget(widgetKey, Teryx.kanban("#repo-scheduler-board", {
      columns,
      draggable: true,
      onMove(cardId, _fromCol, toCol) {
        api(`/api/v1/planned-items/${encodeURIComponent(cardId)}`, {
          method: "PATCH",
          body: JSON.stringify({
            schedule_at: schedulerScheduleAtForBucket(toCol),
            clear_schedule: toCol === "ready-now",
          }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID = payload.planned_item.id;
          mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          toast("success", "Schedule updated", payload.planned_item.title);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Schedule update failed", error.message);
          renderRepoControlsPage(selectedRepoSummary());
        });
      },
      onCardClick(card) {
        if (defaultString(selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary()) && selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary()).id, "") !== defaultString(card && card.id, "")) {
          clearDraftScope(repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(selectedRepoSummary(), selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary())));
        }
        state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID = card.id;
        renderRepoControlsPage(selectedRepoSummary());
      },
    }));
  }

  function renderRepoSchedulerDetail(repo) {
    const host = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-detail");
    if (!host) return;
    renderWithPreservedDraftFocus(() => {
      const item = selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(repo);
      if (!item) {
        host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Select or add a scheduled tracked issue.</div>';
        return;
      }
      const issueNumber = schedulerIssueNumber(item.target_url);
      const draftScope = repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(repo, item);
      host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(repo && repo.repo_slug, "Repo"))}${issueNumber ? ` #${escapeHTML(issueNumber)}` : ""}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(item.title)}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.target_url, "No GitHub issue URL recorded."))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">State</span><span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePill(item.state === "failed" ? "failed" : "queued", item.state)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Work Type</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(item.work_type))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Priority</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(`P${Number(item.priority ?? 5)}`)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Schedule</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(item.schedule_at) : "", "Ready now"))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Updated</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(item.updated_at))}</span></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      ${item.last_error ? `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(item.last_error)}</div>` : ""}
      <div class="scheduler-detail-form" data-draft-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}">
        <label class="selector">
          <span>Title</span>
          <input id="repo-scheduler-detail-title" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(item.title)}" />
        </label>
        <div class="config-grid">
          <label class="selector">
            <span>Priority</span>
            <select id="repo-scheduler-detail-priority">
              ${[0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((priority) => `<option value="${priority}" ${Number(item.priority ?? 5) === priority ? "selected" : ""}>P${priority}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="selector">
            <span>Work Type</span>
            <select id="repo-scheduler-detail-work-type">
              ${["bug_fix", "refactor", "feature", "test_only"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(item.work_type, "feature") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(value))}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="selector">
            <span>Exact Schedule</span>
            <input id="repo-scheduler-detail-schedule" type="datetime-local" value="${escapeHTML(toDateTimeLocal(item.schedule_at))}" />
          </label>
        </div>
        <label class="selector">
          <span>Description</span>
          <textarea id="repo-scheduler-detail-description" rows="5">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.description, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <div class="scheduler-detail-actions">
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-scheduler-save="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Save</button>
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-scheduler-launch="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Launch Now</button>
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-scheduler-delete="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Remove</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
      restoreDraftScope(draftScope, host);
    }, host);
  }

  function renderRepoOverviewPage(repo) {
    const repoRuns = pendingRunsForRepo(repo.repo_slug);
    const repoIssues = issueRows(repo);
    const repoServiceTasks = serviceTaskRows(repo);
    const repoPlannedItems = plannedItemRows(repo);
    const repoWorkItems = pendingWorkItemsForRepo(repo.repo_slug);
    const workSections = [
      renderSurfacePair([
        repoRuns.length ? renderSurface("Pending Jobs", "Work runs mapped to this repo.", '<div id="repo-pending-grid"></div>') : "",
        repoIssues.length ? renderSurface("Issues", "Tracked issues for this repo.", '<div id="repo-issues-grid"></div>') : "",
      ]),
      renderSurfacePair([
        repoServiceTasks.length ? renderSurface("Service Tasks", "Automation work queued or in flight.", '<div id="repo-service-grid"></div>') : "",
        repoPlannedItems.length ? renderSurface("Planned Queue", "Manual launches and scheduled work for this repo.", '<div id="repo-planned-grid"></div>') : "",
      ]),
      repoWorkItems.length ? renderSurface("Work Items", "Inbound items linked to this repo.", '<div id="repo-work-item-grid"></div>') : "",
    ].filter(Boolean).join("");
    ensureBodyStructure(`repo:${repo.repo_slug}:overview`, `
      <section id="repo-metrics" class="metrics-grid metrics-grid-wide"></section>
      <section class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Queue Snapshot</h3>
            <p>Current issue, service, scout-job, and planned-work pressure.</p>
          </div>
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-repo-drop="${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}">Drop Repo</button>
        </div>
        <div id="repo-queue-summary" class="queue-summary"></div>
      </section>
      ${workSections || `<section class="surface">${buildInlineNotice("No tracked work for this repo.")}</section>`}
    `);

    document.getElementById("repo-metrics").innerHTML = buildMetricCards([
      { label: "Queued Issues", value: repo.issue_counts.queued || 0, note: "Issues waiting to be picked up." },
      { label: "Blocked Issues", value: repo.issue_counts.blocked || 0, note: "Issues blocked on policy, timing, or feedback." },
      { label: "Service Queue", value: (repo.service_task_counts.queued || 0) + (repo.service_task_counts.running || 0), note: "Service tasks still executing or waiting." },
      { label: "Scout Queue", value: repoScoutQueueCount(repo), note: "Local scout jobs waiting, paused, active, or failed." },
      { label: "Dismissed Scouts", value: repoDismissedScoutCount(repo), note: "Saved scout proposals available to retry from the Scouts tab." },
      { label: "Planned Queue", value: repoManualPlannedQueueCount(repo), note: "Manual planned launches that still need action." },
      { label: "Pending Jobs", value: repoRuns.length, note: "Work runs currently mapped to this repo." },
      { label: "Work Items", value: repoWorkItems.length, note: "Inbound items linked to this repo." },
    ]);
    document.getElementById("repo-queue-summary").innerHTML = buildQueueSummary([
      { label: "Repo Mode", value: defaultString(repo.repo_mode, "unknown"), note: "Current repo routing mode." },
      { label: "Issue Pick", value: defaultString(repo.issue_pick_mode, "unknown"), note: "Automation issue pick policy." },
      { label: "PR Forward", value: defaultString(repo.pr_forward_mode, "unknown"), note: "How review and publish are forwarded." },
      { label: "Updated", value: formatDateTime(repo.updated_at), note: "Latest repo state refresh." },
      { label: "Checkout", value: repo.source_checkout_ready ? "Ready" : "Missing", note: repo.source_checkout_ready ? "Managed source checkout is available." : "Managed source checkout has not been hydrated yet." },
      { label: "Source Path", value: defaultString(repo.source_path, "Unavailable"), note: "Mapped path for the managed source checkout." },
      { label: "Last Run", value: repo.last_run ? defaultString(repo.last_run.run_id, "Unknown") : "No run recorded", note: repo.last_run ? formatDateTime(repo.last_run.updated_at || repo.last_run.started_at) : "No completed run metadata." },
    ]);
    if (repoDismissedScoutCount(repo) > 0) {
      document.getElementById("repo-queue-summary").insertAdjacentHTML("beforeend", `
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Dismissed Scout Actions</span>
          <strong class="queue-value">${escapeHTML(String(repoDismissedScoutCount(repo)))}</strong>
          <p class="queue-copy">Open Scouts to retry dismissed proposals and return them to the live queue.</p>
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-open-repo="${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}" data-open-repo-tab="scouts">Open Scouts</button>
        </article>
      `);
    }
    if (repoRuns.length) {
      renderGrid("repo-pending-grid", pendingRunColumns(false), runGridRows(repoRuns, false), {
        maxHeight: "360px",
        emptyMessage: "No pending jobs are mapped to this repo.",
      });
    }
    if (repoIssues.length) {
      renderGrid("repo-issues-grid", [
        { field: "source_number", label: "#" },
      { field: "title", label: "Title" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
      { field: "priority", label: "Priority" },
        { field: "status", label: "Status" },
        { field: "triage", label: "Triage" },
        { field: "schedule_at", label: "Scheduled" },
      ], repoIssues, {
        maxHeight: "420px",
        emptyMessage: "No issues are tracked for this repo.",
      });
    }
    if (repoServiceTasks.length) {
      renderGrid("repo-service-grid", [
        { field: "kind", label: "Kind" },
        { field: "status", label: "Status" },
        { field: "issue_key", label: "Target" },
        { field: "attempts", label: "Attempts" },
        { field: "result", label: "Result" },
      ], repoServiceTasks, {
        maxHeight: "420px",
        emptyMessage: "No service tasks are recorded for this repo.",
      });
    }
    if (repoPlannedItems.length) {
      renderGrid("repo-planned-grid", [
      { field: "title", label: "Title" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
      { field: "launch_kind", label: "Launch" },
        { field: "priority", label: "Priority" },
        { field: "schedule_at", label: "Schedule" },
        { field: "state", label: "State" },
        { field: "launch_result", label: "Result" },
      ], repoPlannedItems, {
        maxHeight: "420px",
        emptyMessage: "No planned items are queued for this repo.",
      });
    }
    if (repoWorkItems.length) {
      renderGrid("repo-work-item-grid", [
        { field: "source", label: "Source" },
        { field: "subject", label: "Subject" },
        { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
        { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePillWithPause(row.attention_state, row.status, row.pause_until, row.pause_reason) },
        { field: "draft_kind", label: "Kind" },
        { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
        { field: "id", label: "Open", action: true, template: '<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-work-item-show="{{id}}">Open</button>' },
      ], workItemRows(repoWorkItems, false), {
        maxHeight: "360px",
        emptyMessage: "No work items are linked to this repo.",
      });
    }
  }

  function populateIssueSelector(issues) {
    const select = document.getElementById("issue-select");
    if (!select) return;
    if (!issues.length) {
      state.selectedIssue = "";
      select.innerHTML = '<option value="">No tracked issues</option>';
      return;
    }
    if (!state.selectedIssue || !issues.some((issue) => String(issue.source_number) === state.selectedIssue)) {
      state.selectedIssue = String(issues[0].source_number);
    }
    select.innerHTML = issues.map((issue) => {
      const selected = String(issue.source_number) === state.selectedIssue ? "selected" : "";
      return `<option value="${issue.source_number}" ${selected}>#${issue.source_number} ${escapeHTML(issue.title)}</option>`;
    }).join("");
  }

  function populatePlannedSelector(items) {
    const select = document.getElementById("planned-select");
    if (!select) return;
    const launchable = items.filter((item) => item.state === "queued" || item.state === "failed");
    if (!launchable.length) {
      select.innerHTML = '<option value="">No launchable items</option>';
      return;
    }
    select.innerHTML = launchable.map((item) => {
      return `<option value="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">${escapeHTML(item.title)} · ${escapeHTML(item.priority)}</option>`;
    }).join("");
  }

  function renderIssueForm(issue) {
    const host = document.getElementById("issue-form");
    if (!host) return;
    renderWithPreservedDraftFocus(() => {
      destroyForm("issueForm");
      host.innerHTML = "";
      if (!issue) {
        host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Select a tracked issue to edit.</div>';
        return;
      }
      const draftScope = repoControlsIssueDraftScope();
      state.issueForm = Teryx.form("#issue-form", {
      id: "repo-controls-issue-form",
      action: "#",
      method: "post",
      layout: "vertical",
      submitLabel: "Save Issue",
      fields: [
        {
          name: "priority",
          label: "Priority",
          type: "select",
          required: true,
          value: String(issue.manual_priority_updated_at ? issue.manual_priority : (issue.priority ?? 5)),
          options: [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((priority) => ({ label: `P${priority}`, value: String(priority) })),
        },
        {
          name: "schedule_at",
          label: "Schedule At",
          type: "datetime-local",
          value: toDateTimeLocal(issue.schedule_at),
        },
        {
          name: "deferred_reason",
          label: "Deferred Reason",
          type: "textarea",
          rows: 3,
          value: issue.deferred_reason || "",
        },
      ],
      onSubmit(data) {
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${state.selectedRepo}/issues/${state.selectedIssue}`, {
          method: "PATCH",
          body: JSON.stringify({
            priority: Number(data.priority),
            schedule_at: fromDateTimeLocal(data.schedule_at),
            deferred_reason: data.deferred_reason,
            clear_schedule: !data.schedule_at,
          }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          clearDraftScope(draftScope);
          mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          toast("success", "Issue updated", `Issue #${state.selectedIssue} saved.`);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Issue update failed", error.message);
        });
        return false;
      },
    });
      state.issueForm.el.setAttribute("data-draft-scope", draftScope);
      restoreDraftScope(draftScope, state.issueForm.el);
    }, host);
  }

  function renderPlannedForm() {
    const host = document.getElementById("planned-form");
    if (!host) return;
    renderWithPreservedDraftFocus(() => {
      destroyForm("plannedForm");
      host.innerHTML = "";
      const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
      if (!repo) {
        host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Select a repo first.</div>';
        return;
      }
      const launchDefault = repo.repo_mode === "local" ? "local_work" : "github_issue";
      const draftScope = repoControlsPlannedDraftScope();
      state.plannedForm = Teryx.form("#planned-form", {
      id: "repo-controls-planned-form",
      action: "#",
      method: "post",
      layout: "vertical",
      submitLabel: "Create Planned Item",
      fields: [
        { name: "title", label: "Title", required: true, placeholder: "Schedule a maintenance task" },
        { name: "description", label: "Description", type: "textarea", rows: 4, placeholder: "Describe what Nana should do." },
        {
          name: "work_type",
          label: "Work Type",
          type: "select",
          value: "feature",
          options: ["bug_fix", "refactor", "feature", "test_only"].map((value) => ({ label: workTypeLabel(value), value })),
        },
        {
          name: "priority",
          label: "Priority",
          type: "select",
          value: "3",
          options: [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((priority) => ({ label: `P${priority}`, value: String(priority) })),
        },
        { name: "schedule_at", label: "Schedule At", type: "datetime-local" },
        {
          name: "launch_kind",
          label: "Launch Kind",
          type: "select",
          value: launchDefault,
          options: [
            { label: "Local Work", value: "local_work" },
            { label: "GitHub Issue", value: "github_issue" },
          ],
        },
      ],
      onSubmit(data) {
        const idempotencyKey = ensurePlannedFormIdempotencyKey(state.selectedRepo);
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${state.selectedRepo}/planned-items`, {
          method: "POST",
          headers: { "Idempotency-Key": idempotencyKey },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            title: data.title,
            description: data.description,
            work_type: data.work_type,
            priority: Number(data.priority),
            schedule_at: fromDateTimeLocal(data.schedule_at),
            launch_kind: data.launch_kind,
            idempotency_key: idempotencyKey,
          }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          clearDraftScope(draftScope);
          mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          resetPlannedFormIdempotencyKey(state.selectedRepo);
          if (state.plannedForm && typeof state.plannedForm.reset === "function") {
            state.plannedForm.reset();
          }
          toast("success", "Planned item added", payload.planned_item.title);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Planned item failed", error.message);
        });
        return false;
      },
    });
      state.plannedForm.el.setAttribute("data-draft-scope", draftScope);
      restoreDraftScope(draftScope, state.plannedForm.el);
    }, host);
  }

  function scoutStatusLabel(status) {
    switch (String(status || "").trim()) {
      case "external":
        return "External";
      case "planned":
        return "Planned";
      case "dismissed":
        return "Dismissed";
      default:
        return defaultString(status, "pending").replace(/_/g, " ");
    }
  }

  function scoutActionLabel(action) {
    switch (action) {
      case "promote":
        return "Promote";
      case "retry":
        return "Retry";
      case "dismiss":
        return "Dismiss";
      case "open-run":
        return "Open Run";
      case "reset":
        return "Reset";
      default:
        return action;
    }
  }

  function scoutRoleLabel(roleKey) {
    return repoScoutMeta(String(roleKey || "").replace("-scout", "")).label;
  }

  function workTypeLabel(value) {
    const normalized = String(value || "").trim();
    if (!normalized) return "(untyped)";
    return normalized.replace(/_/g, " ");
  }

  function scoutDestinationLabel(value) {
    switch (String(value || "").trim()) {
      case "review":
        return "Manual Review";
      case "repo":
        return "Repo Issue";
      case "fork":
        return "Fork Issue";
      default:
        return "Auto Promote";
    }
  }

  function scoutItemRows(items) {
    return items.map((item) => ({
      id: item.id,
      title: item.title,
      role: scoutRoleLabel(item.role),
      work_type: workTypeLabel(item.work_type),
      page: defaultString(item.page || item.route, ""),
      severity: defaultString(item.severity, ""),
      audit_mode: defaultString(item.audit_mode, ""),
      destination: scoutDestinationLabel(item.destination),
      status: scoutStatusLabel(item.status),
      status_key: defaultString(item.status === "paused" ? "blocked" : item.status, "pending"),
      pause_reason: defaultString(item.pause_reason, ""),
      pause_until: defaultString(item.pause_until, ""),
      updated_at: formatDateTime(item.updated_at || item.generated_at),
      can_promote: (item.available_actions || []).includes("promote"),
      can_retry: (item.available_actions || []).includes("retry"),
      can_dismiss: (item.available_actions || []).includes("dismiss"),
      can_open_run: (item.available_actions || []).includes("open-run"),
    }));
  }

  function renderScoutDetail(item, hostID = "repo-scout-detail") {
    const host = document.getElementById(hostID);
    if (!host) return;
    if (state.scoutItems.error) {
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.scoutItems.error)}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    if (state.scoutItems.loading && !item) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Loading scout items...</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (!item) {
      host.innerHTML = "";
      return;
    }
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="section-divider"></div>
      <div class="surface-head">
        <div>
          <h3>${escapeHTML(item.title)}</h3>
          <p>${escapeHTML(scoutRoleLabel(item.role))} · ${escapeHTML(scoutDestinationLabel(defaultString(item.destination, "local")))}</p>
        </div>
        ${renderStatePillWithPause(defaultString(item.status === "paused" ? "blocked" : item.status, "pending"), scoutStatusLabel(item.status), item.pause_until, item.pause_reason)}
      </div>
      <div class="config-meta">
        <span><strong>Artifact:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.artifact_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Generated:</strong> ${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(item.generated_at))}</span>
        <span><strong>Updated:</strong> ${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(item.updated_at || item.generated_at))}</span>
        <span><strong>Area:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.area, "Unknown"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Audit mode:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.audit_mode, "unknown"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Surface:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.surface_kind, "unknown"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Target:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.surface_target, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Page:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.page, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Route:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.route, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Work type:</strong> ${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(item.work_type))}</span>
        <span><strong>Severity:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.severity, "unknown"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Target kind:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.target_kind, "unknown"))}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Summary</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.summary, "(none)"))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Suggested Next Step</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.suggested_next_step, "(none)"))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Evidence</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.evidence, "(none)"))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Impact</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.impact, "(none)"))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Rationale</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.rationale, "(none)"))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Files</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(item.files && item.files.length ? item.files.join(", ") : "(none)")}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Screenshots</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(item.screenshots && item.screenshots.length ? item.screenshots.join(", ") : "(none)")}</p>
        </article>
      </div>
      <div class="config-meta">
        <span><strong>Proposal:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.proposal_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Policy:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.policy_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Preflight:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.preflight_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Issue Drafts:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.issue_draft_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Raw Output:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.raw_output_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Confidence:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.confidence, "unknown"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Labels:</strong> ${escapeHTML(item.labels && item.labels.length ? item.labels.join(", ") : "(none)")}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="config-meta">
        <span><strong>Browser ready:</strong> ${escapeHTML(String(Boolean(item.browser_ready)))}</span>
        <span><strong>Preflight reason:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.preflight_reason, "(none)"))}</span>
      </div>
      ${(item.recovery_count || item.last_recovery_at || item.last_recovered_run_id) ? `
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Recovery</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">Auto-retry scheduled after stale startup cleanup. Nana keeps the interrupted run in work history and retries this scout proposal once after the cooldown expires.</p>
        </article>
      </div>
      <div class="config-meta">
        <span><strong>Recovery Count:</strong> ${escapeHTML(String(Number(item.recovery_count || 0)))}</span>
        <span><strong>Recovered Run:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.last_recovered_run_id, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Recovery At:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.last_recovery_at ? formatDateTime(item.last_recovery_at) : "", "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Recovery Reason:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.last_recovery_reason, "(none)"))}</span>
      </div>` : ""}
      <div class="config-meta">
        <span><strong>Run ID:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.run_id, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Planned Item:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.planned_item_id, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Error:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.error, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Pause Until:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.pause_until ? formatDateTime(item.pause_until) : "", "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Pause Reason:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.pause_reason, "(none)"))}</span>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function syncRepoScoutsChrome(selectedCount, allSelected, retryableCount, dismissibleCount) {
    const count = state.scoutItems.items.length || 0;
    const countPill = document.getElementById("repo-scout-count");
    if (countPill) {
      countPill.textContent = `${count} items`;
    }
    const selectAllButton = document.getElementById("repo-scout-select-all");
    if (selectAllButton) {
      selectAllButton.disabled = !count;
    }
    const clearButton = document.getElementById("repo-scout-clear-selection");
    if (clearButton) {
      clearButton.disabled = !selectedCount;
    }
    const retryButton = document.getElementById("repo-scout-bulk-retry");
    if (retryButton) {
      retryButton.disabled = !retryableCount;
      retryButton.textContent = `Retry Selected (${retryableCount})`;
    }
    const dismissButton = document.getElementById("repo-scout-bulk-dismiss");
    if (dismissButton) {
      dismissButton.disabled = !dismissibleCount;
      dismissButton.textContent = `Dismiss Selected (${dismissibleCount})`;
    }
    const selectionCopy = document.getElementById("repo-scout-selection-copy");
    if (selectionCopy) {
      selectionCopy.textContent = allSelected ? `All ${selectedCount} selected` : `${selectedCount} selected`;
    }
  }

  function renderRepoScoutsPage(repo) {
    ensureScoutItemsState(repo);
    const selectedIDs = selectedScoutItemIDs();
    const selectedSet = new Set(selectedIDs);
    const selectedCount = selectedIDs.length;
    const totalCount = allScoutItemIDs().length;
    const allSelected = totalCount > 0 && selectedCount === totalCount;
    const retryableCount = scoutActionableSelection("retry").length;
    const dismissibleCount = scoutActionableSelection("dismiss").length;
    const gridRows = scoutItemRows(state.scoutItems.items).map((row) => ({
      ...row,
      selected: selectedSet.has(row.id),
    }));
    const gridRenderKey = JSON.stringify({
      loading: Boolean(state.scoutItems.loading),
      error: defaultString(state.scoutItems.error, ""),
      rows: gridRows,
    });
    ensureBodyStructure(`repo:${repo.repo_slug}:scouts`, `
      <section class="surface scout-surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Scout Items</h3>
            <p>Scout findings and proposals saved under the repo checkout.</p>
          </div>
          <span id="repo-scout-count" class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(String(state.scoutItems.items.length || 0))} items</span>
        </div>
        <div class="scout-bulk-bar">
          <button id="repo-scout-select-all" class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-scout-select-all="true" ${state.scoutItems.items.length ? "" : "disabled"}>Select All</button>
          <button id="repo-scout-clear-selection" class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-scout-clear-selection="true" ${selectedCount ? "" : "disabled"}>Clear</button>
          <button id="repo-scout-bulk-retry" class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-scout-bulk-action="retry" ${retryableCount ? "" : "disabled"}>Retry Selected (${escapeHTML(String(retryableCount))})</button>
          <button id="repo-scout-bulk-dismiss" class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-scout-bulk-action="dismiss" ${dismissibleCount ? "" : "disabled"}>Dismiss Selected (${escapeHTML(String(dismissibleCount))})</button>
          <p id="repo-scout-selection-copy" class="scout-bulk-copy">${escapeHTML(allSelected ? `All ${selectedCount} selected` : `${selectedCount} selected`)}</p>
        </div>
        <div id="repo-scout-grid"></div>
        <div id="repo-scout-detail" class="scout-detail"></div>
      </section>
    `);
    syncRepoScoutsChrome(selectedCount, allSelected, retryableCount, dismissibleCount);
    if (!state.scoutItems.loading && !state.scoutItems.loaded && !state.scoutItems.error) {
      loadScoutItems(repo.repo_slug, { silent: true });
    }
    renderGrid("repo-scout-grid", [
      {
        field: "id",
        label: "Select",
        render(row) {
          return `<label class="scout-select-cell"><input type="checkbox" class="tx-checkbox" data-scout-toggle="${escapeHTML(row.id)}" ${row.selected ? "checked" : ""} aria-label="Select ${escapeHTML(row.title)}"></label>`;
        },
      },
      { field: "title", label: "Title" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
      { field: "role", label: "Role" },
      { field: "page", label: "Page" },
      { field: "severity", label: "Severity" },
      { field: "audit_mode", label: "Audit" },
      { field: "destination", label: "Destination" },
      { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePillWithPause(row.status_key, row.status, row.pause_until, row.pause_reason) },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
      { field: "id", label: "Details", action: true, template: '<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scout-select="{{id}}">Details</button>' },
      {
        field: "id",
        label: "Actions",
        action: true,
        render(row) {
          const actions = [];
          if (row.can_promote) {
            actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scout-action="promote" data-scout-id="${escapeHTML(row.id)}">Promote</button>`);
          }
          if (row.can_retry) {
            actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scout-action="retry" data-scout-id="${escapeHTML(row.id)}">Retry</button>`);
          }
          if (row.can_dismiss) {
            actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scout-action="dismiss" data-scout-id="${escapeHTML(row.id)}">Dismiss</button>`);
          }
          if (row.can_open_run) {
            actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scout-action="open-run" data-scout-id="${escapeHTML(row.id)}">Open Run</button>`);
          }
          return actions.length ? `<div class="scout-actions">${actions.join("")}</div>` : '<span class="data-value-text">No actions</span>';
        },
      },
    ], gridRows, {
      maxHeight: "460px",
      emptyMessage: state.scoutItems.loading ? "Loading scout items..." : "No scout-discovered items found for this repo.",
      preserveScroll: true,
      renderKey: gridRenderKey,
    });
    renderScoutDetail(selectedScoutItem());
  }

  function configStatusPill(enabled) {
    return enabled
      ? '<span class="status-pill">Start Participation: enabled</span>'
      : '<span class="status-pill">Start Participation: disabled</span>';
  }

  function configFieldName(field) {
    const parts = String(field || "").split(".");
    return parts[parts.length - 1] || "";
  }

  function configFieldOptions(field) {
    switch (configFieldName(field)) {
      case "repo_mode":
        return [
          { value: "disabled", label: "Disabled" },
          { value: "local", label: "Local" },
          { value: "fork", label: "Fork" },
          { value: "repo", label: "Repo" },
        ];
      case "issue_pick_mode":
        return [
          { value: "manual", label: "Manual" },
          { value: "label", label: "Label" },
          { value: "auto", label: "Auto" },
        ];
      case "pr_forward_mode":
        return [
          { value: "approve", label: "Approve" },
          { value: "auto", label: "Auto" },
        ];
      case "fork_issues_mode":
      case "implement_mode":
        return [
          { value: "manual", label: "Manual" },
          { value: "labeled", label: "Labeled" },
          { value: "auto", label: "Auto" },
        ];
      case "publish_target":
        return [
          { value: "local-branch", label: "Local Branch" },
          { value: "fork", label: "Fork" },
          { value: "repo", label: "Repo" },
        ];
      case "enabled":
        return [
          { value: "true", label: "Enabled" },
          { value: "false", label: "Disabled" },
        ];
      case "mode":
        return [
          { value: "auto", label: "Auto" },
          { value: "manual", label: "Manual" },
        ];
      case "schedule":
        return [
          { value: "when_resolved", label: "When Resolved" },
          { value: "always", label: "Always" },
          { value: "daily", label: "Daily" },
          { value: "weekly", label: "Weekly" },
        ];
      case "issue_destination":
        return [
          { value: "local", label: "Local" },
          { value: "repo", label: "Repo" },
          { value: "fork", label: "Fork" },
        ];
      default:
        return [];
    }
  }

  function renderConfigSelect(field, label, value, options, disabled = false) {
    const choices = options.map((option) => {
      const selected = String(option.value) === String(value) ? "selected" : "";
      return `<option value="${escapeHTML(option.value)}" ${selected}>${escapeHTML(option.label)}</option>`;
    }).join("");
    return `
      <label class="selector config-selector">
        <span>${escapeHTML(label)}</span>
        <select name="${escapeHTML(field)}" data-config-field="${escapeHTML(field)}" ${disabled ? "disabled" : ""}>${choices}</select>
      </label>
    `;
  }

  function renderConfigInput(field, label, value, options = {}) {
    const type = options.type || "text";
    const min = options.min !== undefined ? ` min="${escapeHTML(String(options.min))}"` : "";
    const max = options.max !== undefined ? ` max="${escapeHTML(String(options.max))}"` : "";
    const placeholder = options.placeholder ? ` placeholder="${escapeHTML(options.placeholder)}"` : "";
    const disabled = options.disabled ? "disabled" : "";
    return `
      <label class="selector config-selector">
        <span>${escapeHTML(label)}</span>
        <input name="${escapeHTML(field)}" type="${escapeHTML(type)}" value="${escapeHTML(value)}" data-config-field="${escapeHTML(field)}" ${min}${max}${placeholder} ${disabled} />
      </label>
    `;
  }

  function parseConfigFieldValue(field, value) {
    switch (configFieldName(field)) {
      case "enabled":
        return String(value || "") === "true";
      case "labels":
        return String(value || "")
          .split(",")
          .map((label) => label.trim().toLowerCase())
          .filter(Boolean);
      case "session_limit": {
        const parsed = Number.parseInt(String(value || "0"), 10);
        return Number.isFinite(parsed) && parsed > 0 ? parsed : 0;
      }
      default:
        return value;
    }
  }

  function configScoutPolicyPath(repo, roleKey) {
    const scouts = repoScoutConfigsByRole(repo);
    const config = scouts && scouts[roleKey];
    return defaultString(config && config.policy_path, "");
  }

  function repoNeedsScoutCheckoutBootstrap(repo, draft, server) {
    if (!repo || repo.source_checkout_ready || !draft || !server) return false;
    return repoScoutCatalog(repo).some((entry) => {
      const key = entry.config_key;
      return repoConfigSnapshotKey((draft.scouts_by_role && draft.scouts_by_role[key]) || {})
        !== repoConfigSnapshotKey((server.scouts_by_role && server.scouts_by_role[key]) || {});
    });
  }

  function syncCompatibilityScouts(target) {
    if (!target) return;
    const byRole = target.scouts_by_role || {};
    const roleKeys = Array.from(new Set([
      ...repoScoutCatalog(target).map((entry) => entry.config_key),
      ...Object.keys(byRole),
    ]));
    target.scouts = {};
    roleKeys.forEach((roleKey) => {
      target.scouts[roleKey] = byRole[roleKey] || repoScoutSnapshot(roleKey, {});
    });
  }

  function setNestedConfigValue(target, field, value) {
    const parts = String(field || "").split(".");
    let cursor = target;
    for (let index = 0; index < parts.length - 1; index += 1) {
      const key = parts[index];
      cursor[key] = { ...(cursor[key] || {}) };
      cursor = cursor[key];
    }
    cursor[parts[parts.length - 1]] = value;
  }

  function renderScoutConfigSection(repo, roleKey, scout, disabled = false) {
    const roleLabel = scoutRoleLabel(roleKey);
    const policyPath = scout.policy_path || configScoutPolicyPath(repo, roleKey);
    const forkDisabled = disabled || !scout.enabled || scout.issue_destination !== "fork";
    const sessionLimitField = repoScoutMeta(roleKey, repo).defaultSessionLimit > 0
      ? renderConfigInput(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.session_limit`, "Session Limit", String(scout.session_limit || repoScoutMeta(roleKey, repo).defaultSessionLimit), { type: "number", min: 1, max: 6, disabled })
      : "";
    return `
      <div class="config-section">
        <h4>${escapeHTML(roleLabel)}</h4>
        <div class="config-meta">
          <span><strong>Status:</strong> ${escapeHTML(scout.enabled ? "Enabled" : "Disabled")}</span>
          <span><strong>Policy Path:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(policyPath, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="config-grid">
          ${renderConfigSelect(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.enabled`, "Enabled", String(Boolean(scout.enabled)), configFieldOptions("enabled"), disabled)}
          ${renderConfigSelect(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.mode`, "Mode", scout.mode, configFieldOptions("mode"), disabled)}
          ${renderConfigSelect(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.schedule`, "Schedule", scout.schedule || defaultString(repoScoutMeta(roleKey, repo).defaultSchedule, "when_resolved"), configFieldOptions("schedule"), disabled)}
          ${renderConfigSelect(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.issue_destination`, "Destination", scout.issue_destination, configFieldOptions("issue_destination"), disabled)}
          ${renderConfigInput(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.fork_repo`, "Fork Repo", scout.fork_repo || "", { placeholder: "owner/repo", disabled: forkDisabled })}
          ${sessionLimitField}
          ${renderConfigInput(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.labels`, "Labels", (scout.labels || []).join(", "), { placeholder: "comma,separated,labels", disabled })}
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function updateConfigDraft(field, rawValue, options = {}) {
    if (!state.configEditor.draft || state.configEditor.saving) return;
    const next = cloneConfigSnapshot(state.configEditor.draft);
    applyConfigDraftValue(next, selectedRepoSummary(), field, rawValue);
    syncCompatibilityScouts(next);
    state.configEditor.draft = next;
    state.configEditor.dirty = !configDraftEquals(next, state.configEditor.server);
    if (!state.configEditor.dirty) {
      state.configEditor.remoteChanged = false;
      state.configEditor.overridePublish = false;
      state.configEditor.overrideForkIssues = false;
      state.configEditor.overrideImplement = false;
    }
    if (options.rerender !== false) {
      renderRepoConfigPage(selectedRepoSummary());
    }
  }

  function resetConfigDraft(repo) {
    clearDraftScope(repoConfigFocusScope(repo));
    resetConfigEditorForRepo(repo);
    renderRepoConfigPage(repo);
  }

  function saveConfigDraft(repo) {
    if (!repo || !state.configEditor.draft || state.configEditor.saving) {
      return;
    }
    state.configEditor.saving = true;
    renderRepoConfigPage(repo);
    api(`/api/v1/repos/${repo.repo_slug}/settings`, {
      method: "PATCH",
      body: JSON.stringify(state.configEditor.draft),
    }).then((payload) => {
      state.configEditor.saving = false;
      clearDraftScope(repoConfigFocusScope(repo));
      mergeRepoSummary(payload.repo, { resetConfigEditor: true });
      toast("success", "Repo config updated", repo.repo_slug);
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.configEditor.saving = false;
      renderRepoConfigPage(repo);
      toast("danger", "Repo config failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function renderRepoConfigPage(repo) {
    ensureConfigEditor(repo);
    syncConfigEditorTransientDrafts(repo);
    const editor = state.configEditor;
    const draft = editor.draft || repoConfigSnapshot(repo);
    const draftScope = repoConfigFocusScope(repo);
    const rawSettings = repo && repo.settings ? repo.settings : {};
    const rawScouts = repo && repo.scouts_by_role ? repo.scouts_by_role : {};
    const needsScoutCheckoutBootstrap = repoNeedsScoutCheckoutBootstrap(repo, draft, editor.server);
    const configInputsDisabled = Boolean(editor.saving);
    const inventory = [
      { label: "Settings Path", value: defaultString(repo && repo.settings_path, "Unavailable") },
      { label: "Source Checkout", value: repo && repo.source_checkout_ready ? "Ready" : "Missing" },
      { label: "Source Path", value: defaultString(repo && repo.source_path, "Unavailable") },
      { label: "Start State Path", value: defaultString(repo && repo.state_path, "Unavailable") },
    ].concat(repoScoutCatalog(repo).map((entry) => ({
      label: `${scoutRoleLabel(entry.config_key)} Policy`,
      value: defaultString(rawScouts[entry.config_key] && rawScouts[entry.config_key].policy_path, "Unavailable"),
    })));
    const resetDisabled = editor.saving || (!editor.dirty && !editor.remoteChanged);
    const saveDisabled = !editor.dirty || editor.saving;
    const statusCopy = editor.saving
      ? needsScoutCheckoutBootstrap
        ? "Preparing managed checkout and saving scout policies..."
        : "Saving changes..."
      : editor.remoteChanged
        ? "Server config changed while you were editing. Reset to load the latest values."
        : editor.dirty
          ? "Unsaved changes."
          : "All changes saved.";
    ensureBodyStructure(`repo:${repo.repo_slug}:config`, `
      <section class="surface">
        <div id="repo-config-root"></div>
      </section>
    `);
    const host = document.getElementById("repo-config-root");
    if (!host) {
      return;
    }
    renderWithPreservedDraftFocus(() => {
      host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="surface-head">
        <div>
          <h3>Repo Configuration</h3>
          <p>Basic controls set the defaults. Advanced controls and scout policies can override them for this repo.</p>
        </div>
        ${configStatusPill(Boolean(repo.start_participation))}
      </div>
      <div class="config-meta">
        <span><strong>Settings path:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(repo.settings_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Source checkout:</strong> ${escapeHTML(repo.source_checkout_ready ? "Ready" : "Missing")}</span>
        <span><strong>Updated:</strong> ${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(repo.settings && repo.settings.updated_at))}</span>
      </div>
      <form id="repo-config-form" class="config-form" data-focus-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}" data-draft-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}">
        <div class="config-section">
          <h4>Basic Routing</h4>
          <div class="config-grid">
            ${renderConfigSelect("repo_mode", "Repo Mode", draft.repo_mode, configFieldOptions("repo_mode"), configInputsDisabled)}
            ${renderConfigSelect("issue_pick_mode", "Issue Pick", draft.issue_pick_mode, configFieldOptions("issue_pick_mode"), configInputsDisabled)}
            ${renderConfigSelect("pr_forward_mode", "PR Forward", draft.pr_forward_mode, configFieldOptions("pr_forward_mode"), configInputsDisabled)}
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="config-section">
          <h4>Automation Overrides</h4>
          <div class="config-grid">
            ${renderConfigSelect("fork_issues_mode", "Fork Issues", draft.fork_issues_mode, configFieldOptions("fork_issues_mode"), configInputsDisabled)}
            ${renderConfigSelect("implement_mode", "Implement", draft.implement_mode, configFieldOptions("implement_mode"), configInputsDisabled)}
            ${renderConfigSelect("publish_target", "Publish Target", draft.publish_target || "local-branch", configFieldOptions("publish_target"), configInputsDisabled || draft.repo_mode === "disabled")}
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="config-section">
          <h4>Scout Policies</h4>
          <p class="queue-copy">Saving keeps one active policy file per scout under managed scout storage. If the managed source checkout is missing, Nana prepares it before writing scout policies.</p>
        </div>
        ${repoScoutCatalog(repo).map((entry) => renderScoutConfigSection(repo, entry.config_key, draft.scouts_by_role[entry.config_key], configInputsDisabled)).join("")}
        <div class="config-footer">
          <p class="config-status-copy">${escapeHTML(statusCopy)}</p>
          <div class="config-actions">
            <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-config-reset="true" ${resetDisabled ? "disabled" : ""}>Reset</button>
            <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="submit" ${saveDisabled ? "disabled" : ""}>${escapeHTML(editor.saving ? "Saving..." : "Save Changes")}</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </form>
      <div class="section-divider"></div>
      <div class="config-section">
        <h4>Config Inventory</h4>
        <div class="config-meta">
          ${inventory.map((item) => `<span><strong>${escapeHTML(item.label)}:</strong> ${escapeHTML(item.value)}</span>`).join("")}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="config-section">
        <h4>All Repo Configs</h4>
        <p class="queue-copy">Raw repo settings and scout config payloads currently loaded for this repo.</p>
        <div class="config-json-grid">
          <div class="surface">
            <div class="surface-head">
              <div>
                <h4>settings.json</h4>
                <p>Full repo settings payload, including defaults, review rules, and hot-path profile.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <pre class="log-content">${escapeHTML(prettyJSON(rawSettings))}</pre>
          </div>
          <div class="surface">
            <div class="surface-head">
              <div>
                <h4>Scout Configs</h4>
                <p>Effective per-role scout configuration with the loaded policy paths.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <pre class="log-content">${escapeHTML(prettyJSON(rawScouts))}</pre>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
      restoreDraftScope(draftScope, document.getElementById("repo-config-form"));
    }, host);
  }

  function renderRepoControlsPage(repo) {
    ensureRepoScheduler(repo);
    const issues = issueRows(repo);
    const planned = plannedItemRows(repo);
    const launchablePlanned = planned.filter((item) => item.state === "queued" || item.state === "failed");
    ensureBodyStructure(`repo:${repo.repo_slug}:controls`, `
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div id="repo-scheduler-search-panel"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Tracked Issue Schedule</h3>
              <p>Drag scheduled tracked issues between buckets. Clicking a card opens exact edit controls.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="repo-scheduler-board"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Selected Scheduled Issue</h3>
              <p>Override the exact launch time or remove the issue from the manual schedule.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="repo-scheduler-detail"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface-stack">
          <section class="surface">
            <div class="surface-head">
              <div>
                <h3>Manage Existing Tracked Issue</h3>
                <p>Fallback controls for mirrored start-state issues.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <label class="selector inline-selector">
              <span>Issue</span>
              <select id="issue-select" ${issues.length ? "" : "disabled"}></select>
            </label>
            <div id="issue-form"></div>
          </section>
          <section class="surface">
            <div class="surface-head">
              <div>
                <h3>Create Planned Launch</h3>
                <p>Queue repo-local work or create new GitHub issues.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div id="planned-form"></div>
            <div class="launch-controls">
              <div class="section-divider"></div>
              <div class="stack-section-head">
                <h4>Launch Existing</h4>
                <p>Run a queued planned item immediately.</p>
              </div>
              <label class="selector">
                <span>Launch Existing</span>
                <select id="planned-select" ${launchablePlanned.length ? "" : "disabled"}></select>
              </label>
              <button id="launch-planned-button" class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" ${launchablePlanned.length ? "" : "disabled"}>Launch Now</button>
            </div>
          </section>
        </div>
      </section>
    `);
    populateIssueSelector(issues);
    populatePlannedSelector(planned);
    renderIssueForm(selectedIssueRecord());
    renderPlannedForm();
    renderRepoSchedulerSearchPanel(repo);
    renderRepoSchedulerBoard(repo);
    renderRepoSchedulerDetail(repo);
  }

  function renderBody() {
    if (state.currentView === "home") {
      renderGlobalPage();
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "issues") {
      ensureViewData("issues");
      renderIssuesPage();
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "investigations") {
      ensureViewData("investigations");
      renderInvestigationsPage();
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "work") {
      renderWorkPage();
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "usage") {
      ensureViewData("usage");
      renderUsagePage();
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "feedback") {
      ensureViewData("feedback");
      renderFeedbackPage();
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "approvals") {
      ensureViewData("approvals");
      renderApprovalsPage();
      return;
    }
    const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
    const body = document.getElementById("page-body");
    if (!repo) {
      if (state.pageSignature !== "repo-empty") {
        destroyWidgets();
        state.pageSignature = "repo-empty";
      }
      resetScoutItemsState(null);
      body.innerHTML = '<section class="surface empty-surface"><div class="status-pill">No repo is selected.</div></section>';
      return;
    }
    if (state.repoTab === "scouts") {
      renderRepoScoutsPage(repo);
      return;
    }
    if (state.repoTab === "config") {
      renderRepoConfigPage(repo);
      return;
    }
    if (state.repoTab === "controls") {
      renderRepoControlsPage(repo);
      return;
    }
    renderRepoOverviewPage(repo);
  }

  function refreshCounts(repo, updatedState) {
    repo.issue_counts = {};
    repo.service_task_counts = {};
    repo.scout_job_counts = {};
    repo.planned_item_counts = {};
    Object.values(updatedState.issues || {}).forEach((issue) => {
      const key = issue.status || "";
      repo.issue_counts[key] = (repo.issue_counts[key] || 0) + 1;
    });
    Object.values(updatedState.service_tasks || {}).forEach((task) => {
      const key = task.status || "";
      repo.service_task_counts[key] = (repo.service_task_counts[key] || 0) + 1;
    });
    Object.values(updatedState.scout_jobs || {}).forEach((job) => {
      const key = job.status || "";
      repo.scout_job_counts[key] = (repo.scout_job_counts[key] || 0) + 1;
    });
    Object.values(updatedState.planned_items || {}).forEach((item) => {
      const key = item.state || "";
      repo.planned_item_counts[key] = (repo.planned_item_counts[key] || 0) + 1;
    });
  }

  function mergeRepoSummary(updatedRepo, options = {}) {
    if (!state.overview || !updatedRepo) return;
    const index = state.overview.repos.findIndex((entry) => entry.repo_slug === updatedRepo.repo_slug);
    if (index === -1) return;
    const existing = state.overview.repos[index];
    state.overview.repos[index] = {
      ...existing,
      ...updatedRepo,
      state: updatedRepo.state || existing.state || null,
    };
    if (state.configEditor.repoSlug === updatedRepo.repo_slug) {
      if (options.resetConfigEditor) {
        resetConfigEditorForRepo(state.overview.repos[index]);
      } else {
        ensureConfigEditor(state.overview.repos[index]);
      }
    }
    if (options.resetScouts && state.scoutItems.repoSlug === updatedRepo.repo_slug) {
      resetScoutItemsState(state.overview.repos[index]);
    }
    if (options.rerender !== false) {
      renderAppPreservingDraftFocus();
    }
  }

  function mergeRepoState(updatedState) {
    if (!state.overview) return;
    const repo = state.overview.repos.find((entry) => entry.repo_slug === updatedState.source_repo);
    if (!repo) return;
    repo.state = updatedState;
    repo.updated_at = updatedState.updated_at;
    refreshCounts(repo, updatedState);
    reconcileRepoScheduler(repo);
    renderAppPreservingDraftFocus();
  }

  function initLogDrawer() {
    if (state.logDrawer) return;
    state.logDrawer = Teryx.drawer({
      title: "Run Detail",
      position: "right",
      size: "720px",
      content: '<div id="log-drawer-content" class="drawer-shell"></div>',
      onClose() {
        state.logSelection = defaultLogSelection();
        renderLogDrawer();
      },
    });
  }

  function renderLogDrawer() {
    const host = document.getElementById("log-drawer-content");
    if (!host) return;
    const currentLogContent = host.querySelector(".log-content");
    const scrollIdentity = state.logSelection.runID && state.logSelection.filePath
      ? `${state.logSelection.runID}:${state.logSelection.filePath}`
      : "";
    const preserveLogScroll = Boolean(scrollIdentity && scrollIdentity === state.logSelection.scrollIdentity);
    const logScrollTop = preserveLogScroll && currentLogContent ? currentLogContent.scrollTop : 0;
    const updateHost = (html) => {
      host.innerHTML = html;
      if (preserveLogScroll) {
        const nextLogContent = host.querySelector(".log-content");
        if (nextLogContent) {
          nextLogContent.scrollTop = logScrollTop;
        }
      }
      state.logSelection.scrollIdentity = scrollIdentity;
    };

    if (!state.logSelection.runID) {
      updateHost('<div class="log-empty">Choose a run to inspect it.</div>');
      return;
    }

    if ((state.logSelection.loading || state.logSelection.detailLoading) && !state.logSelection.meta && !state.logSelection.detail) {
      updateHost('<div class="log-empty">Loading run detail...</div>');
      return;
    }

    if (state.logSelection.error) {
      updateHost(`<div class="log-empty">${escapeHTML(state.logSelection.error)}</div>`);
      return;
    }

    const meta = state.logSelection.meta;
    const detail = state.logSelection.detail;
    if (!meta && !detail) {
      updateHost('<div class="log-empty">Run detail is unavailable.</div>');
      return;
    }

    const summary = (detail && detail.summary) || (meta && meta.summary) || {};
    const files = (meta && meta.files) || [];
    const options = files.map((file) => {
      const selected = file.path === state.logSelection.filePath ? "selected" : "";
      return `<option value="${escapeHTML(file.path)}" ${selected}>${escapeHTML(file.path)}</option>`;
    }).join("");
    const manifest = detail ? (detail.github_manifest || detail.local_manifest || null) : null;
    const status = detail && detail.github_status ? detail.github_status : null;
    const typedDetail = detail || {};
    const latestCompletionRound = manifest && Array.isArray(manifest.completion_rounds) && manifest.completion_rounds.length
      ? manifest.completion_rounds[manifest.completion_rounds.length - 1]
      : null;
    const phaseSummary = summary.current_round && !summary.pause_until
      ? `${defaultString(summary.current_phase, "Awaiting phase")} · Round ${summary.current_round}`
      : defaultString(summary.current_phase, "Awaiting phase");
    const runPauseSummary = pauseStateSummary(summary.pause_until, summary.pause_reason);
    const laneMarkup = status && Array.isArray(status.lanes) && status.lanes.length
      ? `<ul class="status-list">${status.lanes.map((lane) => `
          <li>
            <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(lane.alias, lane.role))}</strong>
            <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(lane.status, "(none)"))}</span>
            <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(lane.role, "(none)"))}</span>
          </li>
        `).join("")}</ul>`
      : '<div class="status-pill">No lane status is available.</div>';
    const manifestSummaryMarkup = typedDetail.backend === "github" && manifest
      ? `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Next Action</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(typedDetail.next_action, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Human Gate</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(typedDetail.human_gate_reason, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Publication Detail</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(status && status.publication_detail, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Final Gate</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(status && status.final_gate_status, defaultString(manifest && manifest.final_gate_status, "(none)")))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Candidate Audit</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(status && status.candidate_audit_status, defaultString(manifest && manifest.candidate_audit_status, "(none)")))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Latest Completion</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(latestCompletionRound ? `Round ${latestCompletionRound.round}: ${defaultString(latestCompletionRound.status, "(none)")} · ${defaultString(latestCompletionRound.verification_summary, "(none)")}` : "(none)")}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">External URL</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(typedDetail.external_url, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
        <div class="section-divider"></div>
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Lane Status</h3><p>Per-lane runtime state for this GitHub-backed run.</p></div></div>
        ${laneMarkup}
      `
      : `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Next Action</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(typedDetail.next_action, defaultString(summary.current_phase, "(none)")))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Sandbox</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(manifest && manifest.sandbox_path, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Repo Checkout</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(manifest && manifest.sandbox_repo_path, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Iteration</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(manifest && manifest.current_iteration, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          ${manifest && manifest.superseded_by_run_id ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Superseded By</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(manifest.superseded_by_run_id)}</p></article>` : ""}
          ${manifest && manifest.superseded_reason ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Superseded Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(manifest.superseded_reason)}</p></article>` : ""}
          ${manifest && manifest.superseded_at ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Superseded At</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(manifest.superseded_at))}</p></article>` : ""}
        </div>
      `;

    updateHost(`
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">Run</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(summary.run_id || state.logSelection.runID)}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(runRepoDisplay(summary))} · ${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.backend, "unknown"))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Status</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePillWithPause(defaultString(summary.attention_state, "active"), defaultString(summary.status, "active"), summary.pause_until, summary.pause_reason)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Phase</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(phaseSummary)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Artifact Root</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(meta && meta.artifact_root, defaultString(summary.artifact_path, "Unavailable")))}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Updated</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(summary.updated_at))}</span>
          </div>
          ${runPauseSummary ? `<div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Retry</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(runPauseSummary)}</span></div>` : ""}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Run State</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.target_url, "No target URL recorded."))}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Backend</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.backend, "unknown"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Work Type</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(summary.work_type))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Publication</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.publication_state, typedDetail.backend === "github" && manifest && manifest.publication_state || "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Repo</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(runRepoDisplay(summary))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Current Phase</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(phaseSummary)}</p></article>
          ${summary.pause_until ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Pause Until</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(summary.pause_until))}</p></article>` : ""}
          ${summary.pause_reason ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Pause Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(summary.pause_reason)}</p></article>` : ""}
        </div>
        ${manifestSummaryMarkup}
      </div>
      <div class="drawer-toolbar">
        <label class="selector">
          <span>File</span>
          <select id="log-file-select" ${files.length ? "" : "disabled"}>${options || '<option value="">No log files</option>'}</select>
        </label>
        ${typedDetail.stop_allowed ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-run-stop="${escapeHTML(summary.run_id)}">Stop Run</button>` : ""}
        ${typedDetail.resolve_allowed ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-run-resolve="${escapeHTML(summary.run_id)}">Resolve Run</button>` : ""}
        ${typedDetail.rerun_allowed ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-run-rerun="${escapeHTML(summary.run_id)}">Re-run</button>` : ""}
        ${typedDetail.sync_allowed ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-run-sync="${escapeHTML(summary.run_id)}">Sync Run</button>` : ""}
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-run-drop="${escapeHTML(summary.run_id)}">Drop Run</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-log-refresh="true">Refresh</button>
      </div>
      ${state.logSelection.loadingContent ? '<div class="status-pill">Loading log content...</div>' : ""}
      <pre class="log-content">${escapeHTML(state.logSelection.content || "No log content available.")}</pre>
    `);
  }

  function openLogDrawer(runID) {
    initLogDrawer();
    state.logSelection = defaultLogSelection();
    state.logSelection.runID = runID;
    renderLogDrawer();
    state.logDrawer.open();
    loadRunDetail(runID);
    loadLogMetadata(runID);
  }

  function loadRunDetail(runID) {
    state.logSelection.runID = runID;
    state.logSelection.detailLoading = true;
    state.logSelection.error = "";
    renderLogDrawer();
