    return api(`/api/v1/work/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runID)}`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.logSelection.runID !== runID) return;
      state.logSelection.detail = payload;
      state.logSelection.detailLoading = false;
      renderLogDrawer();
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.logSelection.runID !== runID) return;
      state.logSelection.detailLoading = false;
      state.logSelection.error = error.message;
      renderLogDrawer();
      toast("danger", "Run detail failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function loadLogMetadata(runID, options = {}) {
    state.logSelection.runID = runID;
    state.logSelection.loading = true;
    state.logSelection.error = "";
    renderLogDrawer();
    return api(`/api/v1/work/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runID)}/logs`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.logSelection.runID !== runID) return;
      state.logSelection.meta = payload;
      state.logSelection.loading = false;
      const requestedPath = options.preserveFile ? state.logSelection.filePath : "";
      const available = (payload.files || []).map((file) => file.path);
      const filePath = available.includes(requestedPath)
        ? requestedPath
        : (payload.default_path || available[0] || "");
      state.logSelection.filePath = filePath;
      renderLogDrawer();
      if (filePath) {
        return loadLogContent(runID, filePath);
      }
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.logSelection.runID !== runID) return;
      state.logSelection.loading = false;
      state.logSelection.error = error.message;
      renderLogDrawer();
      toast("danger", "Log load failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function loadLogContent(runID, filePath) {
    state.logSelection.filePath = filePath;
    state.logSelection.loadingContent = true;
    renderLogDrawer();
    const query = new URLSearchParams({ path: filePath, tail: "200" });
    return api(`/api/v1/work/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runID)}/logs/content?${query.toString()}`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.logSelection.runID !== runID || state.logSelection.filePath !== filePath) return;
      state.logSelection.loadingContent = false;
      state.logSelection.content = payload.content || "";
      state.logSelection.error = "";
      if (state.logSelection.meta && payload.summary) {
        state.logSelection.meta.summary = payload.summary;
      }
      renderLogDrawer();
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.logSelection.runID !== runID) return;
      state.logSelection.loadingContent = false;
      state.logSelection.error = error.message;
      renderLogDrawer();
      toast("danger", "Log content failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function refreshOpenLogDrawerIfNeeded() {
    if (!state.logSelection.runID || !state.logSelection.meta) return;
    const current = currentRunSummary(state.logSelection.runID);
    if (!current) return;
    const previous = state.logSelection.meta.summary || {};
    if (current.updated_at !== previous.updated_at || current.status !== previous.status || current.current_phase !== previous.current_phase) {
      loadRunDetail(state.logSelection.runID);
      loadLogMetadata(state.logSelection.runID, { preserveFile: true });
    }
  }

  function initWorkItemDrawer() {
    if (state.workItemDrawer) return;
    state.workItemDrawer = Teryx.drawer({
      title: "Work Item",
      position: "right",
      size: "720px",
      content: '<div id="work-item-drawer-content" class="drawer-shell"></div>',
      onClose() {
        state.workItemSelection = defaultWorkItemSelection();
        renderWorkItemDrawer();
      },
    });
  }

  function groupInlineCommentsByPath(comments) {
    const grouped = {};
    (comments || []).forEach((comment) => {
      const key = defaultString(comment.path, "(no path)");
      if (!grouped[key]) {
        grouped[key] = [];
      }
      grouped[key].push(comment);
    });
    return grouped;
  }

  function renderReviewDraftDetail(draft) {
    if (!draft) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">No draft is ready yet.</div>';
    }
    const grouped = groupInlineCommentsByPath(draft.inline_comments || []);
    const groupedHTML = Object.keys(grouped).length
      ? Object.entries(grouped).map(([path, comments]) => `
          <article class="queue-item">
            <span class="queue-label">${escapeHTML(path)}</span>
            <ul class="status-list">
              ${comments.map((comment) => `
                <li>
                  <strong>Line ${escapeHTML(defaultString(comment.line, "-"))}</strong>
                  <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(comment.body, "(none)"))}</span>
                </li>
              `).join("")}
            </ul>
          </article>
        `).join("")
      : '<div class="status-pill">No inline comments were generated.</div>';
    return `
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Summary</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.summary, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Review Event</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.review_event, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Disposition</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.suggested_disposition, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Confidence</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.confidence, "(none)"))}</p></article>
      </div>
      <div class="section-divider"></div>
      <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Review Body</h3><p>Top-level review summary and request.</p></div></div>
      <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.body, "(none)"))}</p>
      <div class="section-divider"></div>
      <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Inline Comments</h3><p>Grouped by file path.</p></div></div>
      <div class="queue-summary">${groupedHTML}</div>
    `;
  }

  function renderReplyDraftDetail(item, draft) {
    if (!draft) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">No draft is ready yet.</div>';
    }
    return `
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Summary</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.summary, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Comment Kind</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.metadata && item.metadata.comment_kind, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Comment Path</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.metadata && item.metadata.comment_path, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Comment Line</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.metadata && item.metadata.comment_line, "(none)"))}</p></article>
      </div>
      <div class="section-divider"></div>
      <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Reply Body</h3><p>Response that will be submitted to the target thread.</p></div></div>
      <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.body, "(none)"))}</p>
    `;
  }

  function renderWorkItemDrawer() {
    const host = document.getElementById("work-item-drawer-content");
    if (!host) return;

    renderWithPreservedDraftFocus(() => {
      if (!state.workItemSelection.itemID) {
        host.innerHTML = '<div class="log-empty">Choose a work item to inspect it.</div>';
        return;
      }

      if (state.workItemSelection.loading && !state.workItemSelection.detail) {
        host.innerHTML = '<div class="log-empty">Loading work item...</div>';
        return;
      }

      if (state.workItemSelection.error) {
        host.innerHTML = `<div class="log-empty">${escapeHTML(state.workItemSelection.error)}</div>`;
        return;
      }

      const detail = state.workItemSelection.detail;
      if (!detail || !detail.item) {
        host.innerHTML = '<div class="log-empty">Work item details are unavailable.</div>';
        return;
      }

      const item = detail.item;
      const draft = item.latest_draft || null;
      const workItemPauseSummary = pauseStateSummary(item.pause_until, item.pause_reason);
      const showRestoreButton = Boolean(item.hidden || item.status === "dropped");
      const workTypeValue = defaultString(state.workItemSelection.workType, defaultString(item.work_type, ""));
      const workTypeDirty = workTypeValue && workTypeValue !== defaultString(item.work_type, "");
      const showExecutionControls = Boolean(detail.execution_allowed);
      const recoverSummary = defaultString(detail.recover_summary, "Recover Work tries to continue linked work when possible and otherwise starts a fresh run using the selected work type.");
      const events = (detail.events || []).map((event) => {
        return `
        <li>
          <strong>${escapeHTML(event.event_type)}</strong>
          <span>${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(event.created_at))}</span>
          <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(event.actor, "-"))}</span>
        </li>
      `;
      }).join("");

      host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">Item</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(item.id)}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.source, "-"))}/${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.source_kind, "-"))} · ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.repo_slug, "Standalone"))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Status</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePillWithPause(defaultString(currentWorkItemSummary(item.id)?.attention_state, "active"), defaultString(item.status, "-"), item.pause_until, item.pause_reason)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Target</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.target_url, "Unavailable"))}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Linked Run</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.linked_run_id, "-"))}</span>
          </div>
	          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
	            <span class="drawer-label">Updated</span>
	            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(item.updated_at))}</span>
	          </div>
	          ${showExecutionControls ? `<div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Work Type</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(workTypeValue ? workTypeLabel(workTypeValue) : "(unset)")}</span></div>` : ""}
	          ${workItemPauseSummary ? `<div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Retry</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(workItemPauseSummary)}</span></div>` : ""}
	        </div>
	      </div>
	      <div class="drawer-toolbar">
	        ${item.status === "paused" ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-requeue="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Return to Queue</button>` : ""}
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-run="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Run</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-fix="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Fix</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-work-item-submit="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Submit</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-drop="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Drop</button>
        ${showRestoreButton ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-restore="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Restore</button>` : ""}
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-refresh="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Refresh</button>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.subject, "(no subject)"))}</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.body, "No source body captured."))}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
	        ${(item.pause_until || item.pause_reason) ? `
	          <div class="queue-summary">
	            ${item.pause_until ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Pause Until</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(item.pause_until))}</p></article>` : ""}
	            ${item.pause_reason ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Pause Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(item.pause_reason)}</p></article>` : ""}
	          </div>
	        ` : ""}
	      </div>
	      ${showExecutionControls ? `
	      <div class="surface">
	        <div class="surface-head">
	          <div>
	            <h3>Execution Controls</h3>
	            <p>Run starts work from this item now. ${escapeHTML(recoverSummary)} Run and Recover Work save the selected work type before acting.</p>
	          </div>
	        </div>
	        <label class="selector config-selector">
	          <span>Work Type</span>
	          <select id="work-item-work-type">
	            <option value="" ${workTypeValue ? "" : "selected"}>${escapeHTML(item.work_type ? "Keep current work type" : "Select a work type")}</option>
	            ${["bug_fix", "refactor", "feature", "test_only"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${workTypeValue === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(value))}</option>`).join("")}
	          </select>
	        </label>
	        <div class="config-actions">
	          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-save="${escapeHTML(item.id)}" ${workTypeDirty ? "" : "disabled"}>Save Work Type</button>
	          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-work-item-recover="${escapeHTML(item.id)}" ${detail.recover_allowed ? "" : "disabled"}>Recover Work</button>
	        </div>
	      </div>
	      ` : ""}
	      <div class="surface">
	        <div class="surface-head">
	          <div>
            <h3>Draft</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft ? draft.summary : "", draft ? "Review the current draft before submission." : "No draft is ready yet."))}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${draft && draft.kind === "review"
          ? renderReviewDraftDetail(draft)
          : renderReplyDraftDetail(item, draft)}
      </div>
      <div class="surface" data-focus-scope="${escapeHTML(workItemFixInstructionFocusScope(item))}">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Revise Draft</h3>
            <p>Write an instruction for Nana to revise the current draft.</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Instruction</span>
          <textarea id="work-item-fix-instruction" rows="4" placeholder="Clarify the justification and tighten the reply.">${escapeHTML(state.workItemSelection.fixInstruction || "")}</textarea>
        </label>
        <div class="config-actions">
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-fix="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Apply Revision</button>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Events</h3>
            <p>Audit history for this item.</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${events ? `<ul class="status-list">${events}</ul>` : '<div class="status-pill">No events are recorded yet.</div>'}
      </div>
    `;
    }, host);
  }

  function openWorkItemDrawer(itemID) {
    initWorkItemDrawer();
    state.workItemSelection = defaultWorkItemSelection();
    state.workItemSelection.itemID = itemID;
    state.workItemSelection.loading = true;
    renderWorkItemDrawer();
    state.workItemDrawer.open();
    loadWorkItemDetail(itemID);
  }

  function workItemRequestedWorkType(detail) {
    if (!detail || !detail.item) return "";
    return String(state.workItemSelection.workType || detail.item.work_type || "").trim();
  }

  function persistWorkItemWorkTypeIfNeeded(itemID) {
    const detail = state.workItemSelection.detail;
    if (!detail || !detail.item || detail.item.id !== itemID) {
      return Promise.resolve(detail);
    }
    const current = String(detail.item.work_type || "").trim();
    const next = workItemRequestedWorkType(detail);
    if (!next || next === current) {
      return Promise.resolve(detail);
    }
    return api(`/api/v1/work-items/${encodeURIComponent(itemID)}`, {
      method: "PATCH",
      body: JSON.stringify({ work_type: next }),
    }).then((payload) => {
      if (state.workItemSelection.itemID !== itemID) return payload;
      state.workItemSelection.detail = payload;
      state.workItemSelection.workType = "";
      renderWorkItemDrawer();
      load();
      return payload;
    });
  }

  function loadWorkItemDetail(itemID, options = {}) {
    state.workItemSelection.itemID = itemID;
    state.workItemSelection.loading = true;
    state.workItemSelection.error = "";
    if (options.resetFixInstruction) {
      state.workItemSelection.fixInstruction = "";
    }
    if (options.resetWorkType) {
      state.workItemSelection.workType = "";
    }
    renderWorkItemDrawer();
    return api(`/api/v1/work-items/${encodeURIComponent(itemID)}`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.workItemSelection.itemID !== itemID) return;
      state.workItemSelection.loading = false;
      state.workItemSelection.detail = payload;
      if (options.resetFixInstruction) {
        state.workItemSelection.fixInstruction = "";
      }
      if (options.resetWorkType) {
        state.workItemSelection.workType = "";
      }
      renderWorkItemDrawer();
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.workItemSelection.itemID !== itemID) return;
      state.workItemSelection.loading = false;
      state.workItemSelection.error = error.message;
      renderWorkItemDrawer();
      toast("danger", "Work item failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function refreshOpenWorkItemDrawerIfNeeded() {
    if (!state.workItemSelection.itemID || !state.workItemSelection.detail) return;
    const current = currentWorkItemSummary(state.workItemSelection.itemID);
    const previous = state.workItemSelection.detail.item || {};
    if (!current) return;
    if (current.updated_at !== previous.updated_at || current.status !== previous.status) {
      loadWorkItemDetail(state.workItemSelection.itemID);
    }
  }

  function renderApp() {
    if (!state.overview && !canRenderWithoutOverview(state.currentView)) {
      syncUsageAutoRefresh();
      return;
    }
    ensureSelection();
    renderSidebar();
    renderHeader();
    renderRepoPicker();
    renderRepoOnboardingDrawer();
    renderBreadcrumbs();
    renderTabs();
    renderBody();
    renderConfirmDialog();
    syncHashState();
    syncUsageAutoRefresh();
    refreshOpenLogDrawerIfNeeded();
    refreshOpenWorkItemDrawerIfNeeded();
    syncTaskDetailModalState();
  }

  function attachHandlers() {
    document.getElementById("refresh-button").addEventListener("click", () => {
      load();
      if (((state.currentView === "repo" && state.repoTab === "scouts") || state.currentView === "investigations") && state.selectedRepo) {
        loadScoutItems(state.selectedRepo, { silent: true });
      }
      if (state.logSelection.runID) {
        loadRunDetail(state.logSelection.runID);
        loadLogMetadata(state.logSelection.runID, { preserveFile: true });
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("repo-picker-host").addEventListener("change", (event) => {
      if (!event.target.matches("[data-repo-picker]")) return;
      const value = String(event.target.value || "");
      if (value === WORKSPACE_SCOPE_ONBOARD) {
        openRepoOnboardingFlow();
        return;
      }
      if (value === WORKSPACE_SCOPE_ALL) {
        setWorkspaceRepoScope("");
        return;
      }
      setWorkspaceRepoScope(value);
    });

    document.body.addEventListener("change", (event) => {
      const repoOnboardField = event.target.getAttribute("data-repo-onboard-field");
      if (!repoOnboardField) return;
      state.repoOnboarding.draft[repoOnboardField] = String(event.target.value || "");
      state.repoOnboarding.error = "";
      renderRepoOnboardingDrawer();
    });

    document.body.addEventListener("input", (event) => {
      const repoOnboardField = event.target.getAttribute("data-repo-onboard-field");
      if (!repoOnboardField) return;
      state.repoOnboarding.draft[repoOnboardField] = String(event.target.value || "");
      state.repoOnboarding.error = "";
    });

    document.body.addEventListener("submit", (event) => {
      if (event.target.id !== "repo-onboard-form") return;
      event.preventDefault();
      submitRepoOnboarding();
    });

    document.getElementById("sidebar-nav").addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      if (event.target.closest("[data-view-filter-reset]")) {
        event.preventDefault();
        event.stopPropagation();
        return;
      }
      const button = event.target.closest("[data-nav-view]");
      if (!button) return;
      const nextView = button.getAttribute("data-nav-view");
      if (nextView && nextView !== "repo") {
        const nextRepo = nextView === "home" ? "" : state.selectedRepo;
        clearDraftsForRouteTransition({ view: nextView, repoSlug: nextRepo, repoTab: state.repoTab });
        state.currentView = nextView;
        state.selectedRepo = nextRepo;
        syncWorkspaceRepoFilters(nextRepo);
        ensureViewData(nextView);
        renderApp();
        return;
      }
      const repoSlug = button.getAttribute("data-repo-slug");
      if (!repoSlug) return;
      openRepoView(repoSlug, "overview");
    });

    document.getElementById("page-tabs").addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      const button = event.target.closest("[data-tab-group]");
      if (!button) return;
      const group = button.getAttribute("data-tab-group");
      const tabID = button.getAttribute("data-tab-id") || "";
      if (group === "repo") {
        clearDraftsForRouteTransition({ view: "repo", repoSlug: state.selectedRepo, repoTab: tabID || "overview" });
        state.repoTab = tabID || "overview";
        renderApp();
        return;
      }
      if (group === "feedback") {
        state.feedbackTab = tabID || "reviews";
        renderApp();
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("page-tabs").addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
      const tab = event.target.closest("[data-tab-group]");
      if (!tab) return;
      if (!["ArrowLeft", "ArrowRight", "Home", "End"].includes(event.key)) return;
      event.preventDefault();
      const group = tab.getAttribute("data-tab-group");
      const tabs = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(`[data-tab-group="${group}"]`));
      const currentIndex = tabs.indexOf(tab);
      if (currentIndex === -1) return;
      let nextIndex = currentIndex;
      if (event.key === "ArrowRight") {
        nextIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % tabs.length;
      } else if (event.key === "ArrowLeft") {
        nextIndex = (currentIndex - 1 + tabs.length) % tabs.length;
      } else if (event.key === "Home") {
        nextIndex = 0;
      } else if (event.key === "End") {
        nextIndex = tabs.length - 1;
      }
      tabs[nextIndex].focus();
      tabs[nextIndex].click();
    });

    document.getElementById("page-body").addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      const repoButton = event.target.closest("[data-open-repo]");
      if (repoButton) {
        openRepoView(
          repoButton.getAttribute("data-open-repo") || "",
          repoButton.getAttribute("data-open-repo-tab") || "overview",
        );
        return;
      }

      const clearWorkspaceScopeButton = event.target.closest("[data-clear-workspace-scope]");
      if (clearWorkspaceScopeButton) {
        setWorkspaceRepoScope("");
        return;
      }

      if (!event.target.closest("button, a, input, select, textarea, summary")) {
        const rowSelect = event.target.closest("[data-row-select-kind]");
        if (rowSelect) {
          const kind = rowSelect.getAttribute("data-row-select-kind");
          const value = rowSelect.getAttribute("data-row-select-id") || "";
          if (kind === "issue") {
            if (defaultString(selectedIssueQueueItem() && selectedIssueQueueItem().id, "") !== value) {
              clearDraftScope(issuesDetailDraftScope(selectedIssueQueueItem()));
            }
            state.issueQueue.selectedID = value;
            renderIssuesPage();
            return;
          }
          if (kind === "investigation") {
            loadInvestigationDetail(value);
            return;
          }
          if (kind === "finding") {
            if (defaultString(selectedTaskFinding() && selectedTaskFinding().id, "") !== value) {
              clearDraftScope(taskFindingDraftScope(selectedTaskScopeRepoSummary(), selectedTaskFinding()));
            }
            state.taskFindings.selectedFindingID = value;
            renderInvestigationsPage();
            return;
          }
          if (kind === "import-session") {
            if (defaultString(selectedFindingImportSession() && selectedFindingImportSession().id, "") !== value) {
              clearDraftScope(findingImportCandidateDraftScope(selectedTaskScopeRepoSummary(), selectedFindingImportSession(), selectedFindingImportCandidate()));
            }
            state.findingImports.selectedSessionID = value;
            state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID = "";
            const session = selectedFindingImportSession();
            if (session && session.candidates && session.candidates[0]) {
              state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID = session.candidates[0].candidate_id;
            }
            renderInvestigationsPage();
            return;
          }
          if (kind === "import-candidate") {
            if (defaultString(selectedFindingImportCandidate() && selectedFindingImportCandidate().candidate_id, "") !== value) {
              clearDraftScope(findingImportCandidateDraftScope(selectedTaskScopeRepoSummary(), selectedFindingImportSession(), selectedFindingImportCandidate()));
            }
            state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID = value;
            renderInvestigationsPage();
            return;
          }
          if (kind === "approval") {
            state.approvals.selectedID = value;
            renderApprovalsPage();
            return;
          }
          if (kind === "run") {
            openLogDrawer(value);
            return;
          }
          if (kind === "work-item") {
            openWorkItemDrawer(value);
            return;
          }
        }
      }

      const repoDropButton = event.target.closest("[data-repo-drop]");
      if (repoDropButton) {
        const repoSlug = repoDropButton.getAttribute("data-repo-drop");
        if (repoSlug) {
          dropRepo(repoSlug);
        }
        return;
      }

      const issueSelectButton = event.target.closest("[data-issue-select]");
      if (issueSelectButton) {
        const nextIssueID = issueSelectButton.getAttribute("data-issue-select") || "";
        if (defaultString(selectedIssueQueueItem() && selectedIssueQueueItem().id, "") !== nextIssueID) {
          clearDraftScope(issuesDetailDraftScope(selectedIssueQueueItem()));
        }
        state.issueQueue.selectedID = nextIssueID;
        renderIssuesPage();
        return;
      }

      const issueInvestigateButton = event.target.closest("[data-issue-investigate]");
      if (issueInvestigateButton) {
        const issueID = issueInvestigateButton.getAttribute("data-issue-investigate") || "";
        const selected = (state.issueQueue.items || []).find((item) => item.id === issueID);
        if (!selected) return;
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${selected.repo_slug}/issues/${selected.source_number}/investigate`, {
          method: "POST",
        }).then((payload) => {
          toast("success", "Investigation started", payload.launch.result || selected.title);
          loadInvestigations({ silent: true });
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Investigation failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const issueLaunchWorkButton = event.target.closest("[data-issue-launch-work]");
      if (issueLaunchWorkButton) {
        const issueID = issueLaunchWorkButton.getAttribute("data-issue-launch-work") || "";
        const selected = (state.issueQueue.items || []).find((item) => item.id === issueID);
        if (!selected) return;
        requestConfirmation({
          title: "Start work from issue?",
          message: `Launch implementation for ${selected.repo_slug} #${selected.source_number}.`,
          confirmLabel: "Start Work",
          onConfirm() {
            api(`/api/v1/repos/${selected.repo_slug}/issues/${selected.source_number}/launch-work`, {
              method: "POST",
            }).then((payload) => {
              toast("success", "Work started", payload.launch.result || selected.title);
              load();
              loadApprovals({ silent: true });
            }).catch((error) => {
              toast("danger", "Launch failed", error.message);
            });
          },
        });
        return;
      }

      const issueOpenRepoButton = event.target.closest("[data-issue-open-repo]");
      if (issueOpenRepoButton) {
        openRepoView(issueOpenRepoButton.getAttribute("data-issue-open-repo") || "", "overview");
        return;
      }

      const schedulerOpenButton = event.target.closest("[data-scheduler-open]");
      if (schedulerOpenButton) {
        const nextPlannedItemID = schedulerOpenButton.getAttribute("data-scheduler-open") || "";
        if (defaultString(selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary()) && selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary()).id, "") !== nextPlannedItemID) {
          clearDraftScope(repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(selectedRepoSummary(), selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary())));
        }
        state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID = nextPlannedItemID;
        renderRepoControlsPage(selectedRepoSummary());
        return;
      }

      const schedulerAddButton = event.target.closest("[data-scheduler-add]");
      if (schedulerAddButton) {
        const resultID = schedulerAddButton.getAttribute("data-scheduler-add") || "";
        const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
        const result = (state.repoScheduler.results || []).find((item) => item.id === resultID);
        if (!repo || !result) return;
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${repo.repo_slug}/tracked-issues/schedule`, {
          method: "POST",
          body: JSON.stringify({
            number: result.number,
            title: result.title,
            target_url: result.target_url,
            labels: result.labels || [],
            work_type: result.work_type || "",
            priority: result.priority,
          }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          clearDraftScope(repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(repo, selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(repo)));
          state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID = payload.planned_item.id;
          mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          toast("success", "Tracked issue scheduled", payload.planned_item.title);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Schedule failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const schedulerSaveButton = event.target.closest("[data-scheduler-save]");
      if (schedulerSaveButton) {
        const itemID = schedulerSaveButton.getAttribute("data-scheduler-save") || "";
        const draftScope = repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(selectedRepoSummary(), selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary()));
        const titleInput = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-detail-title");
        const priorityInput = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-detail-priority");
        const workTypeInput = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-detail-work-type");
        const scheduleInput = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-detail-schedule");
        const descriptionInput = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-detail-description");
        api(`/api/v1/planned-items/${encodeURIComponent(itemID)}`, {
          method: "PATCH",
          body: JSON.stringify({
            title: titleInput ? String(titleInput.value || "").trim() : "",
            description: descriptionInput ? String(descriptionInput.value || "") : "",
            work_type: workTypeInput ? String(workTypeInput.value || "").trim() : "",
            priority: priorityInput ? Number.parseInt(String(priorityInput.value || "3"), 10) : 3,
            schedule_at: fromDateTimeLocal(scheduleInput ? String(scheduleInput.value || "") : ""),
            clear_schedule: !(scheduleInput && String(scheduleInput.value || "").trim()),
          }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          clearDraftScope(draftScope);
          state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID = payload.planned_item.id;
          mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          toast("success", "Scheduled issue updated", payload.planned_item.title);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Save failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const schedulerDeleteButton = event.target.closest("[data-scheduler-delete]");
      if (schedulerDeleteButton) {
        const itemID = schedulerDeleteButton.getAttribute("data-scheduler-delete") || "";
        clearDraftScope(repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(selectedRepoSummary(), selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary())));
        api(`/api/v1/planned-items/${encodeURIComponent(itemID)}`, {
          method: "DELETE",
        }).then((payload) => {
          state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID = "";
          mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          toast("success", "Scheduled issue removed", payload.removed_item.title);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Remove failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const schedulerLaunchButton = event.target.closest("[data-scheduler-launch]");
      if (schedulerLaunchButton) {
        const itemID = schedulerLaunchButton.getAttribute("data-scheduler-launch") || "";
        clearDraftScope(repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(selectedRepoSummary(), selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary())));
        api(`/api/v1/planned-items/${encodeURIComponent(itemID)}/launch-now`, {
          method: "POST",
        }).then((payload) => {
          mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          toast("success", "Tracked issue launched", payload.launch.result || payload.planned_item.title);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Launch failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const issueSaveButton = event.target.closest("[data-issue-save]");
      if (issueSaveButton) {
        const issueID = issueSaveButton.getAttribute("data-issue-save") || "";
        const selected = (state.issueQueue.items || []).find((item) => item.id === issueID);
        if (!selected) return;
        const draftScope = issuesDetailDraftScope(selected);
        const priorityInput = document.getElementById("issue-detail-priority");
        const scheduleInput = document.getElementById("issue-detail-schedule");
        const deferredInput = document.getElementById("issue-detail-deferred");
        const priority = priorityInput ? Number.parseInt(String(priorityInput.value || selected.priority), 10) : selected.priority;
        const scheduleValue = scheduleInput ? String(scheduleInput.value || "") : "";
        const deferredReason = deferredInput ? String(deferredInput.value || "") : "";
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${selected.repo_slug}/issues/${selected.source_number}`, {
          method: "PATCH",
          body: JSON.stringify({
            priority,
            schedule_at: fromDateTimeLocal(scheduleValue),
            deferred_reason: deferredReason,
            clear_schedule: !scheduleValue,
          }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          clearDraftScope(draftScope);
          if (payload.state) {
            mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          }
          toast("success", "Issue updated", selected.title);
          loadIssueQueue({ silent: true });
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Issue update failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const issueClearScheduleButton = event.target.closest("[data-issue-clear-schedule]");
      if (issueClearScheduleButton) {
        const issueID = issueClearScheduleButton.getAttribute("data-issue-clear-schedule") || "";
        const selected = (state.issueQueue.items || []).find((item) => item.id === issueID);
        if (!selected) return;
        clearDraftScope(issuesDetailDraftScope(selected));
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${selected.repo_slug}/issues/${selected.source_number}`, {
          method: "PATCH",
          body: JSON.stringify({
            clear_schedule: true,
            deferred_reason: "",
          }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          if (payload.state) {
            mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          }
          toast("success", "Schedule cleared", selected.title);
          loadIssueQueue({ silent: true });
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Clear schedule failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const taskOpenButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-open]");
      if (taskOpenButton) {
        const taskID = taskOpenButton.getAttribute("data-task-open") || "";
        if (taskID) {
          openTaskDetailModal(taskID);
        }
        return;
      }

      const openTaskScheduleButton = event.target.closest("#open-task-schedule-button");
      if (openTaskScheduleButton) {
        openTaskScheduleModal();
        return;
      }

      const taskOpenJobButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-open-job]");
      if (taskOpenJobButton) {
        const runID = taskOpenJobButton.getAttribute("data-task-open-job") || "";
        if (runID) {
          openLogDrawer(runID);
        }
        return;
      }

      const taskActionButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-action]");
      if (taskActionButton) {
        const taskID = taskActionButton.getAttribute("data-task-id") || "";
        const action = taskActionButton.getAttribute("data-task-action") || "";
        if (!taskID || !action) return;
        api(`/api/v1/tasks/${encodeURIComponent(taskID)}/${encodeURIComponent(action)}`, {
          method: "POST",
        }).then(() => {
          load();
          loadApprovals({ silent: true });
          loadInvestigations({ silent: true });
          if (state.taskDetailModal && state.taskDetailModal.isOpen()) {
            state.taskDetailModal.close();
          }
          toast("success", "Task updated", taskID);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Task action failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const taskStatusFilterButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-status-filter]");
      if (taskStatusFilterButton) {
        const status = taskStatusFilterButton.getAttribute("data-task-status-filter") || "all";
        const current = filterState("investigations").status;
        updateFilter("investigations", "status", current === status ? "all" : status);
        renderInvestigationsPage();
        return;
      }

      const taskFilterClearButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-filter-clear]");
      if (taskFilterClearButton) {
        const field = taskFilterClearButton.getAttribute("data-task-filter-clear") || "";
        if (field === "all") {
          state.filters.investigations = defaultScopedViewFilter(state.selectedRepo);
        } else if (field === "query") {
          updateFilter("investigations", "query", "");
        } else if (field === "status") {
          updateFilter("investigations", "status", "all");
        } else if (field === "kind") {
          updateFilter("investigations", "kind", "all");
        } else if (field === "repo") {
          updateFilter("investigations", "repo", defaultString(state.selectedRepo, ""));
        }
        renderInvestigationsPage();
        return;
      }

      const investigationSelectButton = event.target.closest("[data-investigation-select]");
      if (investigationSelectButton) {
        const runID = investigationSelectButton.getAttribute("data-investigation-select") || "";
        if (runID) {
          loadInvestigationDetail(runID);
        }
        return;
      }

      if (event.target.id === "investigation-start-button") {
        const queryInput = document.getElementById("investigation-query");
        const repoSelect = document.getElementById("investigation-repo-select");
        const query = queryInput ? String(queryInput.value || "").trim() : "";
        const repoSlug = repoSelect ? String(repoSelect.value || "").trim() : "";
        state.investigations.draftQuery = query;
        if (!query) {
          toast("warning", "Missing query", "Enter an investigation query first.");
          return;
        }
        state.investigations.starting = true;
        renderInvestigationsPage();
        api("/api/v1/investigations", {
          method: "POST",
          body: JSON.stringify({ query, repo_slug: repoSlug }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          state.investigations.starting = false;
          toast("success", "Investigation started", payload.launch.result || query);
          loadInvestigations({ silent: true });
        }).catch((error) => {
          state.investigations.starting = false;
          renderInvestigationsPage();
          toast("danger", "Investigation failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      if (event.target.id === "task-save-template-button") {
        saveTaskTemplateFromComposer();
        return;
      }

      if (event.target.id === "task-schedule-button") {
        const repo = selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary();
        if (!repo) {
          toast("warning", "No repo selected", "Pick a repo before scheduling a task.");
          return;
        }
        const kind = state.taskComposer.kind;
        const scheduleAt = fromDateTimeLocal(state.taskComposer.scheduleAt);
        const findingsHandling = String(state.taskComposer.scoutDestination || "review").trim() === "local" ? "auto_promote" : "manual_review";
        let payload = null;
        if (kind === "investigation") {
          const query = String(state.taskComposer.investigationQuery || "").trim();
          if (!query) {
            toast("warning", "Missing query", "Enter the investigation query first.");
            return;
          }
          payload = {
            title: String(state.taskComposer.title || "").trim() || `Investigate: ${query.slice(0, 80)}`,
            description: String(state.taskComposer.description || "").trim(),
            schedule_at: scheduleAt,
            launch_kind: "investigation",
            findings_handling: findingsHandling,
            investigation_query: query,
          };
        } else if (kind === "coding") {
          const title = String(state.taskComposer.title || "").trim();
          if (!title) {
            toast("warning", "Missing title", "Name the coding task before scheduling it.");
            return;
          }
          payload = {
            title,
            description: String(state.taskComposer.description || "").trim(),
            work_type: String(state.taskComposer.codingWorkType || "feature").trim(),
            priority: Number.parseInt(String(state.taskComposer.codingPriority || "3"), 10),
            schedule_at: scheduleAt,
            launch_kind: "local_work",
            findings_handling: findingsHandling,
          };
        } else {
          const scoutComposerSelection = reconcileTaskComposerScoutRole(repo);
          const role = scoutComposerSelection.role;
          if (!role) {
            toast("warning", "Missing scout role", "Choose a scout role before scheduling the task.");
            return;
          }
          const focus = String(state.taskComposer.scoutFocus || "")
            .split(/[\n,]/)
            .map((value) => value.trim())
            .filter(Boolean);
          payload = {
            title: String(state.taskComposer.title || "").trim() || `Run ${scoutRoleLabel(role)}`,
            description: String(state.taskComposer.description || "").trim(),
            schedule_at: scheduleAt,
            launch_kind: "manual_scout",
            findings_handling: findingsHandling,
            scout_role: role,
            scout_destination: String(state.taskComposer.scoutDestination || "review").trim(),
            scout_focus: focus,
          };
          const sessionLimitInput = scoutComposerSelection.meta.supportsSessionLimit
            ? document.getElementById("task-scout-session-limit")
            : null;
          state.taskComposer.scoutSessionLimit = normalizeTaskComposerScoutSessionLimit(
            scoutComposerSelection.meta,
            sessionLimitInput ? String(sessionLimitInput.value || "") : state.taskComposer.scoutSessionLimit,
          );
          if (scoutComposerSelection.meta.supportsSessionLimit) {
            payload.scout_session_limit = Number.parseInt(String(state.taskComposer.scoutSessionLimit || "0"), 10) || 0;
          }
        }
        const idempotencyKey = defaultString(state.taskComposer.idempotencyKey, nextTaskComposerIdempotencyKey());
        state.taskComposer.idempotencyKey = idempotencyKey;
        state.taskComposer.creating = true;
        renderInvestigationsPage();
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${repo.repo_slug}/planned-items`, {
          method: "POST",
          headers: { "Idempotency-Key": idempotencyKey },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            ...payload,
            idempotency_key: idempotencyKey,
          }),
        }).then((response) => {
          state.taskComposer.creating = false;
          state.taskComposer.title = "";
          state.taskComposer.description = "";
          state.taskComposer.scheduleAt = "";
          resetTaskComposerIdempotencyKey();
          if (kind === "investigation") {
            state.taskComposer.investigationQuery = "";
          }
          if (kind === "manual_scout") {
            state.taskComposer.scoutFocus = "";
          }
          if (response.state) {
            mergeRepoState(response.state);
          } else {
            load();
          }
          loadApprovals({ silent: true });
          toast("success", "Task scheduled", response.planned_item && response.planned_item.title || payload.title);
        }).catch((error) => {
          state.taskComposer.creating = false;
          renderInvestigationsPage();
          toast("danger", "Task scheduling failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const taskPlannedLaunchButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-planned-launch]");
      if (taskPlannedLaunchButton) {
        const itemID = taskPlannedLaunchButton.getAttribute("data-task-planned-launch") || "";
        if (!itemID) return;
        api(`/api/v1/planned-items/${encodeURIComponent(itemID)}/launch-now`, {
          method: "POST",
        }).then((payload) => {
          if (payload.state) {
            mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          }
          loadApprovals({ silent: true });
          toast("success", "Task launched", payload.launch.result || defaultString(payload.planned_item && payload.planned_item.title, itemID));
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Launch failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const taskPlannedRemoveButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-planned-remove]");
      if (taskPlannedRemoveButton) {
        const itemID = taskPlannedRemoveButton.getAttribute("data-task-planned-remove") || "";
        if (!itemID) return;
        api(`/api/v1/planned-items/${encodeURIComponent(itemID)}`, {
          method: "DELETE",
        }).then((payload) => {
          if (payload.state) {
            mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          }
          loadApprovals({ silent: true });
          toast("success", "Task removed", defaultString(payload.removed_item && payload.removed_item.title, itemID));
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Remove failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      if (event.target.id === "task-findings-import-button") {
        const repo = selectedTaskScopeRepoSummary();
        const fileInput = document.getElementById("task-findings-import-file");
        const file = fileInput && fileInput.files && fileInput.files[0] ? fileInput.files[0] : null;
        if (!repo) {
          toast("warning", "No repo selected", "Pick a repo before importing findings.");
          return;
        }
        if (!file) {
          toast("warning", "Missing markdown file", "Choose a markdown file first.");
          return;
        }
        file.text().then((markdown) => {
          return createFindingImportSession(repo.repo_slug, file.name, markdown);
        }).then((payload) => {
          toast("success", "Import session created", payload.session && payload.session.id || file.name);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Import failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const taskFindingSaveButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-finding-save]");
      if (taskFindingSaveButton) {
        const repo = selectedTaskScopeRepoSummary();
        const findingID = taskFindingSaveButton.getAttribute("data-task-finding-save") || "";
        const finding = selectedTaskFinding();
        if (!repo || !findingID || !finding) return;
        saveTaskFinding(repo.repo_slug, findingID, {
          title: String(document.getElementById("task-finding-title") && document.getElementById("task-finding-title").value || "").trim(),
          summary: String(document.getElementById("task-finding-summary") && document.getElementById("task-finding-summary").value || "").trim(),
          detail: String(document.getElementById("task-finding-detail-input") && document.getElementById("task-finding-detail-input").value || "").trim(),
          evidence: String(document.getElementById("task-finding-evidence") && document.getElementById("task-finding-evidence").value || "").trim(),
          severity: String(document.getElementById("task-finding-severity") && document.getElementById("task-finding-severity").value || "medium").trim(),
          work_type: String(document.getElementById("task-finding-work-type") && document.getElementById("task-finding-work-type").value || "feature").trim(),
        }).then(() => {
          clearDraftScope(taskFindingDraftScope(repo, finding));
          toast("success", "Finding saved", finding.title || findingID);
        });
        return;
      }

      const taskFindingPromoteButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-finding-promote]");
      if (taskFindingPromoteButton) {
        const repo = selectedTaskScopeRepoSummary();
        const findingID = taskFindingPromoteButton.getAttribute("data-task-finding-promote") || "";
        const finding = selectedTaskFinding();
        if (!repo || !findingID || !finding) return;
        mutateTaskFinding(repo.repo_slug, findingID, "promote").then((payload) => {
          clearDraftScope(taskFindingDraftScope(repo, finding));
          loadApprovals({ silent: true });
          toast("success", "Finding promoted", payload.planned_item && payload.planned_item.id || findingID);
        });
        return;
      }

      const taskFindingDismissButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-finding-dismiss]");
      if (taskFindingDismissButton) {
        const repo = selectedTaskScopeRepoSummary();
        const findingID = taskFindingDismissButton.getAttribute("data-task-finding-dismiss") || "";
        const finding = selectedTaskFinding();
        if (!repo || !findingID || !finding) return;
        mutateTaskFinding(repo.repo_slug, findingID, "dismiss").then(() => {
          clearDraftScope(taskFindingDraftScope(repo, finding));
          toast("success", "Finding dismissed", findingID);
        });
        return;
      }

      const taskImportCandidateSaveButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-import-candidate-save]");
      if (taskImportCandidateSaveButton) {
        const repo = selectedTaskScopeRepoSummary();
        const session = selectedFindingImportSession();
        const candidateID = taskImportCandidateSaveButton.getAttribute("data-task-import-candidate-save") || "";
        const candidate = selectedFindingImportCandidate();
        if (!repo || !session || !candidateID || !candidate) return;
        mutateFindingImportCandidate(repo.repo_slug, session.id, candidateID, "PATCH", {
          title: String(document.getElementById("task-import-candidate-title") && document.getElementById("task-import-candidate-title").value || "").trim(),
          summary: String(document.getElementById("task-import-candidate-summary") && document.getElementById("task-import-candidate-summary").value || "").trim(),
          detail: String(document.getElementById("task-import-candidate-detail") && document.getElementById("task-import-candidate-detail").value || "").trim(),
          evidence: String(document.getElementById("task-import-candidate-evidence") && document.getElementById("task-import-candidate-evidence").value || "").trim(),
          severity: String(document.getElementById("task-import-candidate-severity") && document.getElementById("task-import-candidate-severity").value || "medium").trim(),
          work_type: String(document.getElementById("task-import-candidate-work-type") && document.getElementById("task-import-candidate-work-type").value || "feature").trim(),
        }).then(() => {
          clearDraftScope(findingImportCandidateDraftScope(repo, session, candidate));
          toast("success", "Candidate saved", candidateID);
        });
        return;
      }

      const taskImportCandidatePromoteButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-import-candidate-promote]");
      if (taskImportCandidatePromoteButton) {
        const repo = selectedTaskScopeRepoSummary();
        const session = selectedFindingImportSession();
        const candidateID = taskImportCandidatePromoteButton.getAttribute("data-task-import-candidate-promote") || "";
        const candidate = selectedFindingImportCandidate();
        if (!repo || !session || !candidateID || !candidate) return;
        mutateFindingImportCandidate(repo.repo_slug, session.id, candidateID, "POST", "promote").then(() => {
          clearDraftScope(findingImportCandidateDraftScope(repo, session, candidate));
          loadTaskFindings(repo.repo_slug, { silent: true });
          toast("success", "Candidate promoted", candidateID);
        });
        return;
      }

      const taskImportCandidateDropButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-import-candidate-drop]");
      if (taskImportCandidateDropButton) {
        const repo = selectedTaskScopeRepoSummary();
        const session = selectedFindingImportSession();
        const candidateID = taskImportCandidateDropButton.getAttribute("data-task-import-candidate-drop") || "";
        const candidate = selectedFindingImportCandidate();
        if (!repo || !session || !candidateID || !candidate) return;
        mutateFindingImportCandidate(repo.repo_slug, session.id, candidateID, "POST", "drop").then(() => {
          clearDraftScope(findingImportCandidateDraftScope(repo, session, candidate));
          toast("success", "Candidate dropped", candidateID);
        });
        return;
      }

      if (event.target.id === "feedback-sync-button") {
        api("/api/v1/feedback/sync", {
          method: "POST",
          body: JSON.stringify({}),
        }).then((payload) => {
          state.feedback.reviews = payload.reviews || [];
          state.feedback.replies = payload.replies || [];
          state.feedback.loaded = true;
          state.feedback.error = "";
          renderFeedbackPage();
          load();
          toast("success", "GitHub feedback synced", `Queued ${defaultString(payload.result && payload.result.queued, 0)} items.`);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Feedback sync failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const logButton = event.target.closest("[data-log-run-id]");
      if (logButton) {
        const runID = logButton.getAttribute("data-log-run-id");
        if (runID) {
          openLogDrawer(runID);
        }
        return;
      }

      const externalButton = event.target.closest("[data-open-external]");
      if (externalButton) {
        const targetURL = externalButton.getAttribute("data-open-external");
        if (targetURL) {
          window.open(targetURL, "_blank", "noopener");
        }
        return;
      }

      const runRerunButton = event.target.closest("[data-run-rerun]");
      if (runRerunButton) {
        const runID = runRerunButton.getAttribute("data-run-rerun");
        if (!runID) return;
        rerunWorkRunFromUI(runID);
        return;
      }

      const runSyncButton = event.target.closest("[data-run-sync]");
      if (runSyncButton) {
        const runID = runSyncButton.getAttribute("data-run-sync");
        if (!runID) return;
        api(`/api/v1/work/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runID)}/sync`, {
          method: "POST",
        }).then((payload) => {
          if (payload.detail && state.logSelection.runID === runID) {
            state.logSelection.detail = payload.detail;
            renderLogDrawer();
          }
          load();
          loadApprovals({ silent: true });
          toast("success", "Run synced", runID);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Run sync failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const runResolveButton = event.target.closest("[data-run-resolve]");
      if (runResolveButton) {
        const runID = runResolveButton.getAttribute("data-run-resolve");
        if (!runID) return;
        api(`/api/v1/work/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runID)}/resolve`, {
          method: "POST",
        }).then((payload) => {
          if (payload.detail && state.logSelection.runID === runID) {
            state.logSelection.detail = payload.detail;
            renderLogDrawer();
          }
          load();
          loadApprovals({ silent: true });
          toast("success", "Run resolved", runID);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Run resolve failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const runStopButton = event.target.closest("[data-run-stop]");
      if (runStopButton) {
        const runID = runStopButton.getAttribute("data-run-stop");
        if (!runID) return;
        api(`/api/v1/work/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runID)}/stop`, {
          method: "POST",
        }).then((payload) => {
          if (payload.detail && state.logSelection.runID === runID) {
            state.logSelection.detail = payload.detail;
            renderLogDrawer();
          }
          load();
          loadApprovals({ silent: true });
          toast("success", "Run stopped", runID);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Run stop failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const runDropButton = event.target.closest("[data-run-drop]");
      if (runDropButton) {
        const runID = runDropButton.getAttribute("data-run-drop");
        if (!runID) return;
        requestConfirmation({
          title: "Drop run?",
          message: `Remove run ${runID} from the active workspace queue.`,
          confirmLabel: "Drop Run",
          tone: "danger",
          onConfirm() {
            api(`/api/v1/work/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runID)}/drop`, {
              method: "POST",
            }).then(() => {
              if (state.logSelection.runID === runID && state.logDrawer) {
                state.logDrawer.close();
              }
              load();
              loadApprovals({ silent: true });
              toast("success", "Run dropped", runID);
            }).catch((error) => {
              toast("danger", "Run drop failed", error.message);
            });
          },
        });
        return;
      }

      const scoutSelectButton = event.target.closest("[data-scout-select]");
      if (scoutSelectButton) {
        state.scoutItems.selectedItemID = scoutSelectButton.getAttribute("data-scout-select") || "";
        rerenderScoutSurface();
        return;
      }

      const scoutActionButton = event.target.closest("[data-scout-action]");
      if (scoutActionButton) {
        const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
        const itemID = scoutActionButton.getAttribute("data-scout-id") || "";
        const action = scoutActionButton.getAttribute("data-scout-action") || "";
        if (repo && itemID && action) {
          if (action === "open-run") {
            const item = (state.scoutItems.items || []).find((entry) => entry.id === itemID);
            if (item && item.run_id) {
              openLogDrawer(item.run_id);
            }
            return;
          }
          mutateScoutItem(repo.repo_slug, itemID, action);
        }
        return;
      }

      const scoutSelectAllButton = event.target.closest("[data-scout-select-all]");
      if (scoutSelectAllButton) {
        selectAllScoutItems();
        rerenderScoutSurface();
        return;
      }

      const scoutClearButton = event.target.closest("[data-scout-clear-selection]");
      if (scoutClearButton) {
        clearScoutItemSelection();
        rerenderScoutSurface();
        return;
      }

      const scoutBulkActionButton = event.target.closest("[data-scout-bulk-action]");
      if (scoutBulkActionButton) {
        const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
        const action = scoutBulkActionButton.getAttribute("data-scout-bulk-action") || "";
        const itemIDs = scoutActionableSelection(action);
        if (repo && action && itemIDs.length) {
          mutateScoutItemsBulk(repo.repo_slug, itemIDs, action).then((payload) => {
            const failures = payload.failure_count || 0;
            const successes = payload.success_count || 0;
            if (failures) {
              toast("warning", "Bulk scout action completed", `${successes} updated, ${failures} failed.`);
            } else {
              toast("success", "Bulk scout action completed", `${successes} scout item${successes === 1 ? "" : "s"} updated.`);
            }
          });
        }
        return;
      }

      const workItemShow = event.target.closest("[data-work-item-show]");
      if (workItemShow) {
        const itemID = workItemShow.getAttribute("data-work-item-show");
        if (itemID) {
          openWorkItemDrawer(itemID);
        }
        return;
      }

      const approvalLaunchButton = event.target.closest("[data-approval-launch-planned]");
      if (approvalLaunchButton) {
        const plannedItemID = approvalLaunchButton.getAttribute("data-approval-launch-planned") || "";
        if (!plannedItemID) return;
        requestConfirmation({
          title: "Approve launch?",
          message: "This sends the planned item into execution immediately.",
          confirmLabel: "Approve Launch",
          onConfirm() {
            api(`/api/v1/planned-items/${plannedItemID}/launch-now`, {
              method: "POST",
            }).then((payload) => {
              if (payload.state) {
                mergeRepoState(payload.state);
              } else {
                load();
              }
              loadApprovals({ silent: true });
              toast("success", "Launch requested", payload.launch.result || "Planned item launched.");
            }).catch((error) => {
              toast("danger", "Launch failed", error.message);
            });
          },
        });
        return;
      }

      const approvalRetryScoutButton = event.target.closest("[data-approval-retry-scout]");
      if (approvalRetryScoutButton) {
        const scoutJobID = approvalRetryScoutButton.getAttribute("data-approval-retry-scout") || "";
        const selected = selectedApprovalItem();
        if (!selected || !selected.repo_slug || !scoutJobID) return;
        requestConfirmation({
          title: "Retry scout job?",
          message: "This requeues the failed scout-derived job for execution.",
          confirmLabel: "Retry Job",
          onConfirm() {
            mutateScoutItem(selected.repo_slug, scoutJobID, "retry").then(() => {
              loadApprovals({ silent: true });
              toast("success", "Scout job requeued", selected.subject || scoutJobID);
            }).catch((error) => {
              toast("danger", "Retry failed", error.message);
            });
          },
        });
        return;
      }

      const approvalSelectButton = event.target.closest("[data-approval-select]");
      if (approvalSelectButton) {
        state.approvals.selectedID = approvalSelectButton.getAttribute("data-approval-select") || "";
        renderApprovalsPage();
        return;
      }

      const approvalDropButton = event.target.closest("[data-approval-drop-kind]");
      if (approvalDropButton) {
        dropApprovalItem(
          approvalDropButton.getAttribute("data-approval-drop-kind") || "",
          approvalDropButton.getAttribute("data-approval-drop-id") || "",
          approvalDropButton.getAttribute("data-approval-drop-repo") || "",
          approvalDropButton.getAttribute("data-approval-drop-subject") || "",
        );
        return;
      }

      if (event.target.id === "launch-planned-button") {
        const select = document.getElementById("planned-select");
        const plannedItemID = select ? select.value : "";
        if (!plannedItemID) {
          toast("warning", "No planned item", "Select a queued planned item first.");
          return;
        }
        requestConfirmation({
          title: "Launch planned item now?",
          message: "This moves the selected planned item into execution immediately.",
          confirmLabel: "Launch Now",
          onConfirm() {
            api(`/api/v1/planned-items/${plannedItemID}/launch-now`, {
              method: "POST",
            }).then((payload) => {
              mergeRepoState(payload.state);
              toast("success", "Launch requested", payload.launch.result || "Planned item launched.");
            }).catch((error) => {
              toast("danger", "Launch failed", error.message);
            });
          },
        });
        return;
      }

      if (event.target.closest("[data-config-reset]")) {
        const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
        if (repo) {
          resetConfigDraft(repo);
        }
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("page-body").addEventListener("change", (event) => {
      captureDraftField(event.target);
      const scoutToggle = event.target.getAttribute("data-scout-toggle");
      if (scoutToggle) {
        toggleScoutItemSelection(scoutToggle, Boolean(event.target.checked));
        rerenderScoutSurface();
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-composer-repo") {
        const nextRepoSlug = String(event.target.value || "");
        clearDraftsForRouteTransition({
          view: "investigations",
          repoSlug: nextRepoSlug,
          repoTab: state.repoTab,
        });
        state.taskComposer.repoSlug = nextRepoSlug;
        state.scoutItems = defaultScoutItemsState();
        state.investigations.templatesLoaded = false;
        state.investigations.templatesRepoSlug = "";
        loadTaskTemplates({ silent: true });
        renderInvestigationsPage();
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-composer-template") {
        const templateID = String(event.target.value || "template:custom");
        const template = (state.investigations.templates || []).find((item) => item.id === templateID) || null;
        state.taskComposer.templateID = templateID;
        if (template) {
          applyTaskComposerTemplate(template);
        }
        renderInvestigationsPage();
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-composer-kind") {
        state.taskComposer.kind = String(event.target.value || "investigation");
        renderInvestigationsPage();
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-coding-work-type") {
        state.taskComposer.codingWorkType = String(event.target.value || "feature");
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-coding-priority") {
        state.taskComposer.codingPriority = String(event.target.value || "3");
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-scout-role") {
        reconcileTaskComposerScoutRole(selectedTaskComposerRepoSummary(), {
          role: String(event.target.value || "improvement-scout"),
          resetSessionLimit: true,
        });
        renderInvestigationsPage();
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-findings-handling") {
        state.taskComposer.scoutDestination = String(event.target.value || "review");
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-scout-session-limit") {
        state.taskComposer.scoutSessionLimit = String(event.target.value || "");
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "issue-select") {
        const nextIssue = String(event.target.value || "");
        if (state.selectedIssue !== nextIssue) {
          clearDraftScope(repoControlsIssueDraftScope());
        }
        state.selectedIssue = nextIssue;
        renderIssueForm(selectedIssueRecord());
        return;
      }
      const filterView = event.target.getAttribute("data-view-filter");
      const filterName = event.target.getAttribute("data-view-filter-name");
      if (filterView && filterName) {
        updateFilter(filterView, filterName, String(event.target.value || ""));
        if (filterView === "issues") {
          renderIssuesPage();
        } else if (filterView === "investigations") {
          renderInvestigationsPage();
        } else if (filterView === "work") {
          renderWorkPage();
        } else if (filterView === "feedback") {
          renderFeedbackPage();
        } else if (filterView === "approvals") {
          renderApprovalsPage();
        }
        return;
      }
      const field = event.target.getAttribute("data-config-field");
      if (field) {
        clearDraftField(event.target);
        updateConfigDraft(field, String(event.target.value || ""));
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("page-body").addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
      const selectable = event.target.closest("[data-row-select-kind]");
      if (!selectable) return;
      if (!["Enter", " "].includes(event.key)) return;
      event.preventDefault();
      selectable.click();
    });

    document.getElementById("page-body").addEventListener("submit", (event) => {
      if (event.target.id === "repo-config-form") {
        event.preventDefault();
        saveConfigDraft(selectedRepoSummary());
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "repo-scheduler-search-form") {
        event.preventDefault();
        const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
        const queryInput = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-search-query");
        const query = queryInput ? String(queryInput.value || "").trim() : "";
        if (!repo) return;
        state.repoScheduler.query = query;
        state.repoScheduler.searching = true;
        state.repoScheduler.error = "";
        renderRepoControlsPage(repo);
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${repo.repo_slug}/issue-search`, {
          method: "POST",
          body: JSON.stringify({ query }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          clearDraftScope(repoSchedulerSearchDraftScope(repo));
          state.repoScheduler.searching = false;
          state.repoScheduler.error = "";
          state.repoScheduler.query = payload.query || query;
          state.repoScheduler.effectiveQuery = payload.effective_query || "";
          state.repoScheduler.results = payload.items || [];
          reconcileRepoScheduler(selectedRepoSummary());
          renderRepoControlsPage(selectedRepoSummary());
        }).catch((error) => {
          state.repoScheduler.searching = false;
          state.repoScheduler.error = error.message;
          renderRepoControlsPage(selectedRepoSummary());
        });
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("page-body").addEventListener("input", (event) => {
      captureDraftField(event.target);
      if (event.target.id === "task-composer-title") {
        state.taskComposer.title = String(event.target.value || "");
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-composer-description") {
        state.taskComposer.description = String(event.target.value || "");
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-composer-schedule") {
        state.taskComposer.scheduleAt = String(event.target.value || "");
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-investigation-query") {
        state.taskComposer.investigationQuery = String(event.target.value || "");
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-scout-focus") {
        state.taskComposer.scoutFocus = String(event.target.value || "");
        return;
      }
      const configField = event.target.getAttribute("data-config-field");
      if (configField && typeof event.target.matches === "function" && event.target.matches("input[data-config-field], textarea[data-config-field]")) {
        updateConfigDraft(configField, String(event.target.value || ""));
        return;
      }
      const filterView = event.target.getAttribute("data-view-filter");
      const filterName = event.target.getAttribute("data-view-filter-name");
      if (!filterView || !filterName || filterName !== "query") {
        return;
      }
      updateFilter(filterView, filterName, String(event.target.value || ""));
      if (filterView === "issues") {
        renderIssuesPage();
      } else if (filterView === "investigations") {
        renderInvestigationsPage();
      } else if (filterView === "work") {
        renderWorkPage();
      } else if (filterView === "feedback") {
        renderFeedbackPage();
      } else if (filterView === "approvals") {
        renderApprovalsPage();
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("page-body").addEventListener("submit", (event) => {
      const form = event.target.closest("#usage-filters-form");
      if (!form) return;
      event.preventDefault();
      state.usage.filters = {
        since: defaultString(document.getElementById("usage-filter-since") && document.getElementById("usage-filter-since").value, "30d"),
        root: defaultString(document.getElementById("usage-filter-root") && document.getElementById("usage-filter-root").value, "all"),
        activity: String(document.getElementById("usage-filter-activity") && document.getElementById("usage-filter-activity").value || "").trim(),
        phase: String(document.getElementById("usage-filter-phase") && document.getElementById("usage-filter-phase").value || "").trim(),
        model: String(document.getElementById("usage-filter-model") && document.getElementById("usage-filter-model").value || "").trim(),
      };
      clearDraftScope(usageFiltersDraftScope());
      loadUsage();
    });

    document.getElementById("page-body").addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      const resetButton = event.target.closest("[data-view-filter-reset]");
      if (!resetButton) return;
      event.preventDefault();
      event.stopPropagation();
      const view = resetButton.getAttribute("data-view-filter-reset") || "";
      if (!view) return;
      resetFilter(view);
      if (view === "issues") {
        renderIssuesPage();
      } else if (view === "investigations") {
        renderInvestigationsPage();
      } else if (view === "work") {
        renderWorkPage();
      } else if (view === "feedback") {
        renderFeedbackPage();
      } else if (view === "approvals") {
        renderApprovalsPage();
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("page-body").addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      const resetButton = event.target.closest("[data-usage-reset]");
      if (!resetButton) return;
      event.preventDefault();
      clearDraftScope(usageFiltersDraftScope());
      state.usage = defaultUsageState();
      loadUsage();
    });

    document.getElementById("confirm-dialog-cancel").addEventListener("click", () => {
      closeConfirmationDialog();
    });

    document.getElementById("confirm-dialog-confirm").addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      event.preventDefault();
      const handler = state.confirmDialog.onConfirm;
      closeConfirmationDialog();
      if (typeof handler === "function") {
        handler();
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("confirm-dialog").addEventListener("cancel", (event) => {
      event.preventDefault();
      closeConfirmationDialog();
    });

    window.addEventListener("hashchange", () => {
      applyHashState();
      if (state.currentView === "repo") {
        refreshCurrentView({ silent: true }).catch(() => {});
      } else {
        ensureViewData(state.currentView);
      }
      renderApp();
    });

    document.addEventListener("visibilitychange", () => {
      if (document.visibilityState === "visible") {
        refreshUsageIfStale();
        return;
      }
      syncUsageAutoRefresh();
    });

    document.body.addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      if (event.target.closest("#page-body")) return;
      if (event.target.closest("[data-task-schedule-close]")) {
        if (state.taskScheduleModal) {
          state.taskScheduleModal.close();
        }
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-schedule-button") {
        submitTaskSchedule();
        return;
      }
      if (event.target.id === "task-save-template-button") {
        saveTaskTemplateFromComposer();
        return;
      }
      const taskOpenJobButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-open-job]");
      if (taskOpenJobButton) {
        const runID = taskOpenJobButton.getAttribute("data-task-open-job") || "";
        if (runID) {
          openLogDrawer(runID);
        }
        return;
      }
      const runRerunButton = event.target.closest("[data-run-rerun]");
      if (runRerunButton) {
        const runID = runRerunButton.getAttribute("data-run-rerun") || "";
        if (runID) {
          rerunWorkRunFromUI(runID);
        }
        return;
      }
      const runDropButton = event.target.closest("[data-run-drop]");
      if (runDropButton) {
        const runID = runDropButton.getAttribute("data-run-drop") || "";
        if (runID) {
          dropWorkRunFromUI(runID);
        }
        return;
      }
      const taskActionButton = event.target.closest("[data-task-action]");
      if (taskActionButton) {
        const taskID = taskActionButton.getAttribute("data-task-id") || "";
        const action = taskActionButton.getAttribute("data-task-action") || "";
        if (!taskID || !action) return;
        api(`/api/v1/tasks/${encodeURIComponent(taskID)}/${encodeURIComponent(action)}`, {
          method: "POST",
        }).then(() => {
          load();
          loadApprovals({ silent: true });
          loadInvestigations({ silent: true });
          if (state.taskDetailModal && state.taskDetailModal.isOpen()) {
            state.taskDetailModal.close();
          }
          toast("success", "Task updated", taskID);
        }).catch((error) => {
